# Módulo: auth

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/auth/. Covers the AuthNotifier state machine (signIn/signUp/Google/Apple/cancelOnboarding/passwordReset), AuthService data flows (Firebase mapping, profile getOrCreate rollback, createIfAbsent backfill, reauth helpers, signOut Google disconnect), pure validators + password-strength bar, all 5 screens (welcome/login/register/forgot/splash) with loading/empty/error/success states, the terms-gate on social sign-up, the in-app legal viewer, the trainer inquiry card, and the pure authRedirect gating function including athlete-vs-trainer role behavior and the account-deletion in-flight gate. Existing coverage is strong on validators, AuthFailure mapping, AuthService core flows, and basic screen happy paths; this catalog fills the gaps (Apple cancel-restore, password-reset security invariant exposed at screen level, terms gate, splash routing edge, strength-bar boundaries, role-gating combinations) and restates a few P0 regression anchors. automatable=false only for cases needing the native Google/Apple sheet, real Firebase auth, or device email delivery._

### auth-01 — validateEmail accepts canonical and rejects malformed/empty/null
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — pure static validator EmailPasswordValidator.validateEmail.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call validateEmail('a@b.c') and validateEmail('martin@treino.app').
  2. Call validateEmail('') , validateEmail(null), validateEmail('nobody'), validateEmail('@b.c'), validateEmail('a@b'), validateEmail('a b@c.com').
- **Esperado:** Valid inputs return null. Every invalid/empty/null input returns 'El email no es válido'. Strings with whitespace inside (regex [^\s@]+) are rejected.

### auth-02 — validatePassword enforces >=8 chars + >=1 letter + >=1 digit (boundaries)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — pure static validator EmailPasswordValidator.validatePassword.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call with 'abc12345' (8 chars, letter+digit) and 'Pass1234'.
  2. Call with '' , null, 'abc1234' (7 chars), 'abcdefgh' (no digit), '12345678' (no letter), 'abcdefg1' (exactly 8 boundary).
- **Esperado:** Valid passwords return null. All failures return the single combined message 'La contraseña debe tener al menos 8 caracteres, una letra y un número'. 7-char input fails; exactly-8 with letter+digit passes (boundary).

### auth-03 — validatePasswordMatch returns null only on exact equality
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — pure static validator.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call validatePasswordMatch('Pass1234','Pass1234').
  2. Call with ('Pass1234','pass1234'), (null,'x'), ('x',null), (null,null).
- **Esperado:** Equal pair (including null==null) returns null; any difference returns 'Las contraseñas no coinciden'. Note (null,null) returns null — confirm intended.

### auth-04 — PasswordStrengthBar maps strength 0..3 to lit segments and hint
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PasswordStrengthBar pumped inside MaterialApp + AppPalette scope.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump with password 'abc' (len<8) → expect 0 lit segments, no hint text.
  2. Pump 'abcdefgh' (8+, letters only) → 1 lit segment, 'Débil...' hint.
  3. Pump 'abcd1234' (letter+digit) → 2 lit segments, 'Buena...' hint.
  4. Pump 'abcd123!' (letter+digit+symbol) → 3 lit segments, 'Fuerte.' hint in accent color.
- **Esperado:** Lit segment count equals computed strength; hint text and color match the switch. Boundary at exactly 8 chars promotes from 0 to >=1.

### auth-05 — AuthNotifier.signIn: AsyncLoading then AsyncData(user) on success
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer overriding authServiceProvider with a mock whose signInWithEmail returns a fake User; authStateChanges seeded null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read authNotifierProvider.notifier.
  2. Call signIn(email:'a@b.c', password:'Pass1234').
  3. Capture state transitions.
- **Esperado:** State goes const AsyncLoading() then AsyncData(user). service.signInWithEmail called once with trimmed email + raw password.

### auth-06 — AuthNotifier.signIn: maps thrown AuthFailure to AsyncError
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock authService.signInWithEmail throws AuthFailure.wrongPassword().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signIn with any credentials.
  2. Inspect resulting state.
- **Esperado:** State ends AsyncError holding AuthFailure.wrongPassword() (via AsyncValue.guard); previous user value not retained as data.

### auth-07 — AuthNotifier.signInWithGoogle: cancel restores previous user, no error banner
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** State seeded AsyncData(previousUser); mock signInWithGoogle throws AuthFailure.signInCancelled().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set/seed state to AsyncData(previousUser).
  2. Call signInWithGoogle().
  3. Inspect final state.
- **Esperado:** After AsyncLoading, state is silently restored to AsyncData(previousUser) — NOT AsyncError. This is the cancel-restore invariant that prevents a flashing banner on intentional dismissal.

### auth-08 — AuthNotifier.signInWithGoogle: non-cancel failure surfaces AsyncError
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock signInWithGoogle throws AuthFailure.unknown('network_error') (anything != signInCancelled).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed state AsyncData(previousUser).
  2. Call signInWithGoogle().
  3. Inspect state.
- **Esperado:** State ends AsyncError with the failure (no restore). Only signInCancelled triggers restore.

### auth-09 — AuthNotifier.signInWithApple: cancel-restore mirrors Google
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** State seeded AsyncData(previousUser); mock signInWithApple throws AuthFailure.signInCancelled().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed state AsyncData(previousUser).
  2. Call signInWithApple().
  3. Inspect state.
  4. Repeat with a non-cancel AuthFailure.
- **Esperado:** signInCancelled → silent restore to previousUser; non-cancel failure → AsyncError. Confirms Apple path has identical cancel semantics as Google (regression guard if one path is edited).

### auth-10 — AuthNotifier.signUp: loading then AsyncData(user); no displayName passed
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock authService.signUpWithEmail returns fake User and records args.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signUp(email:'new@b.c', password:'Pass1234').
  2. Inspect state and captured service args.
- **Esperado:** State AsyncLoading then AsyncData(user). service.signUpWithEmail invoked with email+password only — no displayName argument exists (ProfileSetup owns displayName per REQ-AUTH-002).

### auth-11 — AuthNotifier.sendPasswordResetEmail: preserves user value and rethrows on error
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** State seeded AsyncData(currentUser); mock sendPasswordResetEmail (a) completes, (b) throws AuthFailure.networkError().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed AsyncData(currentUser).
  2. Call sendPasswordResetEmail(email:'a@b.c') for success path; assert state.valueOrNull still == currentUser after.
  3. Call again with the throwing mock; assert it rethrows.
- **Esperado:** State value is restored to currentUser regardless (reset does not change auth state). On error the notifier rethrows the AuthFailure so the screen can mask userNotFound. State is NOT left as AsyncError.

### auth-12 — AuthNotifier.cancelOnboarding: success → AsyncData(null); failure → restore + rethrow
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** State seeded AsyncData(onboardingUser); mock cancelOnboarding (a) completes, (b) throws AuthFailure.requiresRecentLogin().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed AsyncData(onboardingUser).
  2. Call cancelOnboarding() success path → expect final AsyncData(null).
  3. Reseed, call with throwing mock → expect state restored to previous AsyncData(onboardingUser) AND the AuthFailure rethrown.
- **Esperado:** Happy path ends signed-out (AsyncData(null)). Failure restores the previous state so the user is not lost mid-onboarding and rethrows so the screen can show a SnackBar.

### auth-13 — AuthNotifier.build seeds from stream and follow-up emissions update state
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authStateChangesProvider overridden with a controllable Stream<User?>.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Emit null as first value → read notifier state.
  2. Later emit a User on the stream.
  3. Verify state without re-running build().
- **Esperado:** Initial state is AsyncData(null) from first emission. Subsequent stream emission flips state to AsyncData(user) via the imperative ref.listen — confirming in-flight imperative actions are not clobbered by a build() rerun.

### auth-14 — Race: stream emission during in-flight signIn does not clobber the action result
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Controllable auth stream + mock signInWithEmail with a completer to hold the future.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Begin signIn() (state → AsyncLoading).
  2. While pending, push an unrelated emission on authStateChanges.
  3. Complete the signIn future.
  4. Inspect final state.
- **Esperado:** Final state reflects the signIn result (AsyncData(user) or AsyncError), not the intervening stream emission — the imperative listener design must not overwrite an in-flight action. (Extends existing race-condition group.)

### auth-15 — AuthService.signUpWithEmail: creates user, sends verification, creates profile doc with displayName null
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock FirebaseAuth.createUserWithEmailAndPassword returns UserCredential(user); mock UserRepository.getOrCreate succeeds.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signUpWithEmail(email,password).
  2. Verify user.sendEmailVerification called.
  3. Verify userRepository.getOrCreate called with uid+email (no displayName).
- **Esperado:** Returns the created User. Verification email requested. Firestore profile created via getOrCreate. updateDisplayName is never called.

### auth-16 — AuthService.signUpWithEmail: Firestore failure rolls back the orphan Auth user and throws profileCreateFailed
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** createUser succeeds; getOrCreate throws; user.delete mockable.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signUpWithEmail.
  2. Capture exception and verify user.delete invoked.
- **Esperado:** Throws AuthFailure.profileCreateFailed(cause: <firestoreError>). Best-effort user.delete() called to avoid an orphan Auth account (REQ-PROF-034/035). If user.delete also throws, profileCreateFailed is still thrown.

### auth-17 — AuthService.signUpWithEmail: maps email-already-in-use and weak-password to AuthFailure
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** createUser throws FirebaseAuthException with code 'email-already-in-use', then 'weak-password'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signUpWithEmail for each code.
  2. Inspect thrown failure.
- **Esperado:** Maps to AuthFailure.emailAlreadyInUse() and AuthFailure.weakPassword() respectively via AuthFailure.fromFirebase.

### auth-18 — AuthService.signInWithEmail: returns user and backfills profile via createIfAbsent (best-effort)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** signInWithEmailAndPassword returns UserCredential(user); UserRepository.createIfAbsent (a) succeeds, (b) throws.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signInWithEmail success → verify createIfAbsent called once with uid+email.
  2. Make createIfAbsent throw → call again → verify sign-in still returns the user.
- **Esperado:** Returns User on success. createIfAbsent is opportunistic backfill and its failure is swallowed — never blocks sign-in (REQ-PROF-037).

### auth-19 — AuthService.signInWithEmail: maps wrong-password and invalid-credential both to wrongPassword
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** signInWithEmailAndPassword throws FirebaseAuthException 'wrong-password' then 'invalid-credential'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signInWithEmail for each code.
  2. Inspect thrown failure.
- **Esperado:** Both codes collapse to AuthFailure.wrongPassword() (intentional collapse so the UI does not leak which field was wrong).

### auth-20 — AuthService.sendPasswordResetEmail: maps user-not-found to userNotFound (screen masks it)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FirebaseAuth.sendPasswordResetEmail (a) completes, (b) throws 'user-not-found'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call success path → completes without error.
  2. Call throwing path → inspect failure.
- **Esperado:** Success completes silently. user-not-found maps to AuthFailure.userNotFound() — the service surfaces it; masking happens at the screen layer (see auth-30).

### auth-21 — AuthService.signInWithGoogle: cancel at authenticate() and at authorizeScopes both throw signInCancelled
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock GoogleSignIn.authenticate / authorizationClient.authorizeScopes can throw GoogleSignInException(canceled).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Make authenticate() throw canceled → assert AuthFailure.signInCancelled().
  2. Make authenticate succeed but authorizeScopes throw canceled → assert AuthFailure.signInCancelled().
  3. Make authenticate throw a non-cancel GoogleSignInException → assert AuthFailure.unknown(code.name).
  4. Make a PlatformException be thrown → assert AuthFailure.unknown(e.code).
- **Esperado:** User cancel at either stage maps to signInCancelled; other Google/platform errors map to AuthFailure.unknown with the underlying code preserved.

### auth-22 — AuthService.signInWithApple: builds OAuth credential with raw nonce to Firebase, hashed to Apple; cancel maps to signInCancelled
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Inject mock AppleSignInGateway returning a fake AuthorizationCredentialAppleID; mock FirebaseAuth.signInWithCredential.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signInWithApple happy path → capture nonce passed to gateway vs rawNonce in OAuthProvider credential.
  2. Make gateway throw SignInWithAppleAuthorizationException(canceled) → assert signInCancelled.
  3. Make gateway throw a generic error → assert AuthFailure.unknown('apple-unknown').
- **Esperado:** Gateway receives the sha256-hashed nonce; OAuthProvider credential receives the RAW nonce (direction invariant). Cancel → signInCancelled; other failures → unknown('apple-unknown'). createIfAbsent backfill swallows errors.

### auth-23 — nonce_helpers: generateNonce length/charset + sha256OfString determinism
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — pure functions in nonce_helpers.dart.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call generateNonce() default → assert length 32 and every char in the allowed charset.
  2. Call generateNonce(16) → assert length 16.
  3. Call sha256OfString('abc') twice → assert equal 64-char lowercase hex; assert it equals the known SHA-256 of 'abc'.
- **Esperado:** generateNonce honors length and charset (uses Random.secure per REQ-NONCE-001). sha256OfString is deterministic lowercase hex.

### auth-24 — AuthService.signOut: disconnects Google session then signs out Firebase
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock GoogleSignIn.signOut and FirebaseAuth.signOut.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call signOut().
  2. Verify both googleSignIn.signOut and firebaseAuth.signOut were invoked.
- **Esperado:** Google signOut is called (so the next picker shows fresh) and Firebase signOut is called. Order: Google before Firebase.

### auth-25 — AuthService.cancelOnboarding: stale-auth Firebase codes trigger local signOut instead of throwing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUser present; userRepository.delete may throw (swallowed); user.delete throws FirebaseAuthException with 'user-not-found' / 'user-token-expired' / 'invalid-user-token'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Make user.delete throw each stale code in turn.
  2. Verify _auth.signOut() is called and NO AuthFailure is thrown.
  3. Then make user.delete throw 'requires-recent-login' and verify AuthFailure is thrown.
- **Esperado:** Stale-auth codes are an escape hatch: the client force-signs-out and does NOT throw. Non-stale Firebase delete errors (e.g. requires-recent-login) are mapped and rethrown. Firestore delete failure is always swallowed.

### auth-26 — AuthService reauth helpers: reauthenticate maps wrong/invalid credential to reAuthFailed; short-circuits Apple sentinel
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock currentUser with reauthenticateWithCredential; build an EmailAuthProvider credential.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call reauthenticate with a normal credential where reauthenticateWithCredential throws 'wrong-password' → assert AuthFailure.reAuthFailed().
  2. Call with no currentUser → assert AuthFailure.userNotFound().
  3. Call reauthenticate with a credential whose providerId is the Apple sentinel → assert it returns without calling reauthenticateWithCredential.
- **Esperado:** wrong-password/invalid-credential → reAuthFailed; no user → userNotFound; sentinel providerId short-circuits (Apple re-auth already done server-side).

### auth-27 — AuthService.getPasswordCredential: throws reAuthFailed when no user or no email
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock FirebaseAuth.currentUser.
- **Pasos:**
  1. currentUser == null → call getPasswordCredential(password:'x') → expect throw.
  2. currentUser present but email == null → call → expect throw.
  3. currentUser with email present → call → expect EmailAuthProvider credential built from that email + password.
- **Esperado:** Both null-user and null-email cases throw AuthFailure.reAuthFailed(provider:'password'). Valid case returns an EmailAuthProvider credential.

### auth-28 — AuthFailure.fromFirebase maps all known codes and falls through to unknown(code)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — construct FirebaseAuthException with each code.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Map each: invalid-email, user-disabled, user-not-found, wrong-password, invalid-credential, email-already-in-use, weak-password, too-many-requests, network-request-failed, account-exists-with-different-credential, requires-recent-login.
  2. Map an unrecognized code e.g. 'bananas'.
- **Esperado:** Each known code maps to its dedicated variant (invalid-credential collapses to wrongPassword; requires-recent-login → requiresRecentLogin). Unknown code → AuthFailure.unknown('bananas') preserving the raw code.

### auth-29 — AuthFailure.userMessage returns a non-empty es-AR string for every variant
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — exhaustive over the sealed AuthFailure variants including profileCreateFailed, requiresRecentLogin, reAuthFailed, deletionFailed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. For each variant construct it and read .userMessage.
  2. Assert non-empty and Spanish (voseo) copy.
- **Esperado:** Every sealed variant yields a non-empty hardcoded es-AR message (ADR-I18N-002 intentional exclusion — domain layer has no BuildContext). Catches a missing arm when a new variant is added.

### auth-30 — ForgotPassword screen: success state renders, field becomes read-only, banner hidden
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump ForgotPasswordScreen with authNotifierProvider overridden so sendPasswordResetEmail completes successfully.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter a valid email.
  2. Tap the CTA (or submit).
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** Success copy (authForgotSuccess) appears; the email AuthInput is rendered disabled (enabled:false); 'volver a login' link is shown; no AuthFailureBanner. CTA spinner cleared.

### auth-31 — ForgotPassword screen SECURITY: userNotFound is masked as success (no account-enumeration)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override so sendPasswordResetEmail throws AuthFailure.userNotFound().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter an email for a non-existent account.
  2. Submit and pump.
- **Esperado:** Screen shows the SAME success state as a real send — NO error banner, _sent==true (REQ-AUTH-011). This is the anti-enumeration invariant; a regression here leaks which emails are registered.

### auth-32 — ForgotPassword screen: non-userNotFound failure shows AuthFailureBanner and clears spinner
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** sendPasswordResetEmail throws AuthFailure.networkError().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter a valid email, submit, pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** AuthFailureBanner with the network error copy is shown; form remains editable; _sent stays false; spinner cleared.

### auth-33 — ForgotPassword screen: CTA disabled while email empty; spinner during in-flight
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** sendPasswordResetEmail backed by a pending completer.
- **Pasos:**
  1. With empty email field, observe CTA onPressed is null (disabled).
  2. Type a valid email → CTA enabled.
  3. Submit → while pending, assert isLoading spinner shown; complete the future → spinner cleared.
- **Esperado:** CTA is disabled when the trimmed email is empty and enabled otherwise; loading spinner is shown only while the request is in flight.

### auth-34 — Login screen: CTA disabled until both email and password non-empty
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump LoginScreen with default overrides (no auth action triggered).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Initially both fields empty → assert CTA disabled.
  2. Type only email → still disabled.
  3. Type only password → still disabled.
  4. Type both → CTA enabled.
- **Esperado:** _fieldsEmpty drives the CTA; it enables only when trimmed email AND password are both non-empty. (Email is trimmed; password is not.)

### auth-35 — Login screen: happy path submit navigates to /home
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override where signIn resolves to AsyncData(fakeUser); a test GoRouter/Navigator observer capturing /home.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter valid email+password.
  2. Tap CTA.
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** After signIn resolves with a non-null user, context.go('/home') fires. Navigation to /home observed.

### auth-36 — Login screen: wrong-password and user-not-found show the correct es-AR banner
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override yielding AsyncError(AuthFailure.wrongPassword()) then AuthFailure.userNotFound().
- **Pasos:**
  1. Submit with each error state in turn.
  2. Pump and read the banner text.
- **Esperado:** AuthFailureBanner shows 'La contraseña es incorrecta' for wrongPassword and 'No encontramos una cuenta con ese email' for userNotFound. No navigation occurs.

### auth-37 — Login screen: spinner during AsyncLoading and social buttons disabled
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override held in AsyncLoading.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump LoginScreen with state AsyncLoading.
  2. Inspect CTA and the Google/Apple AuthSecondaryButtons.
- **Esperado:** CTA shows its loading spinner; Google and Apple buttons have onPressed==null (disabled) while isLoading, preventing concurrent auth attempts.

### auth-38 — Login screen: navigation links to /register and /forgot-password
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LoginScreen pumped inside a test router with /register and /forgot-password routes.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the 'Crear cuenta'/register link → assert push to /register.
  2. Back, tap 'Olvidé mi contraseña' → assert push to /forgot-password.
- **Esperado:** Register link pushes /register; forgot link pushes /forgot-password.

### auth-39 — Login screen: Google sign-in cancel does not navigate or show a banner
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override where signInWithGoogle leaves state restored to the previous (null) user (cancel-restore).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the Google button.
  2. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** No navigation to /home (user still null) and no AuthFailureBanner — the cancel path is silent at the screen too.

### auth-40 — Register screen: CTA disabled until fields filled AND terms accepted
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump RegisterScreen with default overrides.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Fill email, password, confirm with valid values but leave terms unchecked → assert CTA disabled.
  2. Check the terms box → assert CTA enabled.
  3. Uncheck → disabled again.
  4. Clear confirm field → disabled.
- **Esperado:** _canSubmit = !_fieldsEmpty && _termsAccepted. CTA enables only with all three fields non-empty and the terms checkbox checked.

### auth-41 — Register screen: inline validation for invalid email, short password, mismatch
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump RegisterScreen; terms checked so submit runs form validation.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter 'bademail', a valid password twice → submit → expect email error.
  2. Enter valid email, password 'abc1' → submit → expect password error.
  3. Enter valid email+password but confirm differing → submit → expect 'Las contraseñas no coinciden'.
- **Esperado:** Form validators surface the matching es-AR messages and block signUp from being called (no navigation).

### auth-42 — Register screen: email-already-in-use shows error banner, no navigation
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override yielding AsyncError(AuthFailure.emailAlreadyInUse()).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Fill valid fields, check terms, submit.
  2. Pump.
- **Esperado:** AuthFailureBanner shows 'Ya existe una cuenta con ese email'. Stays on register; no /home navigation.

### auth-43 — Register screen TERMS GATE: tapping Google/Apple without terms shows SnackBar and does NOT start auth
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump RegisterScreen with terms unchecked; spy on authNotifier.signInWithGoogle/Apple.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Leave terms unchecked.
  2. Tap the Google button → pump.
  3. Tap the Apple button → pump.
- **Esperado:** A SnackBar 'Aceptá los Términos y la Política de Privacidad para continuar' appears for each, and signInWithGoogle/signInWithApple are NEVER called. Social buttons stay visually enabled (explicit feedback, not a disabled control).

### auth-44 — Register screen: with terms checked, Google sign-in proceeds and navigates on success
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Terms checked; signInWithGoogle resolves to AsyncData(fakeUser); test router with /home.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Check terms.
  2. Tap Google.
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** No SnackBar; signInWithGoogle called once; on non-null user, navigation to /home occurs.

### auth-45 — Register screen: PasswordStrengthBar updates live as the password field changes
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump RegisterScreen.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Type 'abc' in password → expect 0 lit segments / no hint.
  2. Append to make 'abcd1234' → expect 2 lit segments + 'Buena' hint.
  3. Append '!' → 3 lit segments + 'Fuerte'.
- **Esperado:** The ValueListenableBuilder rebuilds PasswordStrengthBar on each keystroke; segment count tracks the live password.

### auth-46 — TermsCheckbox: tapping Términos / Política links opens the in-app LegalDocumentScreen (no SnackBar)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump TermsCheckbox inside a MaterialApp with a Navigator.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the 'Términos' link span.
  2. Assert LegalDocumentScreen with title 'Términos y Condiciones' is pushed.
  3. Pop, tap 'Política de Privacidad' → assert LegalDocumentScreen 'Política de Privacidad' pushed.
  4. Toggle the checkbox → assert onChanged(true/false) fired.
- **Esperado:** Each link pushes the matching LegalDocumentScreen via Navigator.push (works during register regardless of auth state, not intercepted by authRedirect). Checkbox toggling fires onChanged with the new bool.

### auth-47 — LegalDocumentScreen: renders title, all sections, footer, and back affordance
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump LegalDocumentScreen(title:'Términos y Condiciones', sections: kTermsSections).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the screen.
  2. Verify the title and each section heading+body render.
  3. Verify the footer line with kLegalLastUpdated and kLegalContactEmail.
  4. Tap the back IconButton.
- **Esperado:** Title, every section, and the footer (last-updated + contact email) render; itemCount == sections.length + 1. Back button calls maybePop.

### auth-48 — TrainerInquiryCard: tapping opens AlertDialog with team email; Cerrar closes it
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump TrainerInquiryCard inside MaterialApp + AppPalette scope.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Verify shield icon, title, subtitle render.
  2. Tap the card → assert AlertDialog appears with the inquiry body (team email).
  3. Tap the close/Cerrar action → assert dialog dismissed.
- **Esperado:** Card renders its three text/icon elements; tap shows the trainer-inquiry AlertDialog (manual-trainer-creation flow); close action pops it. This is the only trainer-acquisition affordance in the unauthenticated UI.

### auth-49 — Welcome screen: EMPEZAR pushes /register, 'Iniciar sesión' pushes /login
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump WelcomeScreen in a test router with /register and /login.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the primary CTA → assert push to /register.
  2. Tap the 'Iniciar sesión' link → assert push to /login.
- **Esperado:** CTA navigates to /register; sign-in link navigates to /login.

### auth-50 — Welcome screen: account-deleted flag shows 'Tu cuenta fue eliminada' SnackBar exactly once
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump WelcomeScreen with accountDeletedFlagProvider initially false; then set it true.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump Welcome with flag false → assert no SnackBar.
  2. Set accountDeletedFlagProvider to true → pump and settle.
  3. Pump again (rebuild) → assert SnackBar does not reappear.
- **Esperado:** When the flag flips true the listener shows the deletion SnackBar and immediately resets the flag to false, so it shows once only. No duplicate on rebuild.

### auth-51 — Welcome screen: social buttons disabled while auth isLoading
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider override held in AsyncLoading.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump WelcomeScreen.
  2. Inspect Google and Apple AuthSecondaryButtons.
- **Esperado:** Both have onPressed==null while isLoading (prevents double-triggering OAuth from the welcome screen).

### auth-52 — Welcome screen: renders without overflow at small/large viewports and text scales
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump WelcomeScreen at multiple surface sizes.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump at a short viewport (e.g. 320x568) and a tall one.
  2. Pump with MediaQuery textScaleFactor increased.
  3. Assert no RenderFlex overflow / layout exceptions.
- **Esperado:** SliverFillRemaining(hasScrollBody:false) lets content fill yet scroll; eyebrow ellipsis and Wrap prevent overflow. No layout errors at small sizes or large text scaling (F2 regression guard).

### auth-53 — Splash screen: anonymous user routes to /welcome, authenticated routes to /home
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider.future resolves to null (anon) then to a User; test router capturing navigation.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump SplashScreen with auth resolving to null → pump and settle → assert go('/welcome').
  2. Repeat with auth resolving to a User → assert go('/home').
- **Esperado:** _navigate awaits auth resolution then routes: null → /welcome, non-null → /home. No artificial delay. This manual handoff is load-bearing (authRedirect does not move users off /splash).

### auth-54 — Splash screen: renders logo + brand headline on first frame before auth resolves
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump SplashScreen with auth future pending.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump one frame (do not settle).
  2. Assert TreinoLogo and the 'MOVÉS EL HIERRO. NOSOTROS EL RESTO.' headline render.
- **Esperado:** Branding shows immediately while auth resolves; no blank screen.

### auth-55 — authRedirect: anonymous on protected route → /welcome; on public route → stay
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with authNotifierProvider = AsyncData(null).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call authRedirect(read,'/home') and '/workout' → expect '/welcome'.
  2. Call with '/login','/register','/welcome','/forgot-password' → expect null.
  3. Call with '/splash' → expect null.
- **Esperado:** Anonymous users are bounced from any protected route to /welcome but left alone on every public route (including /splash and /forgot-password so a reset is not interrupted).

### auth-56 — authRedirect: AsyncLoading or no-value auth never redirects
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider in const AsyncLoading() (no value).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call authRedirect(read,'/home'), '/login', '/workout'.
- **Esperado:** All return null — REQ-AUTH-024: do not redirect while auth is resolving (prevents flicker). Guard also covers !hasValue.

### auth-57 — authRedirect: authenticated with incomplete profile (displayName null / no doc) → /profile-setup
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authNotifierProvider = AsyncData(user); userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile with displayName==null), and separately AsyncData(null) (no doc).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call authRedirect(read,'/home') with displayName null → expect '/profile-setup'.
  2. Call with profile==null → expect '/profile-setup'.
  3. Call with '/login' (public but logged-in incomplete) → expect '/profile-setup'.
  4. Call with '/profile-setup' → expect null (stay).
- **Esperado:** Logged-in users without a completed displayName are funneled to /profile-setup from any non-setup route; they stay on /profile-setup. Missing doc is treated as incomplete.

### auth-58 — authRedirect: profile loading blocks redirect (no flicker)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** auth = AsyncData(user); userProfileProvider = AsyncLoading.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call authRedirect(read,'/home') and '/profile-setup'.
- **Esperado:** Returns null while the profile is loading — avoids the /home→/profile-setup and /profile-setup→/home flicker for freshly-signed-in users.

### auth-59 — authRedirect: complete profile leaves /profile-setup → /home; authenticated on public → /home (except /splash)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** auth = AsyncData(user); userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile with non-null displayName, athlete role).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call authRedirect(read,'/profile-setup') → expect '/home'.
  2. Call with '/login' and '/welcome' → expect '/home'.
  3. Call with '/home' and '/workout' → expect null (stay).
  4. Call with '/splash' → expect null.
- **Esperado:** Onboarding-complete athlete is pushed out of /profile-setup and off public routes to /home, but stays on protected routes and is never bounced off /splash.

### auth-60 — authRedirect ROLE GATE: trainer with incomplete trainer profile → /profile/edit-trainer?mode=onboarding (athlete is not)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** auth = AsyncData(user); userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile, displayName set). Build two profiles: role=trainer with trainerProfileComplete=false, and role=athlete.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Trainer-incomplete, call authRedirect(read,'/home') → expect '/profile/edit-trainer?mode=onboarding'.
  2. Trainer-incomplete, call with '/profile/edit-trainer' and '/profile/edit-trainer?mode=onboarding' → expect null (self-skip, no loop).
  3. Trainer-incomplete, call with a public route '/login' → expect '/home' (public branch, not the trainer gate).
  4. Athlete with same displayName-complete profile, call '/home' → expect null (athlete NOT gated).
- **Esperado:** The ADR-TPO-003 trainer-incomplete gate fires only for role==trainer && !trainerProfileComplete on non-public, non-edit-trainer routes; it self-skips edit-trainer to avoid a loop; athletes are never sent to trainer onboarding. This is the core athlete-vs-trainer divergence.

### auth-61 — authRedirect: account-deletion-in-flight defers all redirects for logged-in user
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** auth = AsyncData(user); accountDeletionInFlightProvider == true; userProfileProvider can be AsyncData(null) (profile already deleted by CF cascade).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call authRedirect(read,'/home') with the deletion flag true and profile null.
  2. Call with '/profile-setup'.
- **Esperado:** Returns null (defer) while deletion is in flight — prevents a mid-cascade bounce to /profile-setup during the loggedIn==true + profile==null gap. Without this gate the deleting user would flash /profile-setup then /welcome.

### auth-62 — AuthInput: eye toggle flips obscureText and shows correct icon/tooltip
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump AuthInput with obscureText:true, suffixToggle:true.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert the field starts obscured and the eye icon shows 'Mostrar contraseña'.
  2. Tap the eye toggle.
  3. Assert text is now visible and tooltip flips to 'Ocultar contraseña'.
- **Esperado:** Tapping the suffix toggle flips _obscured each time; icon (eye/eyeOff) and tooltip update accordingly. No toggle rendered when suffixToggle is false.

# Módulo: chat

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/chat/. 28 new/uplift cases targeting regression-prone gaps: async loading/error/retry states on both screens, sending-state composer UI, batch atomicity, malformed-doc filtering, boundary preview truncation, relative-time branches, _otherUidOf edge cases, route param parsing, and entry-point failure. Excludes cases already covered by existing tests (chatIdFor, getOrCreate idempotency, basic send, ordering/limit, JSON round-trips, deleted-user rendering)._

### chat-01 — sendMessage commits message doc and parent preview update atomically (batch)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created via getOrCreate(aaa,bbb).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.sendMessage(chatId:'aaa_bbb', senderId:'aaa', text:'hola').
  2. Read the messages sub-collection of chats/aaa_bbb.
  3. Read the parent chats/aaa_bbb doc.
- **Esperado:** Exactly one message doc exists AND the parent has lastMessageText='hola', lastMessageSenderId='aaa', lastMessageAt not null — both writes present from the single batch.commit(), never one without the other.

### chat-02 — sendMessage stores its own generated doc id in the message body
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.sendMessage(chatId:'aaa_bbb', senderId:'aaa', text:'hola').
  2. Fetch the single message doc.
  3. Compare its data field 'id' against the Firestore document id.
- **Esperado:** The message doc's 'id' field equals msgRef.id (the auto-generated document id), so Message.id is self-consistent after fromJson.

### chat-03 — sendMessage rejects empty string with ArgumentError and writes nothing
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.sendMessage(chatId:'aaa_bbb', senderId:'aaa', text:'').
  2. Expect it to throw.
  3. Read the messages sub-collection.
- **Esperado:** Throws ArgumentError; messages sub-collection is empty; parent lastMessage* fields remain unset.

### chat-04 — preview not truncated when text length is exactly previewMaxChars (80) boundary
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created. previewMaxChars=80.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build text = 'x' * 80.
  2. Call repo.sendMessage(chatId:'aaa_bbb', senderId:'aaa', text: that 80-char text).
  3. Read parent lastMessageText.
- **Esperado:** lastMessageText length is exactly 80 with NO ellipsis (boundary <= previewMaxChars returns text unchanged).

### chat-05 — preview truncated at 81 chars producing 80 chars + ellipsis
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build text = 'x' * 81.
  2. Call repo.sendMessage with that text.
  3. Read parent lastMessageText.
- **Esperado:** lastMessageText has length 81 (80 chars + '…') and ends with the Unicode ellipsis — first char over the limit triggers truncation.

### chat-06 — watchMessages filters out docs whose createdAt is still null (unresolved serverTimestamp)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Manually write a raw message doc into chats/aaa_bbb/messages with senderId+text but createdAt:null.
  2. Also send one valid message via repo.sendMessage.
  3. Read repo.watchMessages('aaa_bbb').first.
- **Esperado:** Only the valid message is emitted; the createdAt:null doc is dropped by _messageFromDoc and does not crash fromJson.

### chat-07 — watchChatsForUser filters out chat docs with null createdAt
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Write a raw chats doc with members:['aaa','bbb'], lastMessageAt set, but createdAt:null.
  2. Read repo.watchChatsForUser('aaa').first.
- **Esperado:** The malformed chat is excluded (returns empty / does not include it); no exception thrown by _chatFromDoc.

### chat-08 — watchChatsForUser omits chats that have no lastMessageAt (Firestore orderBy excludes missing field)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. getOrCreate(aaa,bbb) but do NOT send any message (no lastMessageAt).
  2. Read repo.watchChatsForUser('aaa').first.
- **Esperado:** The freshly created, message-less chat is NOT returned — documented MVP behavior: empty chats stay out of the list until first send.

### chat-09 — watchMessages default limit is 50
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; chat 'aaa_bbb' created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Send 55 messages to the chat.
  2. Read repo.watchMessages('aaa_bbb').first using default limit.
- **Esperado:** Exactly 50 messages emitted (defaultMessagesLimit), newest-first.

### chat-10 — chatIdFor sorts uids lexicographically regardless of argument order
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure static helper).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Compute ChatRepository.chatIdFor('mmm','aaa').
  2. Compute ChatRepository.chatIdFor('aaa','mmm').
- **Esperado:** Both return 'aaa_mmm' — deterministic and order-independent.

### chat-11 — messagesProvider short-circuits to empty stream for empty chatId without hitting the repository
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with FakeFirebaseFirestore, currentUid='aaa'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read messagesProvider('').future.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to an empty list immediately (guard returns Stream.value(const [])); no Firestore query issued.

### chat-12 — chatsForCurrentUserProvider emits empty when currentUid is null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUidProvider overridden to null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read chatsForCurrentUserProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to an empty list; repository.watchChatsForUser is never called.

### chat-13 — chatForLinkProvider picks the OTHER member when current user is the trainer
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer, currentUid='trainer-1'; TrainerLink(trainerId:'trainer-1', athleteId:'athlete-1').
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read chatForLinkProvider(link).future.
  2. Inspect returned chat.members.
- **Esperado:** otherId resolves to 'athlete-1' (not self); chat.members contains both 'trainer-1' and 'athlete-1'.

### chat-14 — chatForLinkProvider throws StateError when no authenticated user
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUid null; a TrainerLink.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read chatForLinkProvider(link).future and await.
- **Esperado:** Throws StateError('No hay usuario autenticado'); no chat doc created in Firestore.

### chat-15 — ChatListScreen shows loading spinner while chats stream is pending
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; chatsForCurrentUserProvider overridden with a never-completing/pending stream (e.g. Stream that emits nothing yet).
- **Pasos:**

  2. pump() once (do not pumpAndSettle).
- **Esperado:** A CircularProgressIndicator is shown (loading branch); no list, no empty state.

### chat-16 — ChatListScreen shows error state with Retry that invalidates the provider
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  3. Tap 'Reintentar'.
- **Esperado:** Error state rendered; tapping Reintentar triggers ref.invalidate(chatsForCurrentUserProvider) (provider re-subscribed). Verify via spy override or that the button is wired to onRetry.

### chat-17 — ChatListScreen row falls back to 'Iniciá la conversación' when lastMessageText is null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; one chat with lastMessageText=null but lastMessageAt set; public profile provided.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatListScreen with a chat that has no lastMessageText.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** Row shows the placeholder subtitle 'Iniciá la conversación' instead of a blank/null subtitle.

### chat-18 — ChatListScreen hides the timestamp when lastMessageAt is null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### chat-19 — ChatListScreen row shows skeleton while the other user's public profile is loading
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### chat-20 — _relativeTime returns 'recién' under 1 minute and 'hace Nm' under 1 hour
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; ChatListScreen; chat with lastMessageAt = now-30s, then a second case now-5m.

  2. Render a chat with lastMessageAt 5 minutes ago; assert label.
- **Esperado:** First shows 'recién'; second shows 'hace 5m' — exercises the <1min and <1hour branches.

### chat-21 — _relativeTime shows 'hace Nh' (<1 day) and 'hace Nd' (<7 days) branches

### chat-22 — ChatScreen shows loading spinner while messages stream is pending

### chat-23 — ChatScreen shows error text when messages stream errors

### chat-24 — ChatScreen AppBar falls back to 'Usuario' on public-profile error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### chat-25 — ChatScreen bubble alignment: my messages right/accent, other's left/card
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; currentUid='aaa'; messages stream with one msg from 'aaa' and one from 'bbb'.
- **Pasos:**

  2. Locate the _Bubble (or Align) for each message and inspect alignment.
- **Esperado:** Message with senderId=='aaa' is Alignment.centerRight (isMine, accent background); message from 'bbb' is Alignment.centerLeft (card background with border).

### chat-26 — ChatScreen composer disables input and shows spinner while sending
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope over FakeFirebaseFirestore with a real repo whose sendMessage is delayed (e.g. wrap provider to add latency); currentUid='aaa'; chat created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatScreen, enter 'hola' in the TextField.
  2. Tap 'Enviar'.
  3. pump() once (before the send future completes) and inspect.
- **Esperado:** While _sending is true: the send IconButton's onPressed is null (disabled) and shows a CircularProgressIndicator instead of the send icon; the TextField is disabled (enabled:false). After completion the textfield clears and re-enables.

### chat-27 — ChatScreen shows error SnackBar and keeps text when sendMessage throws
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; chatRepositoryProvider overridden with a stub whose sendMessage throws; currentUid='aaa'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatScreen, enter 'hola', tap 'Enviar'.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** SnackBar 'No pudimos enviar el mensaje. Probá de nuevo.' is shown; the TextField is NOT cleared (text 'hola' preserved); _sending resets to false so the user can retry; no analytics event logged.

### chat-28 — ChatScreen does nothing on send when currentUid is null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; currentUidProvider overridden to null; chat created on FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatScreen, enter 'hola', tap 'Enviar'.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
  3. Read the messages sub-collection.
- **Esperado:** _onSend early-returns (no currentUid); no message persisted; no snackbar; no crash.

### chat-29 — ChatScreen logs analytics chat_message_sent exactly once on successful send
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope over FakeFirebaseFirestore; FakeAnalyticsService injected; currentUid='aaa'; chat created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatScreen, enter 'hola', tap 'Enviar', pumpAndSettle.
  2. Inspect analytics.events.
- **Esperado:** Exactly one 'chat_message_sent' event recorded with chatId and senderId='aaa', fired only after the repo write succeeds (not on validation-failed sends).

### chat-30 — _onSend ignores re-entrant taps while a send is in flight
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; repo with delayed sendMessage; currentUid='aaa'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter 'hola', tap 'Enviar' twice rapidly before the first completes.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
  3. Count persisted messages.
- **Esperado:** Only one message is written — the _sending guard (if (_sending) return) blocks the second invocation.

### chat-31 — Route chat/:chatId parses chatId path param and 'other' query param into ChatScreen
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** go_router configured per lib/app/router.dart; authenticated session reaching the coach branch.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Navigate to '/coach/chat/aaa_bbb?other=bbb'.
  2. Inspect the built ChatScreen widget params.
- **Esperado:** ChatScreen receives chatId='aaa_bbb' and otherUid='bbb'.

### chat-32 — Route chat/:chatId defaults otherUid to empty string when 'other' query param missing
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** go_router configured per router.dart.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Navigate to '/coach/chat/aaa_bbb' with no 'other' query param.
  2. Inspect built ChatScreen.
- **Esperado:** ChatScreen receives otherUid='' (fallback). The screen still renders (AppBar resolves via empty-uid profile lookup → 'Usuario eliminado' or skeleton) without crashing.

### chat-33 — _otherUidOf returns '' when current uid is not a member (defensive orElse)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; ChatListScreen; chat with members ['xxx','yyy']; currentUid='aaa' (not a member).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatListScreen with that mismatched chat and currentUid.
  2. pumpAndSettle and inspect the row's resolved other uid / profile lookup.
- **Esperado:** _otherUidOf returns '' (firstWhere orElse), so the row queries userPublicProfileProvider('') and degrades gracefully (skeleton/'Usuario eliminado') without throwing.

### chat-34 — Athlete entry point _onMessage resolves chat then pushes /coach/chat route with trainer as other
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView with an active TrainerLink; currentUid = athlete; FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the MENSAJE button.
  2. Await chatForLinkProvider resolution.
  3. Inspect the pushed route.
- **Esperado:** On success, navigates to '/coach/chat/{chatId}?other={trainerId}' where chatId matches chatIdFor(athlete,trainer); since this view is athlete-only the 'other' is correctly the trainer.

### chat-35 — Athlete entry point _onMessage shows error SnackBar when chat resolution fails
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView; chatForLinkProvider overridden to throw (e.g. Firestore error).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap MENSAJE.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** No navigation occurs; SnackBar 'No pudimos abrir el chat. Probá de nuevo.' is shown; the context.mounted guard prevents using a stale context.

### chat-36 — ChatScreen renders trainer's own bubbles on the right when viewing as trainer
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; currentUid = 'trainer-1'; messages with one from 'trainer-1' and one from 'athlete-1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ChatScreen(otherUid:'athlete-1') with currentUid='trainer-1'.
  2. pumpAndSettle and inspect bubble alignment.
- **Esperado:** isMine is computed per-viewer: trainer-1's message is right/accent, athlete-1's is left/card — confirms role-agnostic ownership is driven solely by senderId == currentUid.

# Módulo: check_in

_Test-case catalog for lib/features/check_in/ (CheckIn domain model + dateKey, CheckInRepository idempotent per-day upsert at /users/{uid}/checkIns/{date}, todayCheckInProvider + CheckInNotifier, CheckInDialog, and the FeedScreen once-per-session trigger). 32 cases spanning domain/data/logic/ui/integration. Cases are ID-prefixed check_in-NN; titles reference existing SCENARIO ids where they extend prior coverage. Existing tests already cover: dateKey padding, fromJson/toJson roundtrip, repo getToday/create/idempotency/null-gym, provider auth-gate + confirm, dialog subtext/NO/SÍ + error/success handling — those are NOT duplicated; this catalog adds boundary, state, role, and trigger-logic gaps._

### check_in-01 — dateKey uses local date components (timezone boundary)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None. Pure function CheckIn.dateKey.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Construct a local DateTime at a day boundary, e.g. DateTime(2026, 5, 15, 23, 59) and DateTime(2026, 5, 16, 0, 1).
  2. Call CheckIn.dateKey on each.
- **Esperado:** Returns '2026-05-15' and '2026-05-16' respectively — keyed strictly off local Y/M/D, never shifted by time-of-day. Confirms per-day dedup uses the user's local calendar day.

### check_in-02 — dateKey pads single-digit month and day to 2 digits
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call CheckIn.dateKey(DateTime(2026, 1, 3)).
  2. Call CheckIn.dateKey(DateTime(2026, 12, 9)).
- **Esperado:** Returns '2026-01-03' and '2026-12-09'. (Extends existing SCENARIO-326-datekey with both-field padding and a two-digit-month case.)

### check_in-03 — dateKey is stable across DateTime.now microsecond drift
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Capture d = DateTime.now().toLocal().
  2. Call CheckIn.dateKey(d) twice in succession.
  3. Compare both results.
- **Esperado:** Both calls return the identical 'YYYY-MM-DD' string; output ignores hour/minute/second/ms — guaranteeing the doc-id is reproducible for a given day.

### check_in-04 — fromJson maps Firestore Timestamp to UTC DateTime
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None. Uses TimestampConverter via CheckIn.fromJson.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build json with checkedInAt = Timestamp.fromDate(DateTime.utc(2026,5,15,10,0,0)) plus required uid/date.
  2. Call CheckIn.fromJson(json).
  3. Inspect checkedInAt.isUtc and its value.
- **Esperado:** checkedInAt is a DateTime with isUtc == true equal to 2026-05-15T10:00:00Z. Verifies TimestampConverter.fromJson normalizes to UTC (invariant: timestamps stored/read as UTC).

### check_in-05 — toJson serializes checkedInAt back to a Firestore Timestamp
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a CheckIn with checkedInAt = DateTime.utc(2026,5,15,10,0,0).
  2. Call toJson().
  3. Inspect the type and value of json['checkedInAt'].
- **Esperado:** json['checkedInAt'] is a cloud_firestore Timestamp equal to the original instant. Roundtrip (toJson→fromJson) preserves uid/date/gymId/gymName/checkedInAt.

### check_in-06 — fromJson tolerates null gymId and gymName
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build json with gymId: null and gymName: null plus required fields.
  2. Call CheckIn.fromJson(json).
- **Esperado:** Parses without throwing; gymId and gymName are null. (Extends existing SCENARIO-326 null-gym to assert no exception for the at-home check-in shape.)

### check_in-07 — fromJson throws on missing required field (uid/date/checkedInAt)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build json omitting 'checkedInAt' (and separately omitting 'uid').
  2. Call CheckIn.fromJson(json).
- **Esperado:** Throws (TypeError/format error) rather than silently producing a partial model — guards against malformed Firestore docs being treated as valid check-ins.

### check_in-08 — getTodayForUser returns null when no doc exists
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore empty; uid has no checkIns subcollection. (Existing SCENARIO-327 baseline — retain.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Instantiate CheckInRepository with FakeFirebaseFirestore.
  2. Call getTodayForUser('user-x').
- **Esperado:** Returns null. No exception. Confirms the not-checked-in-today path that gates the dialog.

### check_in-09 — getTodayForUser returns null when doc exists for a DIFFERENT day
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with a check-in doc whose id is yesterday's dateKey.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed /users/{uid}/checkIns/{yesterdayKey} with a valid check-in map.
  2. Call getTodayForUser(uid).
- **Esperado:** Returns null — getTodayForUser reads only doc id == today's dateKey. A prior day's check-in must NOT suppress today's dialog. Critical regression guard for the per-day reset.

### check_in-10 — getTodayForUser returns the existing CheckIn for today
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with today's check-in doc (id == today's dateKey). (Existing SCENARIO-328 baseline.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed /users/{uid}/checkIns/{todayKey} with uid/date/checkedInAt/gymId/gymName.
  2. Call getTodayForUser(uid).
- **Esperado:** Returns a CheckIn with matching uid, date == todayKey, gymId, gymName.

### check_in-11 — getTodayForUser scopes reads per-uid (no cross-user leakage)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with today's check-in for userA only.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed /users/userA/checkIns/{todayKey}.
  2. Call getTodayForUser('userB').
- **Esperado:** Returns null for userB. Confirms _col(uid) isolates each user's checkIns subcollection — no other athlete's check-in is visible.

### check_in-12 — createTodayCheckIn writes doc at today's dateKey with inGym=true fields
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore. (Existing SCENARIO-329 baseline.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: true, gymId: 'gym1', gymName: 'Smart Fit').
  2. Read /users/{uid}/checkIns/{todayKey}.
- **Esperado:** Doc exists at id == today's dateKey; data has uid, date == todayKey, gymId 'gym1', gymName 'Smart Fit', and a checkedInAt Timestamp. Returned CheckIn matches.

### check_in-13 — createTodayCheckIn stores null gym fields when inGym=false even if gymId passed
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: false, gymId: 'gym1', gymName: 'Smart Fit').
  2. Inspect returned CheckIn and the persisted doc.
- **Esperado:** gymId and gymName are null in both the returned model and Firestore — inGym is the authority; gym args are ignored when inGym is false. Business-rule guard for the at-home (no-gym) check-in.

### check_in-14 — createTodayCheckIn persists checkedInAt as UTC
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: true, gymId: 'g', gymName: 'G').
  2. Read back the doc and convert checkedInAt Timestamp to DateTime; also re-parse via getTodayForUser.
- **Esperado:** checkedInAt corresponds to now in UTC (repo uses now.toUtc()); getTodayForUser returns it as a UTC DateTime. No local-offset drift in stored time.

### check_in-15 — createTodayCheckIn is idempotent — second call returns existing, no overwrite
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore. (Existing idempotency test baseline — retain.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: true, gymId: 'gym1', gymName: 'Smart Fit').
  2. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: false) again (different params).
  3. Read the checkIns collection.
- **Esperado:** Second call returns the FIRST doc's data (gymId 'gym1', gymName 'Smart Fit') — does not overwrite to null. Exactly one doc with id == todayKey exists. Core invariant: one check-in per local day.

### check_in-16 — createTodayCheckIn idempotency preserves original checkedInAt timestamp
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: true, gymId: 'g', gymName: 'G') and capture returned checkedInAt.
  2. Call createTodayCheckIn(uid, inGym: true, gymId: 'g', gymName: 'G') a second time.
  3. Compare checkedInAt of both returns.
- **Esperado:** Second return's checkedInAt equals the first's (existing doc returned, not a fresh now). The recorded entry time is immutable for the day.

### check_in-17 — todayCheckInProvider returns null when unauthenticated and never calls repo
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUidProvider overridden to null and a mock repo. (Existing baseline — retain.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read todayCheckInProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to null; repo.getTodayForUser is never invoked (verifyNever). Auth-gate enforced at provider layer.

### check_in-18 — todayCheckInProvider delegates to repo and returns its result when authed
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider == 'u1'; mock repo.getTodayForUser('u1') returns a CheckIn.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read todayCheckInProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Returns the repo's CheckIn; repo.getTodayForUser('u1') called once with the current uid.

### check_in-19 — todayCheckInProvider surfaces repository errors as AsyncError
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider == 'u1'; mock repo.getTodayForUser throws (e.g. Firestore unavailable).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Listen to todayCheckInProvider and read its state / await future.
- **Esperado:** Provider enters AsyncError (future throws). The FeedScreen await will propagate — confirms error path is observable rather than silently null.

### check_in-20 — CheckInNotifier.confirm is a no-op when unauthenticated
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider == null; mock repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call checkInNotifierProvider.notifier.confirm(gymId: 'g', gymName: 'G').
  2. Inspect notifier state and repo interactions.
- **Esperado:** Returns early; repo.createTodayCheckIn never called; state not left in error/loading. No write attempted without a uid.

### check_in-21 — CheckInNotifier.confirm with gym maps inGym=true
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider == 'u1'; mock repo returns a CheckIn. (Existing baseline confirms call — extend to assert inGym mapping.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call confirm(gymId: 'gym1', gymName: 'Smart Fit').
  2. Verify repo.createTodayCheckIn args.
- **Esperado:** repo.createTodayCheckIn('u1', inGym: true, gymId: 'gym1', gymName: 'Smart Fit') called once — because gymId != null drives inGym=true.

### check_in-22 — CheckInNotifier.confirm with null gymId maps inGym=false
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider == 'u1'; mock repo returns a CheckIn.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call confirm(gymId: null, gymName: null).
  2. Verify repo.createTodayCheckIn args.
- **Esperado:** repo.createTodayCheckIn('u1', inGym: false, gymId: null, gymName: null) called once — the SÍ button for a user with no configured gym still records a no-gym check-in.

### check_in-23 — CheckInNotifier.confirm sets error state and invalidates today provider correctly on failure vs success
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider == 'u1'; one container where repo.createTodayCheckIn throws, one where it returns a CheckIn.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Failure: call confirm(...) with throwing repo; read checkInNotifierProvider state.
  2. Success: call confirm(...) with succeeding repo; read state and confirm todayCheckInProvider is invalidated/re-fetched.
- **Esperado:** Failure → state.hasError is true (error swallowed into AsyncValue.guard, not rethrown). Success → state holds the CheckIn, no error, and todayCheckInProvider is invalidated so the next FeedScreen mount sees the new check-in.

### check_in-24 — Dialog renders gym subtext when gymId & non-empty gymName provided
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** es-AR locale harness. (Existing SCENARIO-333 baseline.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CheckInDialog(gymId: 'smart-fit-palermo', gymName: 'SMART FIT').
  2. Inspect header and subtext.
- **Esperado:** Header '¿ESTÁS EN EL GYM HOY?' shown; subtext contains 'SMART FIT' (checkInGymSubtext). Map-pin icon present.

### check_in-25 — Dialog renders NEUTRAL subtext when gymId null OR gymName empty
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** es-AR locale harness. (Existing SCENARIO-334 covers null; extend with empty-string gymName.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CheckInDialog(gymId: null, gymName: null) → check subtext.
  2. Pump CheckInDialog(gymId: 'gym1', gymName: '') → check subtext.
- **Esperado:** Both render 'Confirma tu entrenamiento de hoy' (checkInNeutralSubtext). The subtext gate requires gymId != null AND gymName != null AND gymName non-empty — empty gymName falls back to neutral.

### check_in-26 — Dialog NO button pops without writing a check-in
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Dialog opened via showDialog inside harness; mock/real notifier. (Existing SCENARIO-338 partial — extend to assert no confirm call.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the dialog.
  2. Tap 'NO'.
  3. Verify dialog dismissed and notifier.confirm was never called.
- **Esperado:** Dialog closes; no check-in is created (confirm not invoked). User declining must not record a check-in.

### check_in-27 — Dialog SÍ on success closes dialog with no SnackBar
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** checkInNotifierProvider overridden with a notifier whose confirm leaves no error. (Existing error-handling success baseline — retain.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the dialog.
  2. Tap 'SÍ, ENTRÉ'.
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** Dialog dismissed ('SÍ, ENTRÉ' gone); no error SnackBar 'No pudimos registrar tu check-in. Probá de nuevo.' shown.

### check_in-28 — Dialog SÍ on failure keeps dialog open and shows error SnackBar (retry)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** checkInNotifierProvider overridden with a notifier whose confirm sets error via AsyncValue.guard. (Existing error-handling baseline — retain.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the dialog.
  2. Tap 'SÍ, ENTRÉ'.
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** Error SnackBar 'No pudimos registrar tu check-in. Probá de nuevo.' shown AND dialog stays open ('SÍ, ENTRÉ' still present) so the user can retry. Guards the swallowed-error UX contract.

### check_in-29 — Dialog passes correct gymId/gymName through to confirm
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Spy/mock notifier capturing confirm args; CheckInDialog(gymId:'gym1', gymName:'SMART FIT').
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open dialog with gymId 'gym1', gymName 'SMART FIT'.
  2. Tap 'SÍ, ENTRÉ'.
  3. Inspect captured confirm args.
- **Esperado:** confirm called with gymId 'gym1', gymName 'SMART FIT'. SÍ wires the dialog's gym props straight to the notifier (REQ-WRC-007/008).

### check_in-30 — gymNameFromId resolves known/unknown/sentinel/empty ids
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None. Pure function in feed/domain/gym_name.dart (drives dialog copy).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call gymNameFromId('smart-fit-palermo'), gymNameFromId('unknown-gym-99'), gymNameFromId(null), gymNameFromId(''), gymNameFromId(kNoGymId).
- **Esperado:** 'smart-fit-palermo' → 'SMART FIT'; unknown id → 'UNKNOWN-GYM-99' (uppercase fallback, stale-catalog signal); null/''/kNoGymId → '' (empty → caller hides gym subtext, dialog uses neutral copy).

### check_in-31 — FeedScreen trigger: shows dialog at most once per session and respects guards
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated uid; todayCheckInProvider returns null (not checked in); userProfileProvider has gymId. Pump FeedScreen in a Riverpod+MaterialApp harness.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Mount FeedScreen; let the post-frame callback run; assert CheckInDialog appears.
  2. Dismiss it (NO).
  3. Remount FeedScreen (simulate tab switch) within the same ProviderScope.
  4. Assert the dialog does NOT reappear (session flag set).
- **Esperado:** Dialog shown exactly once; on remount the _checkInDialogShownThisSessionProvider guard suppresses it. The flag is set BEFORE awaiting showDialog, preventing duplicate dialogs on rapid remount.

### check_in-32 — FeedScreen trigger: dialog suppressed when unauthenticated or already checked in today
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Two scenarios in fresh ProviderScopes: (a) currentUidProvider null; (b) authed uid but todayCheckInProvider returns a non-null CheckIn.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Scenario (a): mount FeedScreen with null uid; let post-frame run.
  2. Scenario (b): mount FeedScreen with a uid and an existing today check-in; let post-frame run.
- **Esperado:** In both scenarios no CheckInDialog is shown. Auth-gate (uid==null returns early) and check-in guard (today != null returns early) each suppress the dialog. Confirms the athlete who already checked in is not re-prompted.

# Módulo: coach

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/coach/ (TREINO Coach/PF module). Covers role gating (CoachScreen athlete vs trainer), trainer-link lifecycle, agenda booking/slot-computation business rules (24h cancel, 28-day limit, deterministic doc IDs, ADR-1 cancel/rebook, ADR-7 minute precision), availability rules/overrides, trainer discovery (geohash + haversine + filters), trainer-side scheduling (single/recurring + series cancel), athlete read-only agenda, athlete detail (plans/notes/billing/measurements), privacy share toggle, and the 30-day review prompt. Priorities favor data-integrity and business-rule regressions. Many domain/repo cases mirror existing SCENARIO-tagged tests under test/features/coach/ — they are marked here for completeness; net-new high-value gaps are the UI/integration cases._

### coach-01 — CoachScreen renders AthleteCoachView for athlete role
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider resolves a UserProfile with role=athlete; currentAthleteLinkProvider overridden to AsyncData(null)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachScreen inside ProviderScope + MaterialApp with role=athlete
  2. Let providers settle
- **Esperado:** AthleteCoachView is shown (no link → TrainersListScreen discovery is rendered); TrainerCoachView is absent

### coach-02 — CoachScreen renders TrainerCoachView for trainer role
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider resolves role=trainer; trainerLinksStreamProvider overridden to empty list
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachScreen with role=trainer
  2. Let providers settle
- **Esperado:** TrainerCoachView shown with ALUMNOS/AGENDA segmented tabs; AthleteCoachView absent

### coach-03 — CoachScreen shows neutral loading surface when role is null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider in AsyncLoading (or error → valueOrNull null)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachScreen while userProfileProvider has no resolved role
- **Esperado:** _CoachLoadingView renders a blank SizedBox.expand() — no CircularProgressIndicator, no athlete/trainer view

### coach-04 — TrainerCoachView honors initialTab=agenda deep link
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** role=trainer; currentUidProvider returns a trainer uid
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachScreen(initialTab: 'agenda') with role=trainer
  2. Inspect DefaultTabController initial index
- **Esperado:** AGENDA sub-tab is selected (index 1); TrainerAgendaTab visible

### coach-05 — TrainerCoachView defaults to ALUMNOS for null/unknown initialTab
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** role=trainer
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachScreen(initialTab: 'bogus') and again with null
- **Esperado:** _resolveInitialIndex returns 0 → ALUMNOS tab selected in both cases

### coach-06 — Athlete with no link sees discovery list entry point
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** role=athlete; currentAthleteLinkProvider=AsyncData(null); trainerDiscoveryProvider returns a non-empty list
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump AthleteCoachView
  2. Settle
- **Esperado:** TrainersListScreen is rendered (ENCONTRÁ TU COACH title, specialty chips, list of trainers)

### coach-07 — Athlete pending link shows SOLICITUD ENVIADA card with cancel CTA
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentAthleteLinkProvider=AsyncData(link status=pending); userPublicProfileProvider(trainerId) resolves a name
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump AthleteCoachView
  2. Settle

### coach-33 — TrainerLink state machine rejects invalid transitions
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake firestore seeded with links of various statuses
- **Pasos:**
  1. accept() on terminated → expect StateError
  2. decline() on active → expect StateError
  3. terminate() on pending → expect StateError
  4. pause() on paused → expect StateError
  5. resume() on active → expect StateError
- **Esperado:** Each invalid transition throws StateError with current-status message; valid transitions update status + timestamp (mostly existing coverage; ensure all 5 guards)
