### coach-138 — End-to-end booking lifecycle across athlete and trainer accounts
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** emulator seed with linked athlete+coach; coach has availability
- **Pasos:**
  1. As coach create a session for the athlete (single)
  2. As athlete open agenda and verify it appears upcoming
  3. As coach cancel >24h ahead
  4. As athlete verify it disappears
- **Esperado:** Session propagates via streams in real time across both accounts; cancellation removes it from athlete upcoming and trainer dot (cross-account real-time stream behavior)

# Módulo: coach_hub

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/coach_hub/ — the TREINO Coach Hub web module (trainer-only). Covers Excel parse → exercise match → preview → assign-routine flow, the link-lifecycle dashboard (pending/active/paused/terminated), auth-gated login/not-allowed screens, the template builder, and the responsive shell (sidebar/scaffold/collapsed-provider). Cases are deduplicated against existing coverage: I avoided re-asserting the already-tested parser validation set, matcher exact/alias matches, template SCENARIO-727..734 column widths, sidebar 19-item registry, viewportFor() breakpoints, collapsed-provider persistence, and the dashboard SCEN-CHLM-007..017 link-lifecycle widget tests. New cases target gaps: parser boundary values (1/7 days, 52 weeks, repsMax defaulting), matcher fuzzy-score threshold and short-token (<3 char) skip, repository unmatched propagation under partial catalog, preview assign invariants (unmatched-block, no-athlete-block, multi-athlete partial-failure, parsedPlan cleared on success, manual-match removes-from-unmatched + fire-and-forget addAlias, plan==null redirect), upload screen (null bytes, processing error, disabled-button gating, byte formatting), login validation/error humanization, not-allowed sign-out, and shell active-route highlighting + sign-out redirects. Key business invariants identified: (1) day-sheet count must equal daysPerWeek or parse fails; (2) a plan with ANY unmatched exercise cannot be assigned; (3) at least one athlete must be selected; (4) only ACTIVE trainer links are assignable targets; (5) addAlias is fire-and-forget and must never block or surface errors; (6) routine built from plan maps restSec→60 default and exerciseId→'' for matched-but-empty._

### coach_hub-01 — parseExcelBytes accepts boundary daysPerWeek=1 with a single Día 1 sheet
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx built with a Plan sheet (Nombre, Días por semana=1, Duración semanas=8, Nivel=intermedio) and exactly one 'Día 1' sheet with one valid exercise row.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build the workbook bytes via the excel package matching the documented layout.
  2. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
  3. Inspect the returned RawParsedPlan.
- **Esperado:** Returns a RawParsedPlan with daysPerWeek==1, durationWeeks==8, level==ExperienceLevel.intermediate, and days.length==1 (no exception thrown).

### coach_hub-02 — parseExcelBytes accepts boundary daysPerWeek=7 and durationWeeks=52
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx with Plan sheet Días por semana=7, Duración semanas=52, and exactly seven Día sheets (Día 1..Día 7) each with at least one valid row.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build the workbook bytes.
  2. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
- **Esperado:** Returns RawParsedPlan with daysPerWeek==7, durationWeeks==52, days.length==7. Boundary values do not trip the 1..7 / 1..52 range guards.

### coach_hub-03 — parseExcelBytes rejects daysPerWeek=0 and durationWeeks=0 (lower boundary)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Two in-memory workbooks: one with Días por semana=0, one with Duración semanas=0 (otherwise valid).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes on the daysPerWeek=0 workbook.
  2. Call parseExcelBytes on the durationWeeks=0 workbook.
- **Esperado:** Each call throws ExcelParseException — the first with message 'Días por semana debe ser un número entre 1 y 7.', the second 'Duración semanas debe ser un número entre 1 y 52.'.

### coach_hub-04 — parseExcelBytes rejects durationWeeks=53 (upper boundary overflow)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx with Duración semanas=53, otherwise valid.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
- **Esperado:** Throws ExcelParseException with message 'Duración semanas debe ser un número entre 1 y 52.'.

### coach_hub-05 — parseExcelBytes defaults repsMax to repsMin when Reps Max cell is empty
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx with one Día sheet whose only row has Series=3, Reps Min=8, Reps Max cell left blank.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build the workbook bytes.
  2. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
  3. Read days[0].items[0].
- **Esperado:** The parsed item has repsMin==8 and repsMax==8 (empty Reps Max falls back to repsMin, per RawParsedItem repsMax: repsMax ?? repsMin).

### coach_hub-06 — parseExcelBytes accepts decimal Peso Kg and parses optional restSec/notes
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx with one Día row: Series=4, Reps Min=8, Reps Max=10, Peso Kg=52.5, Descanso Seg=90, Notas='Tempo 3-1-1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
  2. Inspect days[0].items[0].
- **Esperado:** Item has weightKg==52.5 (double), restSec==90, notes=='Tempo 3-1-1'. A row with empty Notas yields notes==null.

### coach_hub-07 — parseExcelBytes skips fully-empty rows but errors on a row missing Series
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx Día sheet with: row A fully blank (skipped), row B name='Press' but Series blank.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
- **Esperado:** Throws ExcelParseException naming the day and the 1-based row (e.g. 'Día 1, fila N: faltan series.'). Blank rows are silently ignored; a named row with no Series is a hard error.

### coach_hub-08 — parseExcelBytes errors when repsMin < 1 (zero/negative reps)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx Día row with name set, Series=3, Reps Min=0.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
- **Esperado:** Throws ExcelParseException with message 'Día N, fila M: faltan reps mínimas.'.

### coach_hub-09 — parseExcelBytes sorts day sheets by day number regardless of workbook order
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx with Días por semana=3 and day sheets created out of order (e.g. 'Día 3', 'Día 1', 'Día 2'), each with valid rows.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
  2. Map days to their dayNumber list.
- **Esperado:** Returned days are ordered [1, 2, 3] (days.sort by dayNumber). The 'Día N' regex is case/accent-insensitive (matches 'Dia 1' and 'Día 1').

### coach_hub-10 — parseExcelBytes ignores non-day sheets like Instrucciones when counting days
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** An in-memory .xlsx with Plan, Día 1, Día 2, Día 3 and an extra 'Instrucciones' sheet (Días por semana=3).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseExcelBytes(bytes).
- **Esperado:** Parses successfully; days.length==3. The Instrucciones sheet does not match _daySheetRegex and is not counted, so the daysPerWeek==dayCount invariant holds.

### coach_hub-11 — matchExercises skips tokens shorter than 3 chars in fuzzy matching
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog has one exercise name 'Remo con barra'. Raw day item rowName is 'el de barra' (tokens: 'el'(2,skip), 'de'(2,skip), 'barra'(5)).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build RawParsedDay with the item and call matchExercises(rawDays, catalog).
  2. Inspect the result.
- **Esperado:** Only the >=3-char token 'barra' is scored. Indexing and fuzzy scoring ignore tokens <3 chars, so matching depends solely on long tokens (verify the item resolves to 'Remo con barra' via the single shared token).

### coach_hub-12 — matchExercises requires fuzzy score >= ceil(tokens/2) to accept a match
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog exercise 'Sentadilla con barra' (tokens sentadilla/con/barra). Raw item rowName 'Press banca inclinado' shares zero >=3-char tokens with it.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call matchExercises with this item and a catalog where no exercise shares the majority of tokens.
  2. Inspect result.unmatched and result.days[0].items[0].
- **Esperado:** Item goes to unmatched (exerciseId==null, exerciseName==rowName) because best fuzzy score is below the ceil(tokenCount/2) threshold. Confirms the matcher does not over-match on a single coincidental token when 2+ are required.

### coach_hub-13 — matchExercises prefers exact normalized name over fuzzy match
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog has 'Press banca' (id=P1) and 'Press banca inclinado' (id=P2). Raw item rowName exactly 'Press Banca'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call matchExercises and read the resolved exerciseId.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to P1 (exact name path index.byName runs before _bestFuzzyMatch), not P2. Exact-match precedence is preserved.

### coach_hub-14 — normalize() collapses punctuation/whitespace and strips diacritics
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call normalize('  Sentadilla,  con   Barra (back-squat)!  ').
- **Esperado:** Returns 'sentadilla con barra back squat' — lowercased, accents removed, non-alphanumerics turned to single spaces, repeated whitespace collapsed, trimmed. (Distinct from existing 'quita acentos' test which only checks accents/case.)

### coach_hub-15 — matchExercises returns empty unmatched and preserves item count when every row matches
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog covers all exercise names used across a 2-day raw plan (5 items total).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call matchExercises(rawDays, catalog).
  2. Sum items across result.days; inspect result.unmatched.
- **Esperado:** result.unmatched is empty, total item count equals input (5), and every item has a non-null exerciseId plus exerciseName/muscleGroup taken from the catalog entry (not the raw rowName).

### coach_hub-16 — PlanImportRepository.parseAndMatch maps unmatched rows when catalog is partial
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Fake ExerciseRepository.listAll() returns a catalog covering only some of the plan's exercises. Valid .xlsx bytes available.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Construct PlanImportRepository with the fake exercise repo.
  2. Call parseAndMatch(bytes:).
  3. Inspect the returned ParsedPlan.
- **Esperado:** ParsedPlan carries name/daysPerWeek/durationWeeks/level from the Excel and a non-empty unmatched list for rows not in the catalog; matched rows carry exerciseId. (Complements existing repo test by asserting plan metadata is preserved alongside unmatched.)

### coach_hub-17 — PlanImportRepository.parseAndMatch wraps parse failures as PlanImportException(code:'parse-failed')
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Fake ExerciseRepository present. Bytes are a non-Excel blob (e.g. random bytes).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseAndMatch(bytes: <garbage>).
  2. Catch the thrown exception.
- **Esperado:** Throws PlanImportException with code=='parse-failed'. The underlying ExcelParseException message is surfaced when it is an ExcelParseException; arbitrary errors yield 'No pudimos leer el Excel.'. (Existing test covers corrupt bytes; this asserts the code field explicitly.)

### coach_hub-18 — buildPlanTemplateBytes round-trips and yields exactly 3 day sheets matching daysPerWeek
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call buildPlanTemplateBytes().
  2. Decode the bytes and call parseExcelBytes on them.
  3. Inspect the parsed plan.
- **Esperado:** Parsed plan has daysPerWeek==3 and days.length==3 with the three seeded exercise rows per day; the generated template always satisfies the day-count==daysPerWeek invariant. (Existing SCENARIO-734 round-trips; this adds the day-count assertion.)

### coach_hub-19 — Preview screen blocks assign and shows error when no athlete is selected
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** parsedPlanProvider seeded with a fully-matched ParsedPlan (unmatched empty). userProfileProvider returns a trainer profile. linksForTrainerProvider returns at least one ACTIVE link. No athlete toggled.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachHubPlanPreviewScreen inside a ProviderScope with the overrides.
  2. Tap the 'ASIGNAR PLAN' button without selecting any athlete.
- **Esperado:** No routine is created (routineRepository.createAssigned never called); inline error 'Elegí al menos un atleta antes de asignar.' is shown. Confirms the at-least-one-athlete invariant.

### coach_hub-20 — Preview screen blocks assign when the plan has unmatched exercises
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** parsedPlanProvider seeded with a ParsedPlan whose unmatched list is non-empty. Trainer profile present. At least one active link selected.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the preview screen with overrides.
  2. Select one athlete.
  3. Tap 'ASIGNAR PLAN'.
- **Esperado:** Assign is blocked with error 'Hay ejercicios sin match. Asignalos manualmente antes de continuar.'; no routine created. Confirms the no-unmatched-before-assign invariant. The _UnmatchedWarning banner is also visible.

### coach_hub-21 — Preview screen happy path assigns a single athlete, clears parsedPlan, and navigates to /dashboard
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Fully-matched ParsedPlan. Trainer profile (uid known). One active link. Fake routineRepository.createAssigned returns a routine with an id. Fake analyticsService. go_router test harness with /dashboard route.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the preview screen with overrides.
  2. Select the single active athlete.
  3. Tap 'ASIGNAR PLAN'.
  4. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** createAssigned is called once with a Routine where source==trainerAssigned, assignedBy==trainerUid, assignedTo==athleteId, level and numWeeks from the plan; analytics.logPlanAssigned fires; parsedPlanProvider is reset to null; a success SnackBar 'Plan asignado correctamente.' shows; navigation goes to /dashboard.

### coach_hub-22 — Preview screen assigns to multiple athletes and reports partial failure count
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Fully-matched ParsedPlan. Three active links. Fake routineRepository.createAssigned succeeds for two athletes and throws for one.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump preview screen; select all three athletes.
  2. Verify button label reads 'ASIGNAR PLAN A 3 ATLETAS'.
  3. Tap assign and pump.
- **Esperado:** createAssigned called once per selected athlete; since not all failed, parsedPlan is cleared and SnackBar reads 'Plan asignado a 2 atleta(s). 1 fallaron.' then navigates to /dashboard.

### coach_hub-23 — Preview screen shows global error and stays on screen when ALL assignments fail
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Fully-matched ParsedPlan. Two active links selected. Fake routineRepository.createAssigned throws for every athlete.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump preview screen; select both athletes; tap assign; pump.
- **Esperado:** Inline error 'No pudimos guardar el plan. Probá de nuevo.' is shown, _saving resets to false, parsedPlanProvider is NOT cleared, and no navigation occurs (user can retry). Confirms total-failure path differs from partial.

### coach_hub-24 — Preview screen redirects to /upload-plan when parsedPlan is null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** parsedPlanProvider returns null. go_router harness with /upload-plan route.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump CoachHubPlanPreviewScreen.
  2. Pump one frame so the post-frame callback runs.
- **Esperado:** A loading spinner renders, then a post-frame callback navigates to /upload-plan (guards against deep-linking the preview with no plan in memory).

### coach_hub-25 — Preview screen shows loading spinner while trainer profile is unresolved
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** parsedPlanProvider seeded with a valid plan but userProfileProvider returns AsyncLoading / valueOrNull == null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the preview screen with the profile provider unresolved.
- **Esperado:** Only a CircularProgressIndicator renders (no plan body, no assign button) until the profile resolves.

### coach_hub-26 — Preview manual-match maps an unmatched row, removes it from unmatched, and clears the banner
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ParsedPlan with exactly one unmatched item on Día 1. exercisesProvider returns a catalog containing a pickable exercise. cloudFunctionsProvider overridden with a fake.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the preview screen.
  2. Tap 'Asignar manualmente' on the unmatched item.
  3. In the bottom sheet, tap an exercise to pick it.
  4. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** parsedPlanProvider updates so the row gains exerciseId/exerciseName/muscleGroup from the picked exercise, the item leaves the unmatched list, the 'sin match' badge and _UnmatchedWarning disappear, and (with all rows now matched) assign is no longer blocked by the unmatched guard.

### coach_hub-27 — Preview manual-match search filters by name, muscle group, and alias
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Exercise picker sheet open with a catalog including an exercise whose alias (not name) matches the query.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the picker sheet for an unmatched row.
  2. Type a query that only matches an exercise's alias.
  3. Then type a query that matches nothing.
- **Esperado:** Alias query shows the matching exercise in the list (filter checks name, muscleGroup, and aliases, case-insensitive). The no-match query shows the 'Sin resultados.' empty state.

### coach_hub-28 — Preview addAlias is fire-and-forget — manual match succeeds even when the CF throws
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** cloudFunctionsProvider overridden so httpsCallable('addAlias').call(...) throws/rejects. One unmatched row, catalog available.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump preview; open picker for the unmatched row; pick an exercise; pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** The UI completes the manual match (row mapped, removed from unmatched) and shows no error to the user even though addAlias rejected — the failure is swallowed (debugPrint only). Confirms ADR-CXP-009 fire-and-forget invariant. (Complements existing SCENARIO-746/747 by asserting state still updates.)

### coach_hub-29 — Preview athlete picker shows empty-state when trainer has no ACTIVE links
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** linksForTrainerProvider returns links but none with status active (e.g. only pending/paused). Valid matched plan + trainer profile.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump preview screen and locate the _AthletePicker area.
- **Esperado:** Shows the message 'No tenés alumnos activos para asignarles este plan...' instead of a selectable list. Confirms only ACTIVE links are assignable targets (paused/pending/terminated excluded).

### coach_hub-30 — Preview athlete picker shows loading and error states for the links stream
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Valid matched plan + trainer profile. Variant A: linksForTrainerProvider in loading. Variant B: provider in error.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump preview with links provider loading; observe the picker area.
  2. Re-pump with links provider erroring; observe the picker area.
- **Esperado:** Loading shows a CircularProgressIndicator; error shows 'No pudimos cargar tus alumnos.' (the rest of the preview still renders).

### coach_hub-31 — Preview meta card and day subtitle format reps/rest/weight correctly
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ParsedPlan: daysPerWeek=4, durationWeeks=8, level intermediate. Day item A repsMin==repsMax==10 with restSec=90, weightKg=60; item B repsMin=8/repsMax=12, restSec null, weightKg null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump preview and read the meta tiles and item subtitles.
- **Esperado:** Meta shows 'Días/semana 4', 'Duración 8 sem', 'Nivel Intermedio'. Item A subtitle reads '3 × 10 · 90s · 60.0 kg' style (single rep value when min==max); item B reads '4 × 8-12' with no rest/weight segments when those are null.

### coach_hub-32 — Upload screen disables PROCESAR PLAN until a file is picked
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubUploadPlanScreen pumped with required providers; no file selected.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the upload screen.
  2. Inspect the 'PROCESAR PLAN' ElevatedButton onPressed state.
- **Esperado:** Button is disabled (onPressed==null) while _pickedFile is null and uses the dimmed disabledBackgroundColor. It enables only after a file is picked.

### coach_hub-33 — Upload screen shows error when the picked file has null bytes
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Upload screen with a stubbed picked PlatformFile whose bytes==null (simulating a withData failure).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Drive the screen to the state where _pickedFile is set but file.bytes is null.
  2. Tap 'PROCESAR PLAN'.
- **Esperado:** Error text 'No pudimos leer el archivo. Volvé a elegirlo.' is shown and parseAndMatch is never invoked.

### coach_hub-34 — Upload screen surfaces PlanImportException.message and stays on screen
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Upload screen with a picked file (non-null bytes). planImportRepositoryProvider overridden so parseAndMatch throws PlanImportException('Falta la hoja "Plan".', code:'parse-failed').
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the upload screen with a file selected.
  2. Tap 'PROCESAR PLAN'; pump.
- **Esperado:** The exception's message ('Falta la hoja "Plan".') is shown inline, _submitting resets to false, parsedPlanProvider stays null, and navigation to /upload-plan/preview does NOT happen.

### coach_hub-35 — Upload screen happy path stores ParsedPlan and navigates to preview
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Upload screen with a picked file. planImportRepositoryProvider overridden to return a valid ParsedPlan. go_router harness with /upload-plan/preview route.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump upload screen with file selected.
  2. Tap 'PROCESAR PLAN'; pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** parsedPlanProvider is set to the returned plan and the router navigates to /upload-plan/preview. While awaiting, the button shows a spinner and is non-re-entrant (second tap during _submitting is ignored).

### coach_hub-36 — Upload screen generic error message for non-PlanImportException failures
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Upload screen with picked file. planImportRepositoryProvider overridden to throw a plain Exception (not PlanImportException).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap 'PROCESAR PLAN'; pump.
- **Esperado:** Inline error reads the generic fallback 'No pudimos procesar el archivo. Probá de nuevo.' and the screen does not navigate.

### coach_hub-37 — Upload screen formats the selected file size (B / KB / MB)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Upload screen with a picked file whose size is set (test three sizes: 512 B, 2048 B, 3 MB).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render the _UploadCard with each file size.
- **Esperado:** Displays '512 B', '2.0 KB', and '3.0 MB' respectively (matches _formatBytes thresholds). The file name renders with ellipsis overflow.

### coach_hub-38 — Upload screen download-template triggers a browser download with correct filename/mime
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Upload screen with triggerBrowserDownload swapped for a spy (or run on web target). buildPlanTemplateBytes succeeds.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap 'Descargar template'; pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** triggerBrowserDownload is called once with filename 'treino-plan-template.xlsx' and the xlsx mime type; the button shows a spinner during generation and re-enables after. (Marked non-automatable as a pure widget test if browser_download cannot be injected; automatable if the call is mockable.)

### coach_hub-39 — Login form validates empty email/password and malformed email
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubLoginScreen pumped with auth providers overridden.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap 'INGRESAR' with both fields empty.
  2. Enter 'notanemail' as email and a password, tap 'INGRESAR'.
- **Esperado:** Empty fields show 'Ingresá tu email' and 'Ingresá tu contraseña'. Email without '@' shows 'Email inválido'. signIn is not called while validation fails.

### coach_hub-40 — Login humanizes an AuthFailure via its userMessage on failed sign-in
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Valid-format email/password entered. authNotifierProvider stubbed so signIn results in state.hasError with an AuthFailure carrying userMessage 'Credenciales inválidas.'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter a valid email and password.
  2. Tap 'INGRESAR'; pump.
- **Esperado:** The AuthFailure.userMessage ('Credenciales inválidas.') is shown inline; for a non-AuthFailure error the fallback 'No pudimos ingresar. Probá de nuevo.' is shown. _submitting resets to false so the user can retry.

### coach_hub-41 — Login calls signIn with trimmed email and shows spinner during submit
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Login screen with a spy auth notifier whose signIn never completes (to observe the busy state).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '  trainer@treino.app  ' (with spaces) and a password.
  2. Tap 'INGRESAR'.
- **Esperado:** signIn is invoked with email=='trainer@treino.app' (trimmed) and the raw password (not trimmed); the button shows a CircularProgressIndicator and is disabled while submitting; a second tap is ignored (non-re-entrant).

### coach_hub-42 — Not-allowed screen renders the trainer-only gate and a sign-out button
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubNotAllowedScreen pumped (shown when a non-trainer reaches the hub).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the screen and inspect its content.
- **Esperado:** Displays 'COACH HUB', 'SOLO PARA PFs', the explanatory copy, a lock icon, and a 'Cerrar sesión' OutlinedButton. (Auth-gating decision that routes athletes here is router-level; this verifies the destination screen.)

### coach_hub-43 — Not-allowed / dashboard sign-out calls FirebaseAuth.signOut (router redirect to /login)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Real Firebase auth on a device/emulator session signed in as an athlete (not-allowed) or trainer (dashboard).
- **Pasos:**
  1. From the not-allowed screen tap 'Cerrar sesión' (or 'Salir' on the dashboard).
  2. Observe auth state and routing.
- **Esperado:** FirebaseAuth.instance.signOut() runs; authStateChangesProvider emits null; the router redirects to /login. (Non-automatable as a unit test because it calls the FirebaseAuth singleton directly rather than an injectable provider.)

### coach_hub-44 — Dashboard shows the IMPORTAR PLAN DESDE EXCEL CTA and navigates to /upload-plan
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubDashboardScreen pumped with a trainer profile and trainerLinksStreamProvider returning an empty list. go_router harness with /upload-plan route.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the dashboard.
  2. Tap the 'IMPORTAR PLAN DESDE EXCEL' button.
- **Esperado:** Header greets the trainer ('BIENVENIDO, <NAME>'); tapping the import CTA navigates to /upload-plan.

### coach_hub-45 — Dashboard pending-requests section hides when no pending links and shows count when present
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile present. Variant A: stream returns no pending links. Variant B: stream returns 2 pending links.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump dashboard with no pending links; check for the SOLICITUDES PENDIENTES header.
  2. Re-pump with 2 pending links.
- **Esperado:** Variant A renders no pending section (SizedBox.shrink). Variant B renders 'SOLICITUDES PENDIENTES · 2' with one tile per request (keyed pending_request_<id>) showing Aceptar/Rechazar.

### coach_hub-46 — Dashboard Aceptar on a pending request calls repo.accept, logs analytics, and shows confirmation
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Stream returns one pending link. Fake trainerLinkRepository.accept succeeds. Fake analyticsService.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump dashboard; tap the keyed accept_<id> button; pump.
- **Esperado:** repo.accept(link.id) is called, analytics.logLinkAccepted(linkId:) fires, a 'Vínculo aceptado.' SnackBar shows, and the tile shows a busy spinner during the call (re-entrancy guarded by _busy).

### coach_hub-47 — Dashboard Rechazar on a pending request calls repo.decline; failure shows a SnackBar and re-enables
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Stream returns one pending link. Fake trainerLinkRepository.decline throws.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump dashboard; tap keyed decline_<id>; pump.
- **Esperado:** repo.decline(link.id) is invoked; on failure the error SnackBar 'No pudimos rechazar la solicitud.' shows and _busy resets to false so the buttons reappear. (Existing dashboard tests cover pause/resume/terminate, not accept/decline.)

### coach_hub-48 — Dashboard ACTIVOS section shows loading and error states for the links stream
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile present. Variant A: trainerLinksStreamProvider loading. Variant B: stream erroring. Filter includes active.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump dashboard with the stream loading; locate the ACTIVOS area.
  2. Re-pump with the stream erroring.
- **Esperado:** Loading shows the _SectionLoading spinner; error shows _SectionError text 'No pudimos cargar tus alumnos.' under the 'TUS ALUMNOS' label. (Existing tests assert data/empty states only.)

### coach_hub-49 — Dashboard active card 'Vinculado desde' falls back to requestedAt when acceptedAt is null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Stream returns one active link with acceptedAt==null and requestedAt set to a known date (e.g. 2026-02-03).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump dashboard with the active filter on and read the active tile subtitle.
- **Esperado:** Subtitle reads 'Vinculado desde 03/02/2026' using requestedAt (acceptedAt ?? requestedAt) formatted DD/MM/YYYY with no timezone shift.

### coach_hub-50 — Dashboard student tiles fall back to 'Atleta' when public profile is unresolved
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Stream returns one active link; userPublicProfileProvider(athleteId) returns AsyncLoading/null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump dashboard; read the active tile's name text.
- **Esperado:** Tile shows the placeholder name 'Atleta' (valueOrNull?.displayName ?? 'Atleta') and a default avatar, without crashing while the public profile loads.

### coach_hub-51 — _reasonDisplay maps every termination reason and falls back for unknown/null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (covered indirectly by SCEN-CHLM-011 widget tests, but assert the pure mapping if exposed/refactored).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Evaluate the historial tile for terminationReason values: 'declined', 'cancelled-by-athlete', 'trainer-terminated', null, and an unknown string.
- **Esperado:** Maps to 'Rechazado por el PF', 'Cancelado por el atleta', 'Terminado por el PF', and (for null and unknown) 'Vínculo terminado'. Guards the historial render from crashing on unexpected reasons.

### coach_hub-52 — Sidebar highlights the active item based on the current go_router location
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubSidebar pumped (expanded) inside a go_router whose location is '/rutinas'. sharedPreferencesProvider resolved.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the sidebar at location '/rutinas'.
  2. Then re-pump at a nested location '/rutinas/123'.
- **Esperado:** The 'Rutinas' row is rendered active (accent color, bold) for both '/rutinas' and '/rutinas/123' (active when location==route or startsWith(route + '/')), while other rows are inactive. (Existing sidebar tests cover width/labels and tap-nav, not active highlighting.)

### coach_hub-53 — Scaffold renders exactly one Scaffold with sidebar + top bar + bounded content
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubScaffold pumped with a sentinel child widget. sharedPreferencesProvider resolved.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the scaffold with a keyed child.
  2. Assert structure.
- **Esperado:** Exactly one Scaffold; the CoachHubSidebar and CoachHubTopBar are present; the child is wrapped in a ContentMaxWidth(maxWidth: 1240). (Re-confirms SCENARIO-748/749 single-Scaffold contract.)

### coach_hub-54 — Sidebar uses optimistic-expanded width while SharedPreferences is still resolving
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CoachHubSidebar pumped with sharedPreferencesProvider in AsyncLoading.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the sidebar before prefs resolve and measure the container width.
- **Esperado:** Sidebar renders expanded (264 px) — collapsed resolves to false via maybeWhen(orElse: () => false) until prefs are ready, so the first paint never flashes collapsed.

# Módulo: feed

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/feed/. Covers the 3-segment feed (AMIGOS/MI GYM/PÚBLICO), create-post composer with privacy gating + 280-char limit, user search with 2-char gate + 300ms debounce, public profile with 4-state follow button, friend-request inbox, the full friendship lifecycle (request/accept/reject/unfriend, self-accept block, idempotent sortedDocId, best-effort counter side-effects), and the once-per-session check-in dialog trigger. Key invariant found: the feed module is fully role-agnostic — there is NO athlete vs trainer branching anywhere (screens, providers, repos), so feed-44 asserts that invariant rather than testing divergent behavior. Cases are scoped to avoid duplicating existing coverage under test/features/feed/._

### feed-01 — AMIGOS segment renders friends-privacy posts newest-first
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated athlete with >=2 accepted friends; those friends have >=2 friends-privacy posts with distinct createdAt timestamps.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump FeedScreen with feedSegmentProvider = FeedSegment.amigos
  2. Override myFriendsFeedProvider to return a list of posts ordered newest-first
  3. Let the async settle
- **Esperado:** A PostCard is rendered for each post; cards appear in newest-first order; no empty-state and no spinner shown.

### feed-02 — AMIGOS segment shows empty state when no friend posts
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated user; myFriendsFeedProvider resolves to an empty list (either no friends, or friends with no posts).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump FeedScreen on the AMIGOS segment
  2. Override myFriendsFeedProvider to return const <Post>[]
  3. Settle
- **Esperado:** FeedEmptyState with message 'Aún no hay posts de tus amigos' is shown; no PostCard rendered.

### feed-03 — AMIGOS segment shows spinner while loading then content
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** myFriendsFeedProvider backed by a Completer that has not yet completed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump FeedScreen on AMIGOS with a pending future
  2. Verify a CircularProgressIndicator (accent color) is present
  3. Complete the future with posts and pump
- **Esperado:** Spinner shown during loading; after completion the spinner is gone and PostCards render.

### feed-04 — AMIGOS segment shows error copy on provider error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** myFriendsFeedProvider throws.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override myFriendsFeedProvider to throw
  2. Pump FeedScreen on AMIGOS
  3. Settle
- **Esperado:** Text 'No pudimos cargar tu feed. Intentá de nuevo.' is displayed; no PostCard and no spinner.

### feed-05 — MI GYM segment: null result (user has no gym) shows 'no gym' empty state
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** User profile has gymId == null, so myGymFeedProvider resolves to null (distinct from empty list).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set feedSegmentProvider = FeedSegment.gym
  2. Override myGymFeedProvider to return null
  3. Pump FeedScreen and settle
- **Esperado:** FeedEmptyState 'Todavía no estás en un gym' shown — NOT the 'sin posts' message. The null vs [] distinction is honored.

### feed-06 — MI GYM segment: empty list (gym exists, no posts) shows 'sin posts' empty state
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** User has a gymId; myGymFeedProvider resolves to const <Post>[].
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set segment = gym
  2. Override myGymFeedProvider to return []
  3. Pump and settle
- **Esperado:** FeedEmptyState 'Tu gym todavía no tiene posts' shown (different from the no-gym message).

### feed-07 — MI GYM segment renders gym posts newest-first
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** User has gymId 'smart-fit-palermo' with >=2 gym-privacy posts.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set segment = gym
  2. Override myGymFeedProvider with ordered posts
  3. Pump and settle
- **Esperado:** PostCard per post in newest-first order.

### feed-08 — PÚBLICO segment renders public posts and empty/error states
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** feedPublicProvider can be overridden with data / [] / error.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set segment = public
  2. Case A: override with posts → expect PostCards
  3. Case B: override with [] → expect FeedEmptyState 'Aún no hay posts públicos'
  4. Case C: override to throw → expect 'No pudimos cargar tu feed. Intentá de nuevo.'
- **Esperado:** Each of the three states renders its correct surface.

### feed-09 — Tapping segment pills switches feedSegmentProvider and body
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FeedScreen pumped with all three feed providers overridden to empty lists/null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Default segment is AMIGOS; verify 'Aún no hay posts de tus amigos'
  2. Tap 'MI GYM' pill
  3. Tap 'PÚBLICO' pill
- **Esperado:** Body swaps to MI GYM empty state then PÚBLICO empty state; feedSegmentProvider state updates to gym then public; active pill is visually highlighted (accent).

### feed-10 — Default feed segment is AMIGOS on first build
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Fresh ProviderContainer.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read feedSegmentProvider without any prior mutation
- **Esperado:** Value equals FeedSegment.amigos.

### feed-11 — Feed header navigates to search and create routes
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FeedScreen mounted inside a GoRouter exposing /feed/search and /feed/create.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the search icon in the header
  2. Verify navigation to /feed/search
  3. Pop back, tap the accent plus button
  4. Verify navigation to /feed/create
- **Esperado:** context.push('/feed/search') and context.push('/feed/create') fire and the respective screens load.

### feed-12 — Tapping a post author navigates to that author's public profile
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AMIGOS feed has >=1 post by authorUid 'u2'; router exposes /feed/profile/:uid.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render the feed with a post by u2
  2. Tap the author (avatar+name) region of the PostCard
- **Esperado:** context.go('/feed/profile/u2') fires and PublicProfileScreen for u2 is shown.

### feed-13 — Create post: PUBLICAR disabled when text is empty or whitespace-only
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** createPostNotifier built with default state (text='').
- **Pasos:**
  1. Inspect canSubmit with text=''
  2. setText('   ') (whitespace only)
  3. Inspect canSubmit again
- **Esperado:** canSubmit is false in both cases; PUBLICAR control renders at opacity 0.4 with null onTap.

### feed-14 — Create post: PUBLICAR enabled with valid trimmed text
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** createPostNotifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. setText('Buen entreno')
  2. Inspect canSubmit
- **Esperado:** canSubmit is true; PUBLICAR renders at full opacity and is tappable.

### feed-15 — Create post: 280 grapheme-cluster boundary enforced (canSubmit)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** kMaxPostChars == 280; createPostNotifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. setText with exactly 280 chars → check canSubmit
  2. setText with 281 chars → check canSubmit
  3. setText with multi-byte emoji string of grapheme length 280 → check canSubmit
- **Esperado:** canSubmit true at exactly 280 (incl. emoji counted as single grapheme clusters via characters.length), false at 281. Boundary is grapheme-based not UTF-16-based.

### feed-16 — Create post: char counter turns danger color when over limit
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** CreatePostScreen rendered; profile available.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Type 281 characters into the text field
  2. Read the _CharCounter text and color
- **Esperado:** Counter shows '281 / 280' in palette.danger color. (Note: counter uses text.length, a known UTF-16 vs grapheme discrepancy — document, do not assert grapheme parity here.)

### feed-17 — Create post: successful submit creates post, resets state, invalidates 3 feeds, pops
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated user u1; profile with displayName/gymId; PostRepository.create stubbed to succeed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. setText('Hola feed')
  2. Call notifier.submit()
  3. Inspect return value and resulting state
  4. Verify create() was called with trimmed text, authorUid=u1, denormalized author fields, selected privacy
  5. Verify myFriendsFeedProvider, feedPublicProvider, myGymFeedProvider were invalidated
- **Esperado:** submit() returns true; state resets to default CreatePostState(); text is trimmed before persistence; all three feed providers invalidated; screen pops after ok.

### feed-18 — Create post: double-tap guard prevents concurrent submit
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PostRepository.create backed by a slow/Completer future.
- **Pasos:**
  1. setText('x')
  2. Call submit() (do not await) — sets isSubmitting=true
  3. While submitting, canSubmit must be false; call submit() again immediately
  4. Complete the slow create
- **Esperado:** Second submit() returns false because canSubmit is false while isSubmitting; create() is invoked exactly once. Header shows the inline spinner during submission.

### feed-19 — Create post: gym privacy with no gym is blocked with helper error
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated user whose profile gymId == null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. setPrivacy(PostPrivacy.gym)
  2. setText('post para el gym')
  3. Call submit()
- **Esperado:** submit() returns false; errorMessage == 'Asociate a un gym para postear acá.'; PostRepository.create is NEVER called (defense-in-depth even though the pill is also disabled).

### feed-20 — Create post: MI GYM privacy pill disabled when user has no gym
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

- **Pasos:**

  2. Call submit()
- **Esperado:** submit() returns false; errorMessage == 'No pudimos publicar tu post. Iniciá sesión.'; create() not called.

### feed-22 — Create post: repository throw surfaces retry error and clears submitting
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true

  1. setText('post')
  2. Call submit()
- **Esperado:** submit() returns false; errorMessage == 'No pudimos publicar tu post. Intentá de nuevo.'; isSubmitting reset to false; state.text preserved so the user can retry.

### feed-23 — Create post: setText clears any prior error message
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true

  2. Call setText('nuevo texto')
- **Esperado:** state.errorMessage becomes null (clearError) while text updates.

  1. Read initial state.privacy
- **Esperado:** Equals PostPrivacy.friends.

### feed-27 — Search: below-min query (0 or 1 char) shows prompt and never hits repo
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true

- **Pasos:**

  2. Read searchUsersProvider('a') → expect const []
  3. Verify repository.searchByDisplayName NOT invoked in either case
- **Esperado:** Both return an empty list immediately without delegating to the repository (2-char gate, defense-in-depth).

### feed-28 — Search: query is trimmed and lowercased before delegating
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** searchUsersProvider with a spy repo capturing the argument.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read searchUsersProvider('  Tincho ')
- **Esperado:** Repository.searchByDisplayName called with 'tincho' (trimmed + lowercased). Caller may pass raw input; provider normalizes.

### feed-29 — Search screen: initial and below-min states show the prompt empty state
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  3. Observe state

### feed-30 — Search screen: 300ms debounce — provider not queried until debounce fires
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** SearchUsersScreen mounted with FakeAsync or pumped time control; searchUsersProvider spy.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Type 'ti' then quickly 'tin' then 'tinc'
  2. Advance time < 300ms between keystrokes
  3. Advance time past 300ms after the last keystroke
- **Esperado:** _activeQuery only updates once, 300ms after the final keystroke; searchUsersProvider queried once with the final value, not per-keystroke.

### feed-31 — Search screen: results render tiles and navigate on tap

### feed-33 — Search screen: loading and error states
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### feed-34 — Search screen: clear (X) button resets query and returns to prompt
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** SearchUsersScreen with non-empty input and results shown.
- **Pasos:**

  2. Tap the suffix X icon

### feed-35 — Friendship.sortedDocId is order-independent and deterministic
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Compute sortedDocId('userB','userA')
  2. Compute sortedDocId('userA','userB')
- **Esperado:** Both equal 'userA_userB' (min_max lexicographic). Guarantees one doc per pair regardless of argument order.

### feed-36 — FriendshipRepository.request is idempotent for an existing pair
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore; a friendship doc already exists for sortedDocId(u1,u2).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call request('u1','u2') a second time
- **Esperado:** Returns the existing Friendship without writing a new/overwriting doc; no duplicate created; status unchanged.

### feed-37 — FriendshipRepository.request creates pending doc with sorted uidA/uidB and members
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore, no prior doc for the pair.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call request('u2','u1') (intentionally reversed)
- **Esperado:** Doc id == 'u1_u2'; uidA='u1', uidB='u2'; status=pending; requesterId='u2'; members=['u1','u2']; createdAt is UTC.

### feed-38 — FriendshipRepository.accept blocks self-accept by requester
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pending friendship where requesterId == 'u1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call accept(friendshipId, 'u1')
- **Esperado:** Throws StateError ('Requester cannot self-accept ...'); status remains pending; no counter side-effect.

### feed-39 — FriendshipRepository.accept on missing doc throws StateError
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** No doc with id 'missing'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call accept('missing','u2')
- **Esperado:** Throws StateError ('Friendship missing not found').

### feed-40 — FriendshipRepository.accept sets accepted and increments followingCount (best-effort)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pending friendship requesterId='u1'; userPublicProfiles/u2 exists with followingCount=3; publicProfileRepository injected.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call accept(id, 'u2')
- **Esperado:** status → accepted; userPublicProfiles/u2.followingCount incremented to 4. If the profile write throws, accept still succeeds (error swallowed/logged).

### feed-41 — FriendshipRepository.delete decrements followingCount with clamp at zero
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Accepted friendship; userPublicProfiles/u2.followingCount=0; publicProfileRepository injected.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call delete(id, 'u2')
- **Esperado:** Friendship doc removed; followingCount decrement clamped to 0 (never negative); if profile write fails, delete still completes (error swallowed/logged).

### feed-42 — acceptedFriendsOf returns the OTHER member for each accepted friendship
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** u1 has accepted friendships with u2 and u3, and one pending with u4.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call acceptedFriendsOf('u1')
- **Esperado:** Returns ['u2','u3'] (pending u4 excluded); each entry is the non-self member; empty members produce no entry.

### feed-43 — watchPendingRequestsFor excludes requests sent BY the user (inbox = received only)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pending docs: one where u1 is requester (sent), one where u2 is requester targeting u1 (received).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to watchPendingRequestsFor('u1')
  2. Read first emission
- **Esperado:** Emits only the request where requesterId != u1 (the received one); the request u1 sent is excluded. Stream re-emits on doc changes.

### feed-44 — Feed module is role-agnostic (athlete and trainer see identical surfaces)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Two seeded accounts: athlete and trainer (coach).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render FeedScreen / CreatePostScreen / SearchUsersScreen / PublicProfileScreen once with an athlete profile (role=athlete) and once with a trainer profile (role=trainer)
- **Esperado:** Rendered widget tree, available actions, privacy options, and provider behavior are identical for both roles. INVARIANT: there is no role branching anywhere in lib/features/feed/ — this test guards against accidental role gating being introduced.

### feed-45 — Follow button: null friendship renders SEGUIR and sends a request
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PublicProfileFollowButton with friendship=null, viewerUid=u1, targetUid=u2; friendshipRepository spy.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render the button
  2. Verify label SEGUIR (mint filled)
  3. Tap it
- **Esperado:** repo.request('u1','u2') called once. Stream providers self-update (no manual invalidation of friendship streams); myFriendsFeedProvider NOT invalidated for SEGUIR (only a pending request, accepted list unchanged).

### feed-46 — Follow button: accepted friendship renders SIGUIENDO and opens unfriend sheet

  3. Tap it

### feed-48 — Follow button: pending received renders ACEPTAR and accepts + invalidates AMIGOS feed
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  2. Verify label ACEPTAR (mint filled)
  3. Tap it
- **Esperado:** repo.accept(friendship.id, 'u1') called; myFriendsFeedProvider is explicitly invalidated (ADR-FPS-006) so Feed AMIGOS refreshes; friendship stream self-updates.

### feed-49 — Unfriend sheet: ELIMINAR confirms delete and invalidates AMIGOS; CANCELAR is no-op
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Unfriend sheet shown for an accepted friendship; repo spy.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Case A: tap ELIMINAR → expect onConfirm → repo.delete(id, viewerUid) and myFriendsFeedProvider invalidated; sheet pops
  2. Case B: reopen, tap CANCELAR → sheet pops, onConfirm NOT fired, repo.delete NOT called
- **Esperado:** ELIMINAR deletes and refreshes AMIGOS (delete errors are swallowed but invalidation still runs); CANCELAR dismisses without any mutation.

### feed-50 — Inbox tile: ACEPTAR uses dispose-safe container invalidate and disables buttons while busy
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FriendRequestInboxTile for a pending request; repo spy with a slow accept.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap ACEPTAR
  2. While the accept future is pending, attempt to tap ACEPTAR and RECHAZAR again
  3. Complete the accept
- **Esperado:** _busy guard prevents re-entry (second taps no-op); repo.accept called once; invalidation of myFriendsFeedProvider goes through the root ProviderScope container (survives tile disposal when the stream prunes the row), keeping Feed AMIGOS fresh.

### feed-51 — Inbox tile: RECHAZAR deletes the request and does NOT touch AMIGOS feed
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FriendRequestInboxTile for a pending request; repo spy.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap RECHAZAR
- **Esperado:** repo.delete(friendship.id, viewerUid) called; myFriendsFeedProvider NOT invalidated (rejection never created a friendship); button errors are swallowed (row stays if stream doesn't prune).

### feed-61 — PostCard meta: gym + relative time formatting and null-gym fallback

- **Esperado:** Relative-time buckets render as specified; meta is '<GYM uppercased> · <time>' when gym present, time-only when gymId null/empty.
