### feed-66 — Post.fromJson tolerates missing authorDisplayName (legacy docs default to 'Anónimo')
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Deserialize a post JSON map that omits the authorDisplayName key (with valid id, authorUid, text, privacy, createdAt, nullable author fields)
- **Esperado:** Post.authorDisplayName defaults to 'Anónimo' (json_serializable @Default applied); other fields deserialize correctly.

### feed-67 — PostPrivacy/FriendshipStatus wire mapping rejects unknown values
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. PostPrivacyX.fromJson('friends'/'gym'/'public') → expect enums
  2. PostPrivacyX.fromJson('secret') → expect throw
  3. FriendshipStatusX.fromJson('pending'/'accepted') → enums; fromJson('blocked') → throw
  4. Round-trip toJson() for each enum value
- **Esperado:** Valid wire values map both directions; unknown wire values throw ArgumentError. Round-trips are stable.

### feed-68 — gymNameFromId mapping, sentinel handling, and uppercase fallback
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. gymNameFromId('smart-fit-palermo') → 'SMART FIT'
  2. gymNameFromId(null) / '' / kNoGymId → ''
  3. gymNameFromId('unknown-gym-x') → 'UNKNOWN-GYM-X'
- **Esperado:** Known ids map to display names; null/empty/sentinel return '' (caller hides subtitle); unknown ids return id.toUpperCase() as a visible stale-catalog signal.

### feed-69 — feedForFriends chunks the whereIn query in batches of 10 and re-sorts merged results
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore seeded with friends-privacy posts authored by 11+ distinct UIDs with interleaved createdAt.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call feedForFriends with 11 friend UIDs
- **Esperado:** Issues 2 chunked queries (<=10 each), aggregates results, and the final list is globally newest-first (client re-sort across chunk boundaries). Empty input returns const [] without querying.

### feed-70 — friendUidsKey is order-independent and value-equal (cache stability)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. friendUidsKey(['u3','u1','u2']) and friendUidsKey(['u1','u2','u3'])
  2. Compare strings
  3. Round-trip through feedForFriendsProvider key split
- **Esperado:** Both produce 'u1 u2 u3' (sorted, space-joined); equal Strings → feedForFriendsProvider family reuses cache across acceptedFriends stream re-emissions instead of re-querying; empty list → '' which the provider maps to const <String>[].

### feed-71 — feedForGym excludes posts with null authorGymId and filters by gym + privacy
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore with gym-privacy posts: some with matching gymId, one with null authorGymId, one with a different gym.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call feedForGym('smart-fit-palermo')
- **Esperado:** Returns only gym-privacy posts whose authorGymId == 'smart-fit-palermo', newest-first; null-gym and other-gym posts excluded.

### feed-72 — PostRepository.create denormalizes authorGymId from the user doc when not provided
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore; users/u1 doc has gymId='smart-fit-palermo'; input Post has authorGymId=null and id=''.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call create(inputPost)
- **Esperado:** Persisted post gets a generated id and authorGymId resolved from users/u1.gymId; if input already carries an explicit authorGymId it is preserved (not overwritten).

### feed-73 — Check-in dialog shows once per session when not yet checked in today
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated uid; todayCheckInProvider resolves null (not checked in); _checkInDialogShownThisSessionProvider initially false.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Mount FeedScreen and pump past the first frame / post-frame callback
  2. Verify CheckInDialog appears
  3. Dismiss it, rebuild FeedScreen (simulate tab switch)
- **Esperado:** Dialog shows exactly once; the session flag is set before awaiting showDialog (race guard) so it does not reappear on remount within the same process.

### feed-74 — Check-in dialog suppressed when already checked in or unauthenticated
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Case A: todayCheckInProvider resolves a non-null check-in. Case B: currentUidProvider null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Case A: mount FeedScreen, pump past first frame
  2. Case B: mount FeedScreen unauthenticated, pump
- **Esperado:** No CheckInDialog appears in either case (already-checked-in guard and auth guard).

### feed-75 — PublicProfileStatsRow: null counters render as 0 and k-format applies
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render with all nulls → expect '0' in WORKOUTS/RACHA/SEGUIDORES/SIGUIENDO
  2. Render with followersCount=1500 → expect k-formatted value; racha=7 → raw '7'
- **Esperado:** Null → '0'; WORKOUTS/SEGUIDORES/SIGUIENDO use kFormat (compact), RACHA uses raw integer and accent color.

# Módulo: gyms

_The gyms module is a data/catalog module (domain Gym + GymSource, GymRepository, and Riverpod providers) with NO presentation layer of its own; gym UI lives in consumer features (the _GymPickerSheet in profile_edit_trainer_screen and the gym-name label in trainers_list_screen). Catalog: ~20 docs, seeded via scripts/seed_gyms.js. Repo exposes listAll/getById/getByIds (getByIds chunked at 30 for Firestore whereIn cap) and a resilient _fromDoc that skips malformed docs. Notable gap: createSelfService() is referenced in the repo doc-comment and GymSource.selfService exists, but the method is NOT implemented — there is no client-side create/update/delete path (update/delete are intentionally denied client-side; admin/Cloud Function only). Cases below extend (not duplicate) the existing test/features/gyms/data/gym_repository_test.dart, which already covers listAll happy/empty/id-injection/malformed-skip, getById missing/found, and getByIds empty/partial._

### gyms-01 — listAll returns the full catalog mapped to Gym domain objects
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with multiple valid gym docs (mix of seed and self-service sources).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed gyms/gym-1 and gyms/gym-2 with valid fields (name, lat, lng, geohash, source, createdAt).
  2. Call GymRepository.listAll().
- **Esperado:** Returns a List<Gym> with one entry per doc; ids, names, lat/lng, source, createdAt round-trip correctly; address null stays null.

### gyms-02 — listAll parses a self-service gym preserving source and createdBy
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** One gym doc with source 'self-service' and createdBy set to a trainer uid.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed gyms/gym-ss with source 'self-service', createdBy 'trainer-uid-1'.
  2. Call listAll().
- **Esperado:** Resulting Gym has source GymSource.selfService and createdBy 'trainer-uid-1' (not coerced to seed/null).

### gyms-03 — listAll skips a doc missing the required geohash field
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog with one valid doc and one doc lacking the required 'geohash' string.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a valid gym and a second doc with geohash field omitted (or set to null).
  2. Call listAll().
- **Esperado:** Only the valid gym is returned; the geohash-less doc is skipped via _fromDoc try/catch (not an exception aborting the whole read).

### gyms-04 — listAll skips a doc with an unknown/invalid source value
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog with one valid doc and one doc whose 'source' is an unrecognized string (e.g. 'partner').
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a valid gym and a doc with source 'partner' (not in enum map).
  2. Call listAll().
- **Esperado:** $enumDecode throws for the bad doc; it is caught and skipped; the valid gym is still returned.

### gyms-05 — listAll skips a doc with missing required name
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog with one valid doc and one doc with 'name' omitted (null cast to String fails).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a valid gym and a doc without a name field.
  2. Call listAll().
- **Esperado:** The nameless doc is skipped; the valid gym is returned; no exception propagates.

### gyms-06 — listAll skips a doc with malformed createdAt (not a Timestamp)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog with one valid doc and one doc whose 'createdAt' is a String/int instead of a Firestore Timestamp.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a valid gym and a doc with createdAt set to '2026-01-01' (String).
  2. Call listAll().
- **Esperado:** TimestampConverter cast fails for the bad doc; it is skipped; the valid gym is returned.

### gyms-07 — listAll parses integer lat/lng via num.toDouble()
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** A gym doc whose lat/lng are stored as integers (0) rather than doubles.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed gyms/gym-int with lat 0 and lng 0 stored as int.
  2. Call listAll().
- **Esperado:** Gym.lat and Gym.lng are returned as 0.0 doubles (num.toDouble coercion), doc is not skipped.

### gyms-08 — getById returns null when the document does not exist
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty or unrelated gyms collection.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call getById('does-not-exist').
- **Esperado:** Returns null (no throw); covered/aligned with existing repo test.

### gyms-09 — getById returns null for an existing-but-malformed doc instead of throwing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** A gym doc that exists but has lat stored as a String.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed gyms/broken with lat 'no-soy-double'.
  2. Call getById('broken').
- **Esperado:** _fromDoc catches the parse error and returns null (single-doc resilience parity with listAll).

### gyms-10 — getByIds with empty input returns empty list without any Firestore I/O
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Any catalog state.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call getByIds(const []).
- **Esperado:** Returns const [] immediately, short-circuiting before issuing a whereIn query.

### gyms-11 — getByIds chunks queries when more than 30 ids are requested
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog seeded with 31+ gym docs whose ids are all requested.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed 31 gyms (gym-0..gym-30).
  2. Call getByIds with all 31 ids.
- **Esperado:** All 31 gyms are returned; the >30 case is split across at least 2 whereIn chunks (Firestore 30-value cap respected) with no error.

### gyms-12 — getByIds at exactly 30 ids stays in a single chunk
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog seeded with exactly 30 gym docs.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed 30 gyms.
  2. Call getByIds with the 30 ids.
- **Esperado:** All 30 gyms returned; boundary at chunkSize handled correctly (sublist end index does not overflow).

### gyms-13 — getByIds ignores ids that do not exist and dedupes nothing extra
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog with found-1 and found-2 present.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed found-1 and found-2.
  2. Call getByIds(['found-1','missing','found-2']).
- **Esperado:** Returns only found-1 and found-2; missing id silently dropped (aligned with existing repo test).

### gyms-14 — getByIds skips a malformed doc within a chunk but returns the rest
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** A chunk containing one valid and one malformed (bad lat) doc.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed ok-1 (valid) and broken (lat as String).
  2. Call getByIds(['ok-1','broken']).
- **Esperado:** Returns only ok-1; broken is skipped via whereType<Gym>() filtering of the null from _fromDoc.

### gyms-15 — gymSourceFromString maps wire values case-insensitively and trims
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure function).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call gymSourceFromString('seed'), ('self-service'), (' SELF-SERVICE '), ('Seed').
- **Esperado:** Returns GymSource.seed, GymSource.selfService, GymSource.selfService, GymSource.seed respectively (trim + toLowerCase applied).

### gyms-16 — gymSourceFromString returns null for null, empty, or unknown values
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure function).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call gymSourceFromString(null), (''), ('partner').
- **Esperado:** All three return null (no enum and no throw).

### gyms-17 — GymSource.toWire produces the exact Firestore wire strings
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure function).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call GymSource.seed.toWire() and GymSource.selfService.toWire().
- **Esperado:** Returns 'seed' and 'self-service' exactly (matches @JsonValue and seed script contract).

### gyms-18 — Gym.fromJson/toJson round-trip preserves all fields including nullable address & createdBy
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a Gym JSON map with address and createdBy null plus all required fields.
  2. Decode with Gym.fromJson then re-encode with toJson.
- **Esperado:** Required fields preserved; null address and null createdBy survive the round-trip; source serializes back to its wire string.

### gyms-19 — gymsProvider exposes loading then data for the catalog
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with firestoreProvider overridden to a FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with gyms.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read gymsProvider — assert initial AsyncLoading.
  2. Await gymsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Provider transitions from loading to AsyncData(List<Gym>) matching the seeded catalog.

### gyms-20 — gymsProvider surfaces an error state when the read fails
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** firestoreProvider overridden with a fake/repo override whose listAll throws.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override gymRepositoryProvider with a repo that throws on listAll.
  2. Await gymsProvider and capture the AsyncValue.
- **Esperado:** gymsProvider resolves to AsyncError, allowing consumers to render an error UI instead of crashing.

### gyms-21 — gymByIdProvider family returns the matching gym and null for missing id
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog seeded with gym-x via overridden firestoreProvider.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Await gymByIdProvider('gym-x').future.
  2. Await gymByIdProvider('nope').future.
- **Esperado:** First returns the Gym for gym-x; second returns null; the two family instances are cached independently.

### gyms-22 — Gym picker sheet lists all available gyms sorted by name on open
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer account; catalog with several gyms; no gym yet added to the trainer's locations.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open trainer profile edit, tap Add gym to invoke _addGym.
  2. Observe the _GymPickerSheet list before typing.
- **Esperado:** All catalog gyms render as ListTiles ordered alphabetically by name (sort in _addGym); each shows name and address subtitle (address tile omitted when null).

### gyms-23 — Gym picker excludes gyms already added to the trainer's locations
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer already has one gym location (gymId = gym-1); catalog contains gym-1, gym-2.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the gym picker via _addGym.
- **Esperado:** gym-1 is filtered out (dedup via selectedIds); only gym-2 appears as selectable.

### gyms-24 — Gym picker search filters by name (case-insensitive, trimmed)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog includes 'Megatlon Belgrano' and 'SmartFit Caballito'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open picker, type '  MEGATLON  ' in the search field.
- **Esperado:** Only 'Megatlon Belgrano' remains (lowercase + trim applied to query, contains match on name).

### gyms-25 — Gym picker search also matches on address
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** A gym with name not matching the query but address containing 'Caballito'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open picker, type 'caballito'.
- **Esperado:** Gyms whose address contains the query are included even when the name does not match.

### gyms-26 — Gym picker shows 'Sin resultados.' when a search matches nothing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Catalog has gyms available but none match the query.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open picker (with available gyms), type 'zzz-nomatch'.
- **Esperado:** List is empty and the centered text reads 'Sin resultados.' (not the no-gyms-left copy).

### gyms-27 — Gym picker shows the no-gyms-left message when nothing is available
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer has already added every catalog gym, so the available list is empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the gym picker via _addGym with an empty available list and no query typed.
- **Esperado:** Empty state renders 'No quedan gimnasios disponibles para sumar.' (distinct from the 'Sin resultados.' search-empty copy).

### gyms-28 — Selecting a gym in the picker adds a gym-type TrainerLocation with copied coordinates
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile edit open; picker showing at least one gym.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open picker, tap a gym tile.
  2. Inspect the trainer's _locations after the sheet closes.
- **Esperado:** A TrainerLocation is appended with id 'gym-{picked.id}', type gym, gymId = picked.id, and lat/lng/geohash copied from the picked gym; _error reset to null.

### gyms-29 — Dismissing the picker without selecting leaves locations unchanged
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile edit open with the picker shown.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the picker, then dismiss it (back/scrim) without tapping a gym.
- **Esperado:** showModalBottomSheet returns null, _addGym early-returns, and no TrainerLocation is added.

### gyms-30 — Trainers-list label uses the gym name when the gym is in cache
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** gymsProvider resolved with a gym whose id matches the nearest gym-type TrainerLocation.gymId.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render trainers list with a trainer whose nearest location is a gym present in gymsById.
  2. Read the rendered locationLabel.
- **Esperado:** _labelFor returns the gym's name (e.g. 'Megatlon Belgrano') for the tile.

### gyms-31 — Trainers-list label falls back to 'Gimnasio' on a gym cache miss
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Nearest TrainerLocation is type gym with a gymId NOT present in gymsById (e.g. catalog still loading or gym deleted).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render trainers list where gymsById lacks the location's gymId.
  2. Read the locationLabel.
- **Esperado:** _labelFor returns the literal 'Gimnasio' fallback instead of null or a crash.

### gyms-32 — Trainers-list label uses customLabel for non-gym locations and null when no nearest
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** A trainer with a custom-type nearest location, and another with no nearest location.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call _labelFor with a custom TrainerLocation (customLabel set).
  2. Call _labelFor with nearest == null.
- **Esperado:** First returns the customLabel; second returns null (no label shown).

### gyms-33 — Gym name label still renders while gymsProvider is loading (graceful default)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** gymsProvider in AsyncLoading; trainer has a gym-type nearest location.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render trainers list while gymsAsync.valueOrNull is null (loading).
  2. Observe the tile label.
- **Esperado:** gymsById is empty during loading, so the label falls back to 'Gimnasio' without blocking or erroring the list.

### gyms-34 — Read access is auth-gated by Firestore rules (athlete and trainer can read catalog)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator with deployed firestore.rules; seeded athlete and coach accounts; seeded gyms collection.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in as the athlete, read gyms collection.
  2. Sign in as the trainer, read gyms collection.
  3. Attempt an unauthenticated read.
- **Esperado:** Both authenticated roles can read the catalog; the unauthenticated read is denied per the 'read: authenticated user' rule.

### gyms-35 — Client-side update and delete of a gym doc are denied by rules
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator with deployed rules; trainer signed in; an existing gyms/{id} doc.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As the trainer, attempt to update a field on an existing gym doc.
  2. As the trainer, attempt to delete a gym doc.
- **Esperado:** Both operations are rejected (PERMISSION_DENIED); module exposes no update/delete method and rules block client mutations (admin/Cloud Function only).

### gyms-36 — Self-service gym creation is gated to trainers with enforced source/createdBy
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator with deployed rules; an athlete account and a trainer account.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As the athlete, attempt to create a gyms doc -> expect denial.
  2. As the trainer, attempt to create a gyms doc with source 'self-service' and createdBy == own uid and all required fields.
  3. As the trainer, attempt to create with source 'seed' or createdBy != own uid -> expect denial.
- **Esperado:** Only trainers can create, only with source 'self-service' and createdBy equal to their uid; athlete creates and spoofed source/createdBy are denied. NOTE: no client createSelfService() method is implemented yet, so this is rules-level coverage of a not-yet-wired UI path.

### gyms-37 — listAll returns empty list for an empty catalog without error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty gyms collection.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call listAll() against an empty collection.
- **Esperado:** Returns an empty list (not null, no throw); aligned with existing repo test, kept as the empty-state baseline for async surfaces.

# Módulo: home

_Test-case catalog for lib/features/home/. The module is a role-aware HomeScreen that routes trainers to TrainerDashboardTab and everyone else (athlete, plus loading/error/null role) to the athlete home, always stacking an invisible PermissionGate. The athlete home shows a profile header (with loading skeleton + error fallback), the hardcoded "Empezar Entrenamiento" card, the data-wired "Esta Semana" card (loading/error/empty/loaded), and a resume-session listener that pops ResumeSessionModal when an active session exists. Existing tests under test/features/home/ already cover the bulk of happy paths and many edge cases (header greeting/initials/avatar, CTA button states, EstaSemanaCard loading/error/empty/loaded + navigation, isoWeekNumber boundaries, resume-modal presence). The cases below target regression-prone gaps not yet covered: role-routing invariants (trainer vs athlete vs loading-defaults-to-athlete vs error), PermissionGate gating conditions and once-per-session behavior, the resume-modal discard path (finish + elapsed-min clamp + invalidation), day-strip color/state logic, streak boundary values, and trainer dashboard derivations (resumen counts, próximas sesiones filtering/sorting, pending-request badge). P0 = role routing, permission gating, data-integrity in the discard/finish path, and the always-present PermissionGate. Automatable flags are false only for true native interactions (OS notification prompt result, real auth)._

### home-01 — Trainer role renders TrainerDashboardTab, not athlete home
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider overridden with a UserProfile whose role == UserRole.trainer.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen inside ProviderScope with userProfileProvider returning a trainer profile.
  2. pump 50ms to resolve the role select.
  3. Inspect the widget tree.
- **Esperado:** TrainerDashboardTab is found exactly once; _AthleteHome widgets (EmpezarEntrenamientoCard, EstaSemanaCard) are NOT present.

### home-02 — Athlete role renders athlete home, not trainer dashboard
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider overridden with role == UserRole.athlete.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with an athlete profile override.
  2. pump 50ms.
  3. Inspect the tree.
- **Esperado:** EmpezarEntrenamientoCard and EstaSemanaCard each found once; TrainerDashboardTab is NOT present.

### home-03 — Loading role defaults to athlete home (no stall, no trainer view)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider overridden with a never-completing stream so role stays AsyncLoading.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with an empty/never-emitting userProfileProvider stream.
  2. Single pump (do not settle).
  3. Inspect the tree.
- **Esperado:** Athlete home renders (EmpezarEntrenamientoCard + EstaSemanaCard present) while role is loading; TrainerDashboardTab absent. Confirms the documented default-to-athlete invariant for the 99% common case.

### home-04 — Error role falls back to athlete home, no FlutterError
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider overridden to emit an error.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with userProfileProvider erroring.
  2. pump 50ms.
  3. Inspect tree and check for thrown exceptions.
- **Esperado:** Athlete home renders (role==null branch), no uncaught FlutterError, TrainerDashboardTab absent.

### home-05 — PermissionGate is always mounted in HomeScreen regardless of role
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider overridden with any value (athlete and trainer variants).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with an athlete profile; assert PermissionGate is present.
  2. Re-pump with a trainer profile; assert PermissionGate is present.
  3. Confirm it occupies zero layout (renders SizedBox.shrink).
- **Esperado:** PermissionGate is found in both athlete and trainer trees and contributes no visible layout (size zero).

### home-06 — PermissionGate requests permission once when displayName is set
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider returns a profile with non-null displayName; permissionGateAttemptedProvider starts false; fcmServiceProvider overridden with a spy/fake returning authorized.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen (or PermissionGate directly) with the profile + fake fcm.
  2. pumpAndSettle so the post-frame callback fires.
  3. Inspect the fake fcm requestPermission call count and permissionGateAttemptedProvider state.
- **Esperado:** requestPermission is called exactly once and permissionGateAttemptedProvider becomes true.

### home-07 — PermissionGate does NOT request when displayName is null (setup incomplete)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider returns a profile with displayName == null (or null profile); fake fcmServiceProvider.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate with the null-displayName profile.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
  3. Inspect fake fcm call count.
- **Esperado:** requestPermission is never called; permissionGateAttemptedProvider stays false.

### home-08 — PermissionGate does not re-fire on rebuild within same session
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** profile with displayName set; permissionGateAttemptedProvider already true (simulating a prior attempt this session); fake fcm.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override permissionGateAttemptedProvider to true.
  2. Pump PermissionGate with a complete profile.
  3. pumpAndSettle.
  4. Trigger a rebuild (e.g. invalidate/rebuild parent).
  5. Inspect fake fcm call count.
- **Esperado:** requestPermission is NOT called because attempted flag is already true (once-per-app-session guard).

### home-09 — PermissionGate swallows denial / errors gracefully (no SnackBar, no nav)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** profile with displayName set; fake fcmServiceProvider whose requestPermission throws or returns denied.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with the profile and a throwing/denied fake fcm.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
  3. Inspect for SnackBars, navigation, and thrown exceptions.
- **Esperado:** No exception propagates; no SnackBar shown; no navigation; fcm.init is not called on denial. Gate fails silently per REQ-PN-PERM-002.

### home-10 — OS notification permission prompt appears on first home load (real device)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Fresh install, athlete logged in with completed profile, notifications not yet granted, real iOS device.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in as the seeded athlete with a displayName.
  2. Land on /home for the first time this session.
  3. Observe the native iOS notification permission dialog.
- **Esperado:** The native permission dialog appears exactly once; granting registers the FCM token (fcm.init runs), denying is silent. Subsequent home visits in the same session do not re-prompt.

### home-11 — Active session present -> ResumeSessionModal shown on home open
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** athlete profile; activeSessionForUidProvider overridden to return a non-null (session, setLogs) record.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with athlete profile + non-null activeSessionForUidProvider.
  2. pumpAndSettle so the post-frame callback fires the dialog.
  3. Look for the modal.
- **Esperado:** ResumeSessionModal appears (e.g. 'Entrenamiento en curso' text visible).

### home-12 — No active session -> no resume modal, normal home
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** athlete profile; activeSessionForUidProvider overridden to return null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with athlete profile + null activeSessionForUidProvider.
  2. pumpAndSettle.
  3. Inspect tree.
- **Esperado:** No ResumeSessionModal; EmpezarEntrenamientoCard and EstaSemanaCard present.

### home-13 — Active session loading/error -> home renders without modal
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** athlete profile; activeSessionForUidProvider overridden once with a never-completing future, once with an error future.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with a pending activeSessionForUidProvider; pump 50ms; assert no modal and HomeHeader present.
  2. Re-run with activeSessionForUidProvider erroring; pumpAndSettle; assert no modal and HomeHeader present.
- **Esperado:** In both loading and error states no modal is shown and the home body renders normally.

### home-14 — Resume modal Continuar navigates to resume route
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** athlete profile; activeSessionForUidProvider returns a session with id 'stub-session-001'; GoRouter with a /workout/session/resume/:id route.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen wired to a GoRouter capturing pushes.
  2. pumpAndSettle so modal shows.
  3. Tap the modal's Continue action.
  4. pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** context.push('/workout/session/resume/stub-session-001') is invoked and the modal is popped.

### home-15 — Resume modal Descartar finishes session and invalidates provider
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** athlete profile; activeSessionForUidProvider returns a session + setLogs; sessionRepositoryProvider overridden with a spy/fake repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with the active-session override and fake repo.
  2. pumpAndSettle so modal shows.
  3. Tap the Discard action.
  4. pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** repo.finish is called once with uid==session.uid, sessionId==session.id, a non-null finishedAt, totalVolumeKg equal to sum(reps*weightKg) of the setLogs, and durationMin >= 1; the modal pops and activeSessionForUidProvider is invalidated.

### home-16 — Discard volume sum uses reps*weightKg across all set logs
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** activeSessionForUidProvider returns setLogs with known reps/weight, e.g. [(10,50),(8,60)] => 980; spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with the crafted setLogs.
  2. pumpAndSettle, open modal, tap Discard.
  3. Capture the totalVolumeKg argument passed to repo.finish.
- **Esperado:** totalVolumeKg == 980.0 (10*50 + 8*60); empty setLogs list yields 0.0.

### home-17 — Elapsed minutes clamps to >=1 for a just-started session
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** activeSessionForUidProvider returns a session whose startedAt == DateTime.now() (0 elapsed seconds); spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen with startedAt set to now.
  2. pumpAndSettle, open modal, tap Discard.
  3. Capture durationMin passed to repo.finish.
- **Esperado:** durationMin == 1 (the <=0 seconds branch clamps to 1), never 0 or negative.

### home-18 — Resume modal is non-dismissible by barrier tap

### home-34 — EstaSemanaCard loaded state renders streak, SEMANA and MES counts
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** weeklyInsightsProvider returns streak 5, sessionsCount 3, monthSessionsCount 12.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump card with the loaded insights.
  2. pump + 50ms.
  3. Inspect streak number and period cards.
- **Esperado:** Streak '5' rendered, 'DÍAS' label present, SEMANA count 3 and MES count 12 rendered.

### home-35 — Streak subtext switches on trained-today flag
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true

(Note: assertion of today depends on the run date — prefer asserting the trained vs untrained color contrast and that exactly one bar may carry the today outline.)

### home-40 — isoWeekNumber handles year-boundary edge cases
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure function).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call isoWeekNumber for 2027-01-01 (Fri), 2021-01-01 (Fri), 2023-01-01 (Sun), 2024-12-30 (Mon), 2026-06-16.
  2. Assert results.
- **Esperado:** 2027-01-01 -> 53, 2021-01-01 -> 53, 2023-01-01 -> 52, 2024-12-30 -> 1, 2026-06-16 -> 25; result always in 1..53, never 0.

### home-41 — isoWeeksInYear returns 53 for long years and 52 otherwise

- **Pasos:**

- **Esperado:** 2020 -> 53, 2026 -> 53, 2022 -> 52, 2023 -> 52.

### home-44 — Resumen del día counts pending/done/cancelled from today's appointments

  2. pumpAndSettle.
  3. Read the three stat columns.
- **Esperado:** Pending = count of today's confirmed appts with startsAt after now; Completadas = today's confirmed appts not after now; Canceladas = today's cancelled appts. Appointments on other local days are excluded.

### home-49 — Entrenaron hoy list states (loading/error/empty/data)

# Módulo: insights

_Test-case catalog for lib/features/insights/. The module is a single athlete-facing screen (InsightsScreen, reached via context.push('/home/insights') from the Home "Esta Semana" card) backed by weeklyInsightsProvider (FutureProvider.autoDispose) which computes weekly aggregates client-side from Session + SetLog + exercise catalog + the most-recent session's Routine. Domain: MuscleGroupDisplay (6 display groups + granular→display mapping) and the immutable WeeklyInsights DTO. Widget: BodySilhouettePlaceholder (asset render with icon fallback). Existing tests (SCENARIO-298..304, 401..407) already cover provider aggregation, streak, monthSessionsCount, custom-exercise fallback, and the domain DTO/mapping; this catalog adds the MISSING coverage — screen widget tests (loading/error/empty/data, week strip, muscles card, volume-bar business rules, navigation), boundary/edge cases on the provider, and the silhouette fallback. Note: the module is role-agnostic (no athlete/trainer gate) and data is purely current-uid-centric, so role behavior cases verify the screen behaves identically and is driven only by the signed-in uid's data. KEY caveat surfaced: the provider reads DateTime.now() directly (no clock injection), so any case asserting week-relative bucketing must build seed data relative to now() — flagged in the relevant cases._

### insights-01 — Screen shows loading spinner while weeklyInsightsProvider resolves
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InsightsScreen pumped with weeklyInsightsProvider overridden by a Future that never completes (or a Completer not yet completed).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a ProviderScope overriding weeklyInsightsProvider to return a pending Future.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen inside a MaterialApp + Scaffold (the route normally supplies the Scaffold via the shell).
  3. Do not settle the future.
- **Esperado:** A CircularProgressIndicator is shown in the body (colored palette.accent). The header 'INSIGHTS' is visible. No empty-state, error, or data cards are rendered.

### insights-02 — Screen shows error message when provider throws
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** weeklyInsightsProvider overridden to throw / return a Future.error.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override weeklyInsightsProvider with (ref) async => throw Exception('boom').
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** The centered error copy 'No pudimos cargar tus insights.' is displayed. Header 'INSIGHTS' still visible. No spinner, no cards, no empty state.

### insights-03 — Screen shows empty state when insights is null
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** weeklyInsightsProvider overridden to return null (simulates uid == null path).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override weeklyInsightsProvider with (ref) async => null.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** _EmptyState renders: TreinoIcon.chartBar icon plus copy 'Empezá a entrenar para ver tus insights.'. No week-strip / muscles / volume cards. No VOLVER button.

### insights-04 — Screen shows empty state when sessionsCount is 0
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** weeklyInsightsProvider returns a non-null WeeklyInsights with sessionsCount == 0 (e.g. all-empty stub).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a WeeklyInsights stub with sessionsCount: 0, empty maps, daysTrained all false.
  2. Override the provider to return it; pump InsightsScreen and settle.
- **Esperado:** Same _EmptyState as insights-03 is shown (sessionsCount==0 is treated as empty even though the DTO is non-null). Data cards are NOT rendered.

### insights-05 — Data state renders all three cards plus VOLVER when sessionsCount > 0
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns a WeeklyInsights with sessionsCount >= 1, non-empty setsByGroup and targetByGroup.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a stub: sessionsCount 3, setsByGroup {pecho:8}, targetByGroup {pecho:12}, daysTrained with at least one true.
  2. Override the provider; pump InsightsScreen and settle.
- **Esperado:** Week-strip card (with the SEMANA range and 'N / 5' counter), 'MÚSCULOS DE LA SEMANA' card, 'VOLUMEN POR GRUPO' card, and the 'VOLVER' OutlinedButton are all present. Empty state and error not shown.

### insights-06 — Week-strip counter renders sessionsCount over plannedSessionsCount
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns WeeklyInsights with sessionsCount: 4, plannedSessionsCount: 5.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build stub with sessionsCount 4, plannedSessionsCount 5, at least one set so cards render.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
- **Esperado:** The week-strip header shows the text '4 / 5' in accent color.

### insights-07 — Week-strip renders 7 day chips with trained day showing a check
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns daysTrained = [true,false,false,false,false,false,false] (Monday trained).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build stub with that daysTrained and sessionsCount 1, plus a set so cards render.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Inspect the day-chip row.
- **Esperado:** Exactly 7 _DayChip slots render under labels L M M J V S D. The trained (index 0) chip shows TreinoIcon.checkCircleFill in an accent-filled circle; the other 6 show their day-of-month number in an outlined circle.

### insights-08 — Week-strip highlights today's chip when today is not trained
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** daysTrained all false; today (DateTime.now weekday) falls within Mon..Sun of the rendered week. NOTE: _DayChip computes todayIndex from DateTime.now() at build time — not injectable.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build stub with daysTrained all false but sessionsCount 1 (so cards render) and a set.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Locate the chip at index == (DateTime.now().weekday - DateTime.monday).
- **Esperado:** Today's chip uses the accent outline + accent-colored day number (the isToday branch); non-today untrained chips use the muted border + muted number. Only one chip is in the today style.

### insights-09 — Week-strip date range label is formatted as 'SEMANA · D MMM – D MMM'
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns weekStart = 2026-05-18 (Mon) and weekEnd = 2026-05-24 23:59:59.999.

  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Read the range label text.
- **Esperado:** Label reads 'SEMANA · 18 MAY – 24 MAY' using the Spanish 3-letter month abbreviations from _monthsEs.

### insights-10 — Muscles card lists all 6 display groups in canonical order
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns setsByGroup with only some groups populated (e.g. {pecho:8, piernas:5}).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build stub with setsByGroup {pecho:8, piernas:5} and sessionsCount 2.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Read the MÚSCULOS DE LA SEMANA card rows top-to-bottom.
- **Esperado:** Six rows render in order PECHO, ESPALDA, PIERNAS, BRAZOS, HOMBROS, CORE (MuscleGroupDisplay.displayOrder). Groups absent from setsByGroup display '0' SETS. PECHO shows 8, PIERNAS shows 5.

### insights-11 — Muscle row with zero sets renders muted (dot + label) and value 0
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns setsByGroup missing at least one group (e.g. CORE absent).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build stub with setsByGroup {pecho:8} (CORE absent), sessionsCount 1.
  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Inspect the CORE row vs the PECHO row.
- **Esperado:** CORE row shows '0', muted dot color (palette.textMuted) and muted label color; PECHO row shows '8' with accent dot and primary label color. The trailing 'SETS' suffix is always muted.

### insights-12 — Volume card shows 'needs routine' message when targetByGroup is empty
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns sessionsCount >= 1 but targetByGroup == {} (no routine assigned / routine not found).

  3. Inspect the VOLUMEN POR GRUPO card.
- **Esperado:** The card shows the copy 'Necesitás una rutina asignada para ver tu volumen objetivo.' and renders NO _VolumeBarRow / LinearProgressIndicator widgets.

### insights-13 — Volume card renders a progress bar per group with a positive target only
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns targetByGroup {pecho:12, espalda:0} and setsByGroup {pecho:8}.
- **Pasos:**

  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Count LinearProgressIndicator rows.
- **Esperado:** Exactly one _VolumeBarRow renders (PECHO, '8 / 12 sets'); ESPALDA is skipped because its target is 0 (the `(target ?? 0) > 0` guard). The bar value is 8/12 ≈ 0.667.

### insights-14 — Volume bar clamps ratio to 1.0 when done exceeds target
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns setsByGroup {pecho:20}, targetByGroup {pecho:12} (over-target).
- **Pasos:**

  3. Read the PECHO _VolumeBarRow.
- **Esperado:** Label text reads '20 / 12 sets' (raw counts, not clamped) but the LinearProgressIndicator.value is exactly 1.0 (ratio clamped to [0,1]); the bar does not overflow.

### insights-15 — Volume bar renders 0 progress when done is 0 against a positive target
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns targetByGroup {pecho:12} and setsByGroup with no pecho entry.

  2. Pump InsightsScreen and settle.
  3. Read the PECHO _VolumeBarRow.
- **Esperado:** PECHO row shows '0 / 12 sets' and LinearProgressIndicator.value == 0.0. The PECHO bar is still rendered because its target > 0.

### insights-16 — Back IconButton pops when a previous route exists
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InsightsScreen is pushed on top of a Home route in a real go_router stack (context.canPop() == true).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Configure a GoRouter with /home and nested /home/insights routes.
  2. Navigate to /home, then push /home/insights.
  3. Tap the header back IconButton (TreinoIcon.back).
- **Esperado:** _safePopOrHome calls context.pop(); the app returns to /home (the previous route), not a fresh go('/home').

### insights-17 — Back / VOLVER falls back to /home when there is no route to pop
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InsightsScreen is the only/initial entry on the stack (context.canPop() == false).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Configure a GoRouter whose initialLocation is /home/insights (deep-link entry, nothing to pop).
  2. Pump and settle.
  3. Tap the VOLVER OutlinedButton (and separately the back IconButton).
- **Esperado:** _safePopOrHome calls context.go('/home'); the app navigates to /home rather than throwing or staying on insights.

### insights-18 — Tapping the Home 'Esta Semana' card navigates to /home/insights
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Home screen rendered with EstaSemanaCard in loaded state (sessionsCount > 0). Router with /home and /home/insights configured.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump HomeScreen (or EstaSemanaCard within the router) with provider returning loaded insights.
  2. Tap the EstaSemanaCard GestureDetector.
  3. Settle navigation.
- **Esperado:** Router location becomes /home/insights and InsightsScreen is shown. (Confirms the documented entry point into the module.)

### insights-19 — Provider returns null when current uid is null (signed-out / no auth)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider overridden to null. (Already covered by SCENARIO-401 — listed for completeness; do not duplicate the existing test.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Create a ProviderContainer overriding currentUidProvider with null.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Result is null; no repository calls are made (the screen will show the empty state). Confirms auth-gating of the data.

### insights-20 — Provider buckets sessions strictly inside the current Mon-00:00..next-Mon window
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock SessionRepository. Build sessions relative to now() (provider uses DateTime.now(), not injectable): one at weekStart exactly (Mon 00:00), one at weekEnd boundary (Sun 23:59), one at the previous Sunday 23:59 (just before weekStart), one at next Monday 00:00 (weekEndExclusive).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Compute mondayOfWeek from now() the same way the provider does.
  2. Seed finished sessions at mondayOfWeek, mondayOfWeek+6d23h59m, mondayOfWeek-1ms, and mondayOfWeek+7d.
  3. Override exercises empty and routine null; read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** sessionsCount == 2 (only the Monday-00:00 and the Sunday-23:59 sessions are inside). The session 1ms before weekStart and the one at next-Monday-00:00 (exclusive end) are both excluded. daysTrained[0] and daysTrained[6] are true, all others false.

### insights-21 — Provider excludes non-finished sessions from weekly counts, sets, and daysTrained
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock repo returns one active and one finished session this week. (Extends SCENARIO-403 which only checks sessionsCount and that setLogs aren't read for active.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed an active session and a finished session both started today.
  2. Stub listSetLogs for the finished session with 2 chest sets.
  3. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** sessionsCount == 1, daysTrained reflects only the finished session's day, setsByGroup[pecho] == 2, and listSetLogs is never called for the active session id.

### insights-22 — Provider aggregates each SetLog as exactly one set regardless of setNumber
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock repo, one finished session this week with 3 chest SetLogs having arbitrary/duplicate setNumber values.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Stub listSetLogs returning 3 chest logs with setNumber 1,1,7.
  2. Provide exercises catalog mapping e-chest→chest; routine null.
  3. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** setsByGroup[pecho] == 3 — each SetLog row counts as one set; setNumber is not used as a weight or dedupe key.

### insights-23 — Provider drops SetLogs whose exerciseId resolves to an unknown muscle group
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock repo, finished session with a log for an exercise whose catalog muscleGroup is unrecognized AND not present in any routine slot.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Stub a chest log and an 'e-unknown' log (catalog muscleGroup 'forearms').
  2. Routine null so no slot fallback exists; read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** setsByGroup[pecho] == 1 and no spurious group key is added for the unknown exercise (toDisplayGroup returns null → skipped defensively). Total mapped sets == 1.

### insights-24 — Provider resolves custom-exercise sets via routine slot when absent from catalog
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Public catalog empty; finished session's logs reference a custom exerciseId present only as a routine slot with denormalized muscleGroup. (Already covered by SCENARIO-407 — keep, do not duplicate.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Empty exercisesProvider; routine with a slot exerciseId='e-custom' muscleGroup='back' targetSets 3.
  2. Stub 2 logs for e-custom; read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** setsByGroup[espalda] == 2 (resolved via slot fallback) and targetByGroup[espalda] == 3. Confirms the catalog-miss → slot-group fallback invariant.

### insights-25 — Provider prefers catalog muscleGroup over slot group when both exist and differ
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Exercise e1 has catalog muscleGroup 'chest'; the routine slot for e1 carries a (stale) muscleGroup 'back'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Provide exercises [e1→chest]; routine slot e1 muscleGroup 'back' targetSets 3.
  2. Stub 2 logs for e1; read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** setsByGroup[pecho] == 2 (catalog wins for set bucketing via `byId[...] ?? slotGroupById[...]`). targetByGroup still derives from the slot, so targetByGroup[espalda] == 3 — documents the intentional asymmetry between set-bucketing source and target source.

### insights-26 — Provider sums targetSets across all routine days, mapping granular groups to display groups
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Routine with two days; quads and glutes both map to PIERNAS. (Extends SCENARIO-406.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Routine day1: chest targetSets 4, back 3; day2: quads 5, glutes 3.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** targetByGroup[pecho]==4, [espalda]==3, [piernas]==8 (5+3 merged). Confirms cross-day summation and granular→display merge for targets.

### insights-27 — Provider uses the MOST RECENT session's routine as the target source
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** listByUid returns sessions ordered DESC by startedAt (per repo contract); the first one has routineId 'rNew', an older one 'rOld'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed two finished sessions this week, newest with routineId 'rNew', older with 'rOld'.
  2. Override routineByIdProvider('rNew') to a routine with chest target 4; routineByIdProvider('rOld') to a routine with back target 9.
  3. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** targetByGroup is derived from 'rNew' only (targetByGroup[pecho]==4, espalda absent). routineByIdProvider('rOld') is not used for targets. Documents the 'most recent session routine' heuristic.

### insights-28 — Provider returns empty targetByGroup when most-recent routine is not found (null)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Most recent finished session has a routineId whose routineByIdProvider resolves to null (deleted routine).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed one finished session this week with routineId 'rGone'.
  2. Override routineByIdProvider('rGone') to null; stub one chest log.
  3. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** targetByGroup is empty (the screen's volume card then shows the 'needs routine' message), while setsByGroup[pecho]==1 still computes from the catalog. No crash on null routine.

### insights-29 — Provider plannedSessionsCount is hardcoded to 5
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Any non-null result path (mock repo, at least one session or empty list).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future for a user with any sessions.
  2. Inspect plannedSessionsCount.
- **Esperado:** plannedSessionsCount == 5 regardless of actual training count (decision 5, pending Coach plannedDays). Guards against accidental change of the denominator.

### insights-30 — Provider streak counts consecutive days including today (trained today)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Finished sessions today and yesterday. (Covered by SCENARIO-300 — listed for traceability, do not duplicate.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed finished sessions for today and yesterday.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** streak >= 2 (today + yesterday counted via computeStreak from today backwards).

### insights-31 — Provider streak counts from yesterday when not trained today
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Finished sessions yesterday and day-before, none today. (Covered by SCENARIO-301.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed finished sessions yesterday and the day before; none today.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** streak == 2 (counts backward from yesterday when today is absent).

### insights-32 — Provider streak breaks on a gap day
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Finished sessions today and two-days-ago, with yesterday missing. (Covered by SCENARIO-302.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed finished sessions today and two days ago (yesterday absent).
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** streak == 1 (only today; the gap breaks the chain).

### insights-33 — Provider streak is 0 with no finished sessions and ignores active sessions
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Repo returns empty list, or only active sessions. (Covered by SCENARIO-303 + 'active not counted'.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Case A: listByUid returns []. Case B: listByUid returns one active session today.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future for each.
- **Esperado:** streak == 0 in both cases; active sessions never contribute to the streak.

### insights-34 — Provider monthSessionsCount counts only current calendar-month finished sessions
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Finished sessions this month and previous month, plus an active one this month. (Extends SCENARIO-304 + 'active excluded'.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed: 3 finished this calendar month, 1 finished previous month, 1 active this month.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** monthSessionsCount == 3 (calendar month by startedAt.toLocal year+month; NOT a rolling 30-day window; previous-month and active excluded).

### insights-35 — Provider parallelizes setLog reads per session and aggregates across multiple sessions
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Two finished sessions this week, each with its own setLog subcollection.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed session A (2 chest logs) and session B (3 back logs), both this week.
  2. Stub listSetLogs per sessionId accordingly; read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** listSetLogs is invoked once per session (A and B) and results merge: setsByGroup[pecho]==2, [espalda]==3. Confirms the Future.wait batch path aggregates correctly across sessions.

### insights-36 — Provider handles a finished session with zero set logs (empty subcollection)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** One finished session this week whose listSetLogs returns [].
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed one finished session this week; stub listSetLogs → [].
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** sessionsCount==1, daysTrained reflects the day, setsByGroup is empty (no keys). No crash; the muscles card would show all groups at 0.

### insights-37 — Provider surfaces an error (AsyncError) when the repository throws
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock SessionRepository.listByUid throws (Firestore failure / offline).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Stub listByUid to throw a FirebaseException/Exception.
  2. Read weeklyInsightsProvider — expect it to throw / be in error state.
- **Esperado:** weeklyInsightsProvider completes with an error (not null, not a partial result), which the screen renders as the 'No pudimos cargar tus insights.' error state. Confirms error propagation end-to-end.

### insights-38 — Provider is autoDispose — recomputes on each fresh mount
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mock repo whose listByUid return value changes between two reads.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future once (state A).
  2. Update the mock to return different sessions; create a fresh listener/read after the provider has been disposed (no active listeners) to force re-evaluation.
  3. Compare results.
- **Esperado:** Because the provider is autoDispose, a fresh subscription recomputes from the repository and reflects the updated data rather than serving a stale cached value.

### insights-39 — Role parity: trainer account sees the same insights UI driven by their own uid data
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator seed with a trainer (coach) account signed in; currentUidProvider = trainer uid. The route /home/insights is not role-gated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in as trainer / override currentUidProvider with the trainer uid.
  2. Seed the trainer uid with their own finished sessions + a routine.
  3. Navigate to /home/insights and settle.
- **Esperado:** InsightsScreen renders identically to the athlete experience, computing aggregates from the trainer's OWN sessions/routine (no athlete data leaks in). The module has no athlete-only gate — trainer with zero own sessions sees the empty state.

### insights-40 — Data isolation: provider only reads the signed-in uid's sessions and setLogs
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Two seeded accounts (athlete A, athlete/trainer B). currentUidProvider == A.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override currentUidProvider with uid A.
  2. Verify listByUid is called with 'A' and listSetLogs is called with uid:'A' for A's sessions only.
  3. Read weeklyInsightsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Repository is queried strictly with uid A; no call uses uid B. Aggregates contain only A's data. Confirms per-user data scoping (permission/isolation invariant).

### insights-41 — BodySilhouettePlaceholder falls back to icon when body asset fails to load
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped in a test without the asset bundle (Image.asset errorBuilder triggers).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump BodySilhouettePlaceholder(width:160,height:240) inside MaterialApp.
  2. Pump and settle so the asset load fails.
- **Esperado:** The errorBuilder renders TreinoIcon.tabWorkout (accent at 0.5 alpha) instead of crashing; the card border/background still render. Confirms 'the card never breaks visually' invariant.

### insights-42 — BodySilhouettePlaceholder shows two bodies when showBack is true, one otherwise
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped in both configurations.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump with showBack:false → expect a single _BodyImage (bodyfront).
  2. Pump with showBack:true → expect two _BodyImage widgets (bodyfront + bodyback).
- **Esperado:** showBack:false renders exactly 1 body image; showBack:true renders 2 side-by-side. (Insights screen uses the single-front variant; Home card uses showBack:true.)

### insights-43 — BodySilhouettePlaceholder renders optional caption label when provided
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped with label:'Tocá para ver tus insights'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump BodySilhouettePlaceholder with a non-null label.
  2. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** The label text is shown beneath the silhouette; when label is null no caption Text is rendered.

### insights-44 — MuscleGroupDisplay mapping is case-insensitive and defensive for unknown/empty input
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure unit test of String.toDisplayGroup(). (Largely covered by muscle_group_test; included to assert the full invariant set.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert 'Chest'/'CHEST'→pecho, 'GLUTES'→piernas, 'abs'→core, 'triceps'→brazos.
  2. Assert ''→null, 'forearms'→null, 'random'→null.
- **Esperado:** All known granular groups (chest, back, shoulders, quads/hamstrings/glutes/calves, biceps/triceps, core/abs) map to the correct display group regardless of case; unknown and empty strings map to null.

### insights-45 — WeeklyInsights value equality and copyWith preserve all fields including maps and lists
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure unit test of the DTO. (Covered by weekly_insights_test; included for completeness of the catalog.)
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build two instances with identical data including setsByGroup, targetByGroup, daysTrained → assert == and equal hashCode.
  2. Mutate one field via copyWith → assert inequality; copyWith() with no args → assert equal.
- **Esperado:** Deep equality holds (listEquals/mapEquals + stable map hash); copyWith overrides only the targeted field and preserves the rest. Guards against regressions in the immutable DTO contract.

### insights-46 — Data state body is scrollable and respects bottom safe-area inset
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Provider returns a loaded WeeklyInsights with all cards; render with a non-zero MediaQuery bottom padding.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Wrap InsightsScreen with MediaQuery providing padding.bottom = 34 (simulated home indicator).
  2. Pump and settle; verify a ListView with AlwaysScrollableScrollPhysics exists.
  3. Attempt a drag/scroll gesture.
- **Esperado:** The body is a scrollable ListView (AlwaysScrollableScrollPhysics) and its bottom padding includes 20 + MediaQuery bottom inset, so the VOLVER button is not obscured by the home indicator/navbar.

# Módulo: measurements

_Test-case catalog for lib/features/measurements/ (domain Measurement, MeasurementRepository, measurementsForAthleteProvider, LogMeasurementScreen, MeasurementProgressChart) plus its integration point in coach/athlete_detail_screen.dart (_AntropometriaSection). No prior tests exist (test/features/measurements/ is absent), so this is greenfield coverage. Project has fake_cloud_firestore + mocktail + Riverpod overrides + TestAppWrapper, so data/logic/ui cases are automatable; only real-auth and native-keyboard/gesture cases are manual._

### measurements-01 — Repository add() assigns auto-generated id and persists the document
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore instance; MeasurementRepository constructed with it.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a Measurement with id:'' , a valid athleteId, recordedBy, recordedAt, and weightKg:80.0.
  2. Call repository.add(measurement).
  3. Read back the doc from the 'measurements' collection using the returned model's id.
- **Esperado:** add() returns a Measurement whose id equals the generated Firestore doc id (non-empty, not ''). The persisted document exists, its stored 'id' field equals the doc id, athleteId/recordedBy/weightKg round-trip intact.

### measurements-02 — Repository add() serializes recordedAt via TimestampConverter (DateTime <-> Timestamp)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; repository.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Create a Measurement with recordedAt = a known UTC DateTime.
  2. add() it, then read the raw stored document map.
  3. Decode it back via Measurement.fromJson({...data,'id':docId}).
- **Esperado:** Stored recordedAt is a Firestore Timestamp; decoded recordedAt equals the original DateTime (UTC preserved). No exception during encode/decode.

### measurements-03 — Repository delete() removes the document
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with one measurement already added (id known).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repository.delete(id) for the existing doc.
  2. Attempt to read the doc back.
- **Esperado:** Document no longer exists (snapshot.exists == false). No exception thrown.

### measurements-04 — watchRecordedBy emits only measurements whose recordedBy matches the trainer uid
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with 2 docs recordedBy 'trainerA' and 1 doc recordedBy 'trainerB'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repository.watchRecordedBy('trainerA').
  2. Read the first emitted list.
- **Esperado:** Emitted list contains exactly the 2 'trainerA' docs; the 'trainerB' doc is excluded. (Note: repo does NOT sort — sorting is the provider's job.)

### measurements-05 — watchForAthlete emits only measurements for the given athleteId (athlete self-view path)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with 2 docs athleteId 'ath1' and 1 doc athleteId 'ath2'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repository.watchForAthlete('ath1').
  2. Read the first emitted list.
- **Esperado:** Emitted list contains exactly the 2 'ath1' docs; 'ath2' is excluded. Confirms the alternate query exists and is correct even though no provider currently exposes it.

### measurements-06 — watch streams are live: adding/deleting a matching doc re-emits an updated list
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore empty; subscription to watchRecordedBy('trainerA') captured via emittedList collector.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe and record first emission ([]).
  2. add() a doc recordedBy 'trainerA'.
  3. Wait for next emission.
  4. delete() that doc.
  5. Wait for next emission.
- **Esperado:** Emissions progress []  -> [1 item] -> []. Stream reacts to writes without re-subscription.

### measurements-07 — _fromDoc skips a malformed document instead of breaking the whole list
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with one valid doc (recordedBy 'trainerA') and one corrupt doc (recordedBy 'trainerA' but recordedAt stored as a String like 'not-a-timestamp', or required athleteId missing).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repository.watchRecordedBy('trainerA').
  2. Read the first emitted list.
- **Esperado:** Emitted list contains only the 1 valid measurement; the malformed doc is silently dropped (whereType filters the null). No exception propagates to the stream; a developer.log warning is emitted.

### measurements-08 — _fromDoc injects the Firestore doc id even when the stored body omitted 'id'
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore; manually write a measurement map WITHOUT an 'id' key (or with id:'') directly to a doc with a known generated id.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Write the doc directly (bypassing add()).
  2. Subscribe to watchRecordedBy with that recordedBy and read first emission.
- **Esperado:** The decoded Measurement.id equals the Firestore snapshot id, not '' — confirms the {...data,'id':snap.id} merge.

### measurements-09 — Measurement.fromJson/toJson round-trips with all metric fields null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure unit).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Construct a Measurement with only required fields (id, athleteId, recordedBy, recordedAt) and every optional metric null.
  2. Serialize toJson then fromJson the result.
- **Esperado:** Round-trip produces an equal Measurement; all metric fields remain null. No crash on absent keys.

### measurements-10 — measurementsForAthleteProvider returns empty list when no trainer is authenticated
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer overriding currentUidProvider to return null; measurementRepositoryProvider may be a fake/throwing repo to prove it is never queried.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override currentUidProvider -> null.
  2. Read measurementsForAthleteProvider('ath1').future / first value.
- **Esperado:** Provider yields const [] immediately (Stream.value([])) and does NOT call the repository. Guards against unauthenticated reads.

### measurements-11 — measurementsForAthleteProvider filters by recordedBy(current trainer) AND athleteId
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider overridden to 'trainerA'. Repository (fake firestore) seeded with: doc1 recordedBy trainerA/athlete ath1, doc2 recordedBy trainerA/athlete ath2, doc3 recordedBy trainerB/athlete ath1.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read measurementsForAthleteProvider('ath1').
  2. Await first data emission.
- **Esperado:** Returns only doc1 (trainerA + ath1). doc2 excluded by client-side athleteId filter; doc3 excluded by the recordedBy query. Confirms a trainer never sees measurements another trainer logged for the same athlete.

### measurements-12 — measurementsForAthleteProvider sorts results ascending by recordedAt
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider -> 'trainerA'. Seed 3 measurements for ath1/trainerA with recordedAt out of order (e.g. Mar, Jan, Feb).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read measurementsForAthleteProvider('ath1').
  2. Await first data emission and inspect ordering.
- **Esperado:** List is sorted ascending by recordedAt (Jan, Feb, Mar). This is the invariant the summary card ('latest = last') and the chart depend on.

### measurements-13 — measurementsForAthleteProvider returns empty list when trainer has no measurements for that athlete
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider -> 'trainerA'. Firestore has measurements for other athletes only.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read measurementsForAthleteProvider('athWithNone').
  2. Await first emission.
- **Esperado:** Returns [] (empty), AsyncData not AsyncError. Drives the empty-state UI in measurements-30.

### measurements-14 — Log screen: happy path saves a measurement with parsed numeric fields and pops with success snackbar
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump LogMeasurementScreen(athleteId:'ath1') inside ProviderScope with currentUidProvider -> 'trainerA' and a spy/fake measurementRepositoryProvider; wrapped so Navigator.pop is observable.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '80.5' in Peso, '15' in Grasa, '35' in Masa muscular.
  2. Tap 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN'.
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** repository.add called once with athleteId 'ath1', recordedBy 'trainerA', weightKg 80.5, fatPercentage 15.0, muscleMassKg 35.0, recordedAt non-null UTC. Screen pops; a 'Medición guardada' SnackBar is shown.

### measurements-15 — Log screen: all fields empty still saves a valid measurement (every metric null)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen with currentUidProvider -> 'trainerA', spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Do not enter any field.
  2. Tap 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN'.
- **Esperado:** repository.add is called with a Measurement where ALL metric fields and notes are null (only athleteId/recordedBy/recordedAt set). Business rule: a measurement with no metrics is allowed. Screen pops with success snackbar.

### measurements-16 — Log screen: comma decimal input is normalized to a dot before parsing
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen, currentUidProvider -> 'trainerA', spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '80,5' (comma) in Peso.
  2. Tap 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN'.
- **Esperado:** repository.add receives weightKg == 80.5 (comma converted to dot via _parseDouble). Covers es-AR keyboard decimal entry.

### measurements-17 — Log screen: invalid / non-numeric input is silently treated as null (not zero, no crash)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen, currentUidProvider -> 'trainerA', spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter 'abc' in Peso and '12.3.4' in Grasa.
  2. Tap 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN'.
- **Esperado:** repository.add receives weightKg null and fatPercentage null (double.tryParse fails -> null). No exception; save succeeds. Confirms invalid input does NOT become 0.

### measurements-18 — Log screen: whitespace-only Peso parses to null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen, trainer authed, spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '   ' (spaces) in Peso.
  2. Save.
- **Esperado:** _parseDouble trims to empty -> weightKg null in the saved model.

### measurements-19 — Log screen: zero is a valid, persisted value (boundary)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen, trainer authed, spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '0' in Peso.
  2. Save.
- **Esperado:** repository.add receives weightKg == 0.0 (NOT null). Distinguishes 'zero entered' from 'left blank'.

### measurements-20 — Log screen: notes containing only whitespace are saved as null; non-empty notes are trimmed
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen, trainer authed, spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Case A: enter '   ' in Notas, save -> assert.
  2. Case B (fresh screen): enter '  buen progreso  ', save -> assert.
- **Esperado:** Case A: notes == null. Case B: notes == 'buen progreso' (trimmed, no surrounding spaces).

### measurements-21 — Log screen: bilateral fields persist to the correct L/R model fields
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen, trainer authed, spy repo.
- **Pasos:**

  2. In the Bíceps row enter '38' on the left (I) field and '39' on the right (D) field.
  3. Save.
- **Esperado:** repository.add receives bicepsLCm == 38.0 and bicepsRCm == 39.0 (left maps to L, right maps to R — not swapped).

### measurements-22 — Log screen: CIRCUNFERENCIAS section is collapsed by default and expands/collapses on tap
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen pumped.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Verify the 'Hombros' field (inside the section) is not present initially.
  2. Tap the CIRCUNFERENCIAS header; verify TRONCO/Hombros now visible and chevron is chevronUp.
  3. Tap the header again; verify content hidden and chevron is chevronDown.
- **Esperado:** Default state collapsed (chevronDown, inner fields absent). First tap expands (inner fields present, chevronUp). Second tap collapses again.

### measurements-23 — Log screen: Save button disabled and shows error snackbar when no trainer is authenticated
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogMeasurementScreen pumped with currentUidProvider -> null.
- **Pasos:**

  2. (If button were forced) attempt _save with null uid.
- **Esperado:** canSave == false so onPressed is null (button visually disabled, border/muted colors). _save short-circuits: shows 'No hay sesión activa. No se puede guardar.' snackbar and never calls repository.add. Auth gate enforced.

### measurements-24 — Log screen: error from repository keeps screen open, re-enables save, shows retry snackbar
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

- **Esperado:** Screen is NOT popped. _saving reset to false (button usable again). SnackBar 'No pudimos guardar la medición. Probá de nuevo.' shown. No data loss (controllers retain values).

### measurements-25 — Log screen: shows progress spinner and ignores double-tap while saving
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  3. Tap 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN' again.
- **Esperado:** After first tap _saving==true: button shows CircularProgressIndicator, onPressed becomes null, Cancelar is also disabled. Second tap does nothing (guard 'if (_saving) return'); repository.add invoked exactly once.

### measurements-26 — Log screen: Cancelar pops without saving and is disabled while saving
