### measurements-27 — Log screen: recordedAt is stored in UTC and recordedBy is the current trainer uid
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true

- **Esperado:** recordedAt.isUtc == true and is within the test window of DateTime.now(); recordedBy == 'trainerXYZ'; athleteId == the widget's athleteId. id is '' at call time (repo assigns real id).

### measurements-28 — Antropometria section: loading state shows 'Cargando…' card
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pump AthleteDetailScreen (or _AntropometriaSection) with measurementsForAthleteProvider overridden to a stream that never emits (pending).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump one frame without settling.
  2. Find the ANTROPOMETRIA section.
- **Esperado:** A card with text 'Cargando…' is shown under the ANTROPOMETRIA header. No summary card, no chart.

### measurements-29 — Antropometria section: error state shows 'No pudimos cargar las medidas.'
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _AntropometriaSection with measurementsForAthleteProvider overridden to emit an error (AsyncError).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and settle.
  2. Locate the ANTROPOMETRIA card.
- **Esperado:** Card text 'No pudimos cargar las medidas.' shown. The UI degrades gracefully — no red error screen, no exception.

### measurements-30 — Antropometria section: empty state shows 'Sin mediciones todavía. Cargá la primera.'
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _AntropometriaSection with provider overridden to AsyncData([]).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** Card text 'Sin mediciones todavía. Cargá la primera.' shown; no summary card, no chart, no hint card.

### measurements-31 — Antropometria section: single measurement shows summary + singular count + 'load another' hint (no chart)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _AntropometriaSection with provider overridden to one measurement (weightKg 80, fatPercentage 15).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** Summary card shows the date and metric chips (Peso 80 kg, % Graso 15%). Count line reads '1 medición registrada' (singular). The chart is NOT rendered; instead the hint card 'Cargá otra medición para ver el progreso.' is shown (since count < 2).

### measurements-32 — Antropometria section: latest measurement = last item (relies on ASC sort), plural count, chart rendered
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _AntropometriaSection with provider overridden to 3 measurements sorted ASC, the last having a distinct weightKg (e.g. 78) vs earlier.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and settle.
  2. Inspect the summary card values.
- **Esperado:** Summary card reflects the LAST measurement (latest), not the first. Count line reads '3 mediciones registradas' (plural). MeasurementProgressChart is rendered (count >= 2), hint card absent.

### measurements-33 — Antropometria section: summary card omits null metrics and shows 'Sin datos de composición.' when all four are null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _AntropometriaSection with one measurement having only circumference fields set (weightKg, fatPercentage, muscleMassKg, waistCm all null).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and settle.
  2. Inspect the metric row in the summary card.
- **Esperado:** No Peso/%Graso/Masa muscular/Cintura chips rendered; instead the _MetricRow fallback text 'Sin datos de composición.' is shown. Confirms only non-null key metrics appear.

### measurements-34 — Antropometria section: '+ Cargar' opens LogMeasurementScreen as a fullscreen dialog with the correct athleteId
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteDetailScreen / _AntropometriaSection(athleteId:'ath1') pumped inside a MaterialApp with a navigator observer.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap '+ Cargar' in the ANTROPOMETRIA header.
  2. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** A MaterialPageRoute with fullscreenDialog:true is pushed containing LogMeasurementScreen whose athleteId == 'ath1'. The log form's 'Cargar medición' title and 'GUARDAR MEDICIÓN' button are visible.

### measurements-35 — Chart _buildAvailable: only metrics with >=2 non-null points are selectable
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** List of 3 measurements: weightKg present in all 3; waistCm present in only 1; fatPercentage present in 2.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump MeasurementProgressChart(measurements: list).
  2. Inspect rendered metric chips (selector row).
- **Esperado:** Chips include 'Peso' and '% Graso' (>=2 points each) but NOT 'Cintura' (only 1 point). First available metric is pre-selected.

### measurements-36 — Chart _buildAvailable fallback: when no metric has >=2 points, falls back to first metric (Peso)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** 2 measurements where every metric is null in at least one (no metric reaches 2 points).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump MeasurementProgressChart with that list.
- **Esperado:** _available is [Peso] (the guaranteed non-empty fallback). One chip 'Peso' shown; since its points < 2 the LineChart is not drawn (no >=2 data points) but no crash occurs.

### measurements-37 — Chart bilateral _avg: averages L and R when both present, falls back to the single non-null side
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Measurements where biceps L/R both set in some, only one side set in others.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Unit-test the extractor behavior via the rendered chart, or extract _avg semantics: _avg(38,40)=39; _avg(38,null)=38; _avg(null,40)=40; _avg(null,null)=null.
  2. Select the 'Bíceps' chip and read the header current value.
- **Esperado:** Both sides -> mean; one side -> that side's value; neither -> excluded as a data point. Header current value equals the averaged value of the latest point.

### measurements-38 — Chart header: delta and up/down glyph computed from first vs last point of selected metric
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Measurements with weightKg ascending then ending lower, e.g. [80, 82, 78] sorted by date.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump chart, ensure 'Peso' selected.
  2. Read the header delta text.
- **Esperado:** Current value shows 78 (last). Delta = last-first = 78-80 = -2.0 -> glyph '▼' and '2.0 kg'. For a rising series last>first the glyph is '▲'. (delta>=0 uses '▲').

### measurements-39 — Chart header value formatting: integers shown without decimals, non-integers with one decimal
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Two series: one whose last value is 80.0, one whose last value is 80.4.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and read the large current-value text for each.
- **Esperado:** 80.0 renders as '80' (value%1==0 -> toStringAsFixed(0)); 80.4 renders as '80.4' (toStringAsFixed(1)). Delta always uses one decimal.

### measurements-40 — Chart span label: days vs weeks pluralization
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure-function coverage of _spanLabel via chart rendering with controlled recordedAt gaps.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Series spanning 1 day -> assert '(1 día)'.
  2. Series spanning 3 days -> '(3 días)'.
  3. Series spanning 7 days -> '(1 semana)'.
  4. Series spanning 21 days -> '(3 semanas)'.
- **Esperado:** <7 days uses 'día/días'; >=7 days converts to rounded weeks using 'semana/semanas'. Singular/plural correct at each boundary.

### measurements-41 — Chart: selecting a different metric chip updates the header and line
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Measurements with >=2 points for both 'Peso' (kg) and '% Graso' (%).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump chart (Peso selected by default).
  2. Tap the '% Graso' chip.
  3. Pump.
- **Esperado:** Selected chip becomes '% Graso' (accent styling), header unit switches to '%', current value reflects fat series. Selection is reflected via setState.

### measurements-42 — Chart didUpdateWidget: keeps selection if still valid, resets to first when selection disappears
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Initial measurements make 'Peso' and '% Graso' available; '% Graso' selected.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Rebuild the chart with a NEW measurements list (different object) where '% Graso' now has <2 points but 'Peso' still has >=2.
  2. Pump.
- **Esperado:** Because '% Graso' is no longer in _available, selection resets to _available.first ('Peso'). If instead the new list still contains '% Graso', the selection is preserved. No exception, no stale extractor.

### measurements-43 — Chart: flat series (all equal values) renders without divide-by-zero padding crash
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Measurements with identical weightKg across all points (range 0).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump chart with the flat series, 'Peso' selected.
- **Esperado:** minY/maxY use the fixed pad 1.0 (since range<0.001) so the y-axis has a valid non-zero span; LineChart renders without NaN/Infinity or exception.

### measurements-44 — Chart _labelIndices: at most 4 bottom labels (first, last, ~2 interior) for long series
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** A series of 10 points for a selected metric.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Compute/observe label indices used for bottom titles.
- **Esperado:** <=4 distinct indices, always including first and last; with >4 points two evenly spaced interior indices are added. With <=4 points all indices are labelled.

### measurements-45 — Chart gating: with <2 data points for selected metric no LineChart is drawn (header may still show)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Measurements where selected metric has exactly 1 non-null point but is somehow selected (e.g. fallback case).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump chart and look for LineChart widget.
- **Esperado:** No LineChart in the tree when points.length < 2; header value still renders if points.isNotEmpty. No render-overflow or chart exception. (Caller also gates at >=2 measurements, but the widget self-guards.)

### measurements-46 — Chart tooltip: tapping a data point shows value + unit + short date
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Real device or integration test; chart with >=2 points.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap directly on a plotted dot.
  2. Observe the tooltip.
- **Esperado:** Tooltip displays '<value> <unit>' and the short date (e.g. '78 kg\n7 abr'). Requires real touch hit-testing on the fl_chart canvas, which is unreliable in widget tests.

### measurements-47 — End-to-end on device: trainer logs a measurement and the Antropometria section updates live
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Firebase emulator seeded with a trainer account linked to an athlete; trainer signed in; on AthleteDetailScreen for that athlete.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap '+ Cargar'.
  2. Enter Peso 80,5 using the native decimal keyboard.
  3. Tap GUARDAR MEDICIÓN.
  4. Observe return to athlete detail.
- **Esperado:** Form dismisses, 'Medición guardada' snackbar appears, and the ANTROPOMETRIA summary card updates within seconds (live Firestore stream) showing Peso 80.5 kg and an incremented count. Requires real auth + native keyboard + live Firestore, so manual.

### measurements-48 — Permission/isolation on device: a measurement logged by trainer B is not visible to trainer A for the same athlete
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator with two trainer accounts both linked to the same athlete; trainer B has logged one measurement.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in as trainer A.
  2. Open AthleteDetailScreen for the shared athlete.
  3. Inspect the ANTROPOMETRIA section.
- **Esperado:** Trainer A sees 'Sin mediciones todavía' (or only A's own), NOT trainer B's measurement — because the provider queries recordedBy == current trainer. Confirms data-isolation business rule end to end. Needs real multi-account auth, so manual (the logic equivalent is covered by measurements-11).

# Módulo: notifications

_FCM/push-notification infrastructure module (no notification-list UI). Surfaces: FcmTokenRepository (users/{uid}.fcmTokens array via arrayUnion/arrayRemove), FcmService (token lifecycle init/dispose + permission request + foreground/background/cold-start message streams), fcmLifecycleProvider (auth-driven init/dispose), PermissionGate (once-per-session OS permission request gated on completed profile), goDeepLink router (with /coach fallback), and ForegroundSnackBarHandler (in-app SnackBar with deep-link action). The module is role-agnostic for athlete vs trainer — the only role-shaped behavior is which deep links are valid, with /coach as universal fallback. Existing test coverage under test/features/notifications/ is strong (SCENARIO-619..687); this catalog re-states P0 happy/critical paths for completeness and adds genuine gaps: malformed/non-string payloads, multi-device token isolation, sign-out-before-grant race, provisional authorization, foreground SnackBar with empty notification, and lifecycle re-init token de-dup._

### notifications-01 — saveToken creates fcmTokens array on a doc that lacks the field
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with users/{uid} doc existing but no fcmTokens field.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed users/{uid} = {uid}
  2. Call repo.saveToken(uid, 'tok-1')
  3. Read back users/{uid}.fcmTokens
- **Esperado:** fcmTokens == ['tok-1']; field created via arrayUnion merge without touching other fields.

### notifications-02 — saveToken is idempotent for a duplicate token
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** users/{uid}.fcmTokens == ['tok-1'].
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.saveToken(uid, 'tok-1') again
  2. Read back fcmTokens
- **Esperado:** fcmTokens stays ['tok-1'] (length 1); arrayUnion dedupes — no duplicate Firestore entries.

### notifications-03 — saveToken appends a second device token without overwriting the first
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** users/{uid}.fcmTokens == ['tok-phone'].
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.saveToken(uid, 'tok-tablet')
  2. Read back fcmTokens
- **Esperado:** fcmTokens contains both 'tok-phone' and 'tok-tablet'; length 2 — multi-device support preserved.

### notifications-04 — removeToken removes only the specified token
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** users/{uid}.fcmTokens == ['tok-1','tok-2'].
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.removeToken(uid, 'tok-1')
  2. Read back fcmTokens
- **Esperado:** fcmTokens == ['tok-2']; arrayRemove targets exactly one element, other devices' tokens untouched.

### notifications-05 — removeToken of an absent token is a no-op
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** users/{uid}.fcmTokens == ['tok-2'].
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.removeToken(uid, 'tok-999')
  2. Read back fcmTokens
- **Esperado:** Completes normally; fcmTokens unchanged == ['tok-2'].

### notifications-06 — removeToken on a non-existent user doc swallows not-found and does not throw
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** users/{uid} document never created.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.removeToken(uid, 'tok-ghost')
- **Esperado:** Completes normally (FirebaseException code 'not-found' caught and returned); logout cleanup never crashes the app.

### notifications-07 — removeToken rethrows non-not-found Firebase errors
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Firestore stubbed to throw a FirebaseException with code != 'not-found' (e.g. 'permission-denied') on update.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.removeToken(uid, 'tok-x')
- **Esperado:** The exception propagates (is rethrown) — only 'not-found' is swallowed, so genuine failures stay visible.

### notifications-08 — Token field name is fcmTokens (camelCase), never fcm_tokens
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** users/{uid} doc seeded.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.saveToken(uid, 'tok-camel')
  2. Inspect document keys
- **Esperado:** data contains key 'fcmTokens' and does NOT contain 'fcm_tokens' (ADR-PN-001) — guards against schema drift that would silently break server-side sends.

### notifications-09 — FcmService.init persists the initial token from getToken
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** messaging.getToken() returns 'tok-init'; onTokenRefresh empty; repo mocked.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
- **Esperado:** getToken called once; repo.saveToken(uid, 'tok-init') called once.

### notifications-10 — FcmService.init does NOT call requestPermission
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** messaging.getToken() returns a token; onTokenRefresh empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
- **Esperado:** messaging.requestPermission(...) never called — permission is owned exclusively by PermissionGate (ADR-PN-003), preventing an OS prompt at sign-in.

### notifications-11 — onTokenRefresh emission persists the refreshed token
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** init() done; onTokenRefresh wired to a controllable stream.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
  2. Emit 'tok-refreshed' on the refresh stream
  3. Pump microtasks
- **Esperado:** repo.saveToken(uid, 'tok-refreshed') called once — token rotation is captured.

### notifications-12 — init swallows getToken null without saving
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** messaging.getToken() returns null; onTokenRefresh empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
- **Esperado:** Completes normally; repo.saveToken never called (no null/empty token written).

### notifications-13 — init swallows apns-token-not-set FirebaseException but still subscribes to onTokenRefresh
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** messaging.getToken() throws FirebaseException(code:'apns-token-not-set'); onTokenRefresh is a controllable stream.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid) and assert it completes
  2. Emit 'tok-after-permission' on the refresh stream
  3. Pump microtasks
- **Esperado:** init completes (no throw to caller, no Crashlytics noise); saveToken not called for the failed getToken; but the later refresh DOES call saveToken(uid,'tok-after-permission') — subscription registered even when getToken failed (SCENARIO-685).

### notifications-14 — init swallows unexpected (non-Firebase) getToken errors
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** messaging.getToken() throws a generic Exception; onTokenRefresh empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
- **Esperado:** Completes normally; error swallowed and logged; saveToken not called — generic catch branch is exercised.

### notifications-15 — Calling init twice cancels the previous refresh subscription (no duplicate writes)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** onTokenRefresh is a broadcast stream so a leaked listener would also receive events; getToken returns a token.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid) twice
  2. clearInteractions on repo
  3. Emit one 'tok-refreshed' event
  4. Pump microtasks
- **Esperado:** saveToken(uid,'tok-refreshed') called exactly once — the old listener was cancelled before resubscribing, preventing duplicate Firestore writes (sign-in + PermissionGate re-init path).

### notifications-16 — FcmService.dispose removes the current token
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** init() done with getToken returning 'tok-current'; onTokenRefresh empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
  2. Call service.dispose(uid)
- **Esperado:** getToken called again to resolve the current token; repo.removeToken(uid,'tok-current') called once.

### notifications-17 — dispose swallows removeToken errors
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** init() done; repo.removeToken throws Exception('Firestore unavailable').
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
  2. Call service.dispose(uid)
- **Esperado:** dispose completes normally — sign-out cleanup never crashes even if the user is already signed out from Firestore.

### notifications-18 — dispose cancels the refresh subscription so later refreshes are ignored
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** init() done with controllable refresh stream.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
  2. Call service.dispose(uid)
  3. clearInteractions on repo
  4. Emit 'tok-after-dispose'
  5. Pump microtasks
- **Esperado:** saveToken never called after dispose — no zombie listener writes a token for a signed-out user.

### notifications-19 — dispose swallows getToken failure during cleanup
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** init() done; messaging.getToken() throws on the dispose call.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call service.init(uid)
  2. Call service.dispose(uid)
- **Esperado:** Completes normally; removeToken not called; error caught in dispose try/catch.

### notifications-20 — fcmLifecycleProvider calls init(uid) when auth emits a non-null user
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer overrides authStateChangesProvider with a controllable stream and fcmServiceProvider with a mock; fcmLifecycleProvider eagerly read.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Add a non-null user (uid 'uid-test-user') to the auth stream
  2. Pump microtasks
- **Esperado:** fcmService.init('uid-test-user') called once (SCENARIO-650) — sign-in registers the token lifecycle.

### notifications-21 — fcmLifecycleProvider calls dispose(prevUid) when auth emits null after a user
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Same container as above; lifecycle registered.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Add non-null user to the stream and pump
  2. Add null to the stream and pump
- **Esperado:** fcmService.dispose('uid-test-user') called once with the PREVIOUS uid (SCENARIO-651) — sign-out cleans up the right user's token.

### notifications-22 — fcmLifecycleProvider does nothing when auth emits only null (never signed in)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Same container; lifecycle registered.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Add only null to the auth stream
  2. Pump microtasks
- **Esperado:** Neither init nor dispose called (SCENARIO-683) — no crash, no spurious cleanup for a user that never authenticated.

### notifications-23 — fcmLifecycleProvider listener uses fireImmediately:false (no init on bare registration)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Container built; fcmLifecycleProvider read; auth stream has emitted nothing yet.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read fcmLifecycleProvider
  2. Pump microtasks without emitting any auth event
- **Esperado:** init/dispose not called until a real auth event arrives — the listener does not fire on its initial seed.

### notifications-24 — goDeepLink with null routes to /coach fallback
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget wrapped in InheritedGoRouter with a mock GoRouter.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, null)
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach') called once (SCENARIO-654).

### notifications-25 — goDeepLink with empty string routes to /coach fallback
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InheritedGoRouter with mock router.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, '')
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach') called once — empty payload never crashes navigation.

### notifications-26 — goDeepLink without a leading slash logs and falls back to /coach
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InheritedGoRouter with mock router.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, 'no-leading-slash')
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach') called once; a warning is logged (SCENARIO-682) — malformed server payloads are contained.

### notifications-27 — goDeepLink with whitespace-only string falls back to /coach
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InheritedGoRouter with mock router.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, '   ')
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach') called once — '   ' does not start with '/' so it is treated as invalid.

### notifications-28 — goDeepLink with a valid path navigates exactly to that path
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InheritedGoRouter with mock router.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, '/coach/chat/abc?other=xyz')
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach/chat/abc?other=xyz') called once; router.go('/coach') NOT called — query string preserved verbatim (SCENARIO-653).

### notifications-29 — goDeepLink preserves query parameters on a tabbed deep link
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InheritedGoRouter with mock router.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, '/coach?tab=agenda')
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach?tab=agenda') called once exactly; no fallback fired.

### notifications-30 — goDeepLink navigates to a trainer profile deep link (role-shaped target)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** InheritedGoRouter with mock router.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goDeepLink(context, '/coach/trainer/uid-1')
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach/trainer/uid-1') called once — a coach/trainer deep link is passed through unchanged; routing/role guards are handled downstream by the router, not this function.

### notifications-31 — PermissionGate requests permission once when profile setup is complete
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope with authenticated user and userProfile having a non-null displayName; permissionGateAttemptedProvider default false.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate inside a Scaffold
  2. pumpAndSettle to run the post-frame callback
- **Esperado:** fcmService.requestPermission() called exactly once (SCENARIO-659).

### notifications-32 — PermissionGate does NOT request permission when displayName is null (setup incomplete)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Authenticated user; userProfile.displayName == null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission never called (SCENARIO-660) — the prompt is deferred until onboarding completes.

### notifications-33 — PermissionGate does NOT request permission while profile is still loading (null profile)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider stream value is null (not yet resolved); authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission never called — null profile is treated as setup-not-done, avoiding a premature prompt.

### notifications-34 — PermissionGate requests only once across a re-mount in the same ProviderScope
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** UncontrolledProviderScope reused across two pumps with the same container; profile has displayName.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Mount PermissionGate (Scaffold body), pumpAndSettle
  2. Re-pump with a different tree shape (PermissionGate inside a Column) on the same container, pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission called exactly once total — permissionGateAttemptedProvider survives the widget State teardown, so tab nav / parent rebuilds never re-fire the prompt (SCENARIO-661).

### notifications-35 — PermissionGate re-fires init(uid) after an authorized grant to register the token
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** requestPermission returns authorized; authenticated user uid 'uid-test'; fcmService.init stubbed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate with a completed profile
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission called once AND fcmService.init('uid-test') called once — re-init registers the token now that APNS is provisioned (SCENARIO-687), fixing silent no-notifications until next sign-in.

### notifications-36 — PermissionGate re-fires init on provisional authorization
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** requestPermission returns NotificationSettings with authorizationStatus == AuthorizationStatus.provisional; authenticated user.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate with completed profile
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** fcmService.init(uid) called once — provisional is treated as granted (status authorized OR provisional triggers re-init), so quiet-delivery users still get a token.

### notifications-37 — PermissionGate does NOT re-fire init when permission is denied
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** requestPermission returns denied; authenticated user.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate with completed profile
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission called once; fcmService.init NEVER called (SCENARIO-687 denial path) — no APNS provisioning means re-init would just fail.

### notifications-38 — PermissionGate handles denial gracefully with no SnackBar, no retry, no crash
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** requestPermission returns denied; completed profile.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission called once; no SnackBar present; app continues normally (SCENARIO-662) — denial is logged and swallowed.

### notifications-39 — PermissionGate swallows a thrown platform error without crashing or retrying
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** requestPermission throws Exception('platform error'); completed profile.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate
  2. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** requestPermission attempted once; no crash; PermissionGate still renders (SizedBox) — error caught in _requestPermission try/catch.

### notifications-40 — PermissionGate renders zero-layout SizedBox.shrink (no visible UI)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Any profile state.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump PermissionGate
  2. Search for visible widgets
- **Esperado:** PermissionGate present; no Text/Button rendered — it has zero layout impact in the home shell.

### notifications-41 — PermissionGate does NOT request permission for an unauthenticated session even with a displayName
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authStateChangesProvider yields null user but userProfile somehow has a displayName.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override authStateChangesProvider to Stream.value(null)
  2. Pump PermissionGate with displayName set
  3. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** Either requestPermission is not called, or if it is called the post-grant init is skipped because the user is null (init only runs when await authStateChangesProvider.future != null) — no token registered for a null user. Documents the auth-gate invariant; tighten the assertion to match implementation.

### notifications-42 — Foreground message shows a SnackBar with title and body
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ForegroundSnackBarHandler mounted in a Scaffold with a ScaffoldMessengerKey; fcmService.onForegroundMessage wired to a controllable stream.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Emit RemoteMessage(notification: title 'Hola', body 'Mensaje nuevo')
  2. pump and advance ~100ms
- **Esperado:** SnackBar visible showing both 'Hola' and 'Mensaje nuevo' (SCENARIO-652).

### notifications-43 — Foreground SnackBar 'Ver' action navigates to the deep link
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

- **Pasos:**
  1. Emit a message with deepLink '/coach/chat/chat-1?other=uid-xyz'
  2. Invoke the SnackBar action onPressed directly
  3. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach/chat/chat-1?other=uid-xyz') called once (SCENARIO-653).

### notifications-44 — Foreground SnackBar action with no deepLink falls back to /coach

  2. Invoke the SnackBar action onPressed
  3. pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach') called once (SCENARIO-654) — missing payload field is contained.

### notifications-45 — Foreground SnackBar uses a 4-second duration

### notifications-47 — No SnackBar appears when the foreground stream emits nothing

### notifications-48 — Foreground message with notification == null (data-only push) shows an empty-content SnackBar without crashing

### notifications-49 — Foreground SnackBar action is a no-op when no router context is available
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Handler whose _routerContext is null (e.g. action invoked after dispose / before first build context capture).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Drive the handler so the action fires with a null routerCtx (simulate via direct handler unit harness)
  2. Invoke action onPressed
- **Esperado:** goDeepLink is not called and no navigation occurs (early return on null routerCtx) — guards against navigating on a dead tree (ADR-PN-010).

### notifications-50 — Background tap (onMessageOpenedApp) with a deepLink navigates to it

- **Esperado:** router.go called once for each path respectively — repeated taps are not coalesced or dropped.

### notifications-54 — Cold-start getInitialMessage with a deepLink navigates after the first frame

- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach/trainer/uid-1') called once after the frame (SCENARIO-657) — navigation waits until GoRouter is mounted.

### notifications-55 — Cold-start getInitialMessage returning null performs no navigation
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** App harness; getInitialMessage returns null; onMessageOpenedApp empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** router.go never called (SCENARIO-658) — normal launch is unaffected.

### notifications-56 — Cold-start with an invalid deepLink falls back to /coach
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** App harness; getInitialMessage returns deepLink 'no-leading-slash'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and pumpAndSettle
- **Esperado:** router.go('/coach') called once — invalid cold-start payload contained.

### notifications-57 — Module behavior is identical for athlete and trainer accounts (role-agnostic token + permission flow)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator seed with both an athlete and a coach/trainer account; module wired in the home shell.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in as athlete; complete profile; grant permission; verify a token is written to users/{athleteUid}.fcmTokens
  2. Sign out; sign in as trainer; complete profile; grant permission; verify a token is written to users/{trainerUid}.fcmTokens
- **Esperado:** Both roles register tokens via the same code path; PermissionGate, init/dispose, and SnackBar behavior are identical — no role branching exists in this module. Only the resolved deep-link targets differ (handled downstream by the router).

### notifications-58 — Sign-out before a permission grant completes does not register a token for the signed-out user
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** On a real/instrumented session, user authenticated with completed profile; PermissionGate about to fire.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Trigger PermissionGate so requestPermission begins
  2. Sign out before the OS prompt resolves
  3. Resolve the prompt as authorized
- **Esperado:** Post-grant init is skipped because authStateChangesProvider.future yields null after sign-out (the explicit null-user guard) — no orphan token saved for the just-signed-out uid.

### notifications-59 — Real device permission prompt grant end-to-end registers and later removes the token
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Physical iOS device (APNS provisions only on real hardware), athlete account, emulator/staging Firestore reachable.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in and complete profile
  2. Tap Allow on the native notification prompt
  3. Inspect users/{uid}.fcmTokens in Firestore
  4. Sign out
- **Esperado:** A non-empty FCM token appears in fcmTokens after grant; on sign-out that exact token is removed via arrayRemove — full device lifecycle works (cannot be simulated; iOS Simulator throws apns-token-not-set).

### notifications-60 — Real push delivered while app is foregrounded shows the in-app SnackBar and its action deep-links
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Physical device with notifications granted; app in foreground; ability to send a test FCM push with a deepLink.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Send a push with title/body and data.deepLink='/coach?tab=agenda'
  2. Observe the in-app SnackBar
  3. Tap 'Ver'
- **Esperado:** SnackBar appears with the push title/body; tapping 'Ver' navigates to /coach?tab=agenda — validates the live onMessage stream wiring that mocks cannot.

# Módulo: payments

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/payments/. The module has no presentation/ of its own — UI lives in coach (trainer_dashboard_tab.dart: "PAGOS POR COBRAR" list + "+ Cobro suelto" sheet + "¿Marcar como cobrado?" dialog; athlete_coach_view.dart: "TU CUOTA" + alias; athlete_detail_screen.dart: "COBRO" config sheet). Core logic is in 3 derived providers (pagosPorCobrarProvider, miCuotaProvider, athleteBillingProvider) plus 2 repos and 2 freezed domain models. Existing tests cover only the porSesion acceptedAt floor and the ISO-week period key; everything below is net-new. Money flows offline (athlete pays to alias, trainer confirms) — miCuota is read-only by design. Key invariants: recurring charges dedup by periodKey (monthKey YYYY-MM / ISO weekKey YYYY-Www using owning year); porSesion counts finished sessions after max(link.acceptedAt, lastPaidAt) and is sharedWithTrainer-gated on the trainer side only; one-off pendings surface regardless of cadence; amounts are ints that must be > 0._

### payments-01 — Payment.fromJson/toJson round-trips all fields incl. timestamps and enum
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure unit).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a Map with id, trainerId, athleteId, amountArs:5000, concept, status:'paid', periodKey:'2026-06', createdAt and paidAt as Firestore Timestamps.
  2. Call Payment.fromJson(map).
  3. Call .toJson() on the result.
- **Esperado:** fromJson maps status->PaymentStatus.paid, amountArs->5000 (int), periodKey preserved, TimestampConverter yields DateTime for createdAt/paidAt; toJson re-emits 'paid' for status and Timestamps for the dates, lossless for the parsed fields.

### payments-02 — Payment.fromJson defaults: pending status, null periodKey and paidAt allowed
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build minimal Map with required fields, status:'pending', createdAt only (no periodKey, no paidAt).
  2. Call Payment.fromJson(map).
- **Esperado:** Parses to PaymentStatus.pending with periodKey==null and paidAt==null; no exception.

### payments-03 — AthleteBilling.fromJson maps all four cadence JsonValues
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. For each cadence string 'mensual','semanal','por_sesion','suelto' build a billing Map with amountArs and updatedAt Timestamp.
  2. Call AthleteBilling.fromJson on each.
- **Esperado:** Maps to BillingCadence.mensual / .semanal / .porSesion / .suelto respectively; amountArs is int; updatedAt is a DateTime.

### payments-04 — PaymentRepository.add writes auto-id and stamps it into the doc body
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore instance.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Construct PaymentRepository(firestore: fake).
  2. Call add(Payment(id:'', ... status:pending)).
  3. Read back the single doc from collection('payments').
- **Esperado:** One doc exists under payments/{autoId}; its 'id' field equals the generated ref.id (not empty string), and remaining fields match the payment's toJson.

### payments-05 — PaymentRepository.markPaid sets status=paid and paidAt (UTC) without touching other fields
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with a pending payment doc.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a pending payment via add().
  2. Call markPaid(id, DateTime(2026,6,16,10,0) local).
  3. Read the doc back.
- **Esperado:** status becomes 'paid'; paidAt stored as Timestamp equal to the UTC-converted instant; amountArs/concept/trainerId/athleteId unchanged.

### payments-06 — watchForTrainer streams only the trainer's payments
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with payments for trainerA and trainerB.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed 2 payments with trainerId='tA' and 1 with trainerId='tB'.
  2. Listen to watchForTrainer('tA').first.
- **Esperado:** Emits a list of exactly the 2 tA payments; tB payment excluded.

### payments-07 — watchForAthlete streams only the athlete's payments
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with payments for athleteA and athleteB.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed payments for athleteId='aA' (x2) and 'aB' (x1).
  2. Listen to watchForAthlete('aA').first.
- **Esperado:** Emits exactly the 2 aA payments; aB excluded.

### payments-08 — Repository skips unparseable payment docs instead of throwing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with one valid payment and one malformed doc (e.g. amountArs as a String, or missing required field) under the same trainerId.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a valid payment and a malformed doc directly via collection().add({...}).
  2. Listen to watchForTrainer(trainerId).first.
- **Esperado:** Stream emits a list containing only the valid payment; the malformed doc is silently dropped (logged via developer.log), no exception surfaces to the listener.

### payments-09 — BillingRepository uses deterministic doc id {trainerId}_{athleteId}
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call setConfig(AthleteBilling(trainerId:'tA', athleteId:'aA', amountArs:7000, cadence:mensual, ...)).
  2. Inspect collection('athlete_billing') doc ids.
- **Esperado:** Exactly one doc with id 'tA_aA' containing the serialized billing fields.

### payments-10 — BillingRepository.setConfig merges (does not clobber) existing config
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with an existing tA_aA doc carrying an extra field.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pre-seed athlete_billing/tA_aA with the billing fields plus an unrelated field 'extra':1.
  2. Call setConfig with a new amountArs/cadence for the same pair.
  3. Read the doc.
- **Esperado:** amountArs and cadence are updated; the unrelated 'extra' field is preserved (SetOptions(merge:true) behavior).

### payments-11 — BillingRepository.watch emits null when no config doc exists
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Listen to watch('tA','aA').first without seeding any doc.
- **Esperado:** Stream emits null (not an error, not an empty object).

### payments-12 — athleteBillingProvider returns null stream when no trainer is authenticated
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUidProvider overridden to null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override currentUidProvider => null.
  2. Read athleteBillingProvider('aA') and await its value.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to data(null) without hitting the repository.

### payments-13 — trainerPaymentsProvider yields empty list when unauthenticated
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUidProvider => null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override currentUidProvider => null.
  2. Read trainerPaymentsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to const [] (empty list), repository.watchForTrainer never invoked.

### payments-14 — athletePaymentsProvider yields empty list when unauthenticated
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUidProvider => null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override currentUidProvider => null.
  2. Read athletePaymentsProvider.future.
- **Esperado:** Resolves to const [].

### payments-15 — pagosPorCobrar returns empty when trainer has no active links
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer; trainerLinksStreamProvider overridden with only pending/ended links (no active).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override trainerLinksStreamProvider to emit links all with status != active.
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider after settling.
- **Esperado:** AsyncValue.data([]) — no per-athlete streams subscribed.

### payments-16 — pagosPorCobrar: mensual charge appears when this month is unpaid
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** One active link aA; athleteBilling(aA)=mensual amount 7000; no paid payment for current monthKey.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed billing mensual/7000 and trainerPayments=[] (or only prior-month paid).
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider after settling.
- **Esperado:** Exactly one CobroPendiente for aA, cadence mensual, amountArs 7000, concept 'Mensual <Month> <Year>'.

### payments-17 — pagosPorCobrar: mensual suppressed once a paid payment exists for current monthKey
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA; billing mensual; a paid Payment with periodKey == current YYYY-MM.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed billing mensual and a paid payment whose periodKey equals current month key.
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider after settling.
- **Esperado:** No mensual CobroPendiente for aA (deduped by periodKey).

### payments-18 — pagosPorCobrar: semanal charge keys off ISO weekKey, suppressed when current week paid
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA; billing semanal; toggle a paid payment with periodKey == isoWeekPeriodKey(now).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Case A: no paid week payment -> read provider.
  2. Case B: add paid payment with periodKey == current isoWeekPeriodKey -> read provider.
- **Esperado:** Case A emits one semanal CobroPendiente (concept 'Semana NN'); Case B emits none.

### payments-19 — pagosPorCobrar: porSesion counts finished sessions after acceptedAt floor
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA with acceptedAt set and sharedWithTrainer=true; billing porSesion amount 3000; sessions before and after acceptedAt.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed 2 finished sessions before acceptedAt and 3 after; no paid payments.
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider after settling.
- **Esperado:** One porSesion CobroPendiente: sessionsCount==3, amountArs==9000, concept '3 sesiones'.

### payments-20 — pagosPorCobrar: porSesion floor advances to latest paidAt after a payment
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA (acceptedAt earlier); billing porSesion 3000; a paid porSesion payment with paidAt; sessions before and after that paidAt.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed a paid payment with paidAt=T; seed 1 finished session before T and 2 after T.
  2. Read provider after settling.
- **Esperado:** Count==2 (only sessions finished after the latest paidAt), amountArs==6000.

### payments-21 — pagosPorCobrar: porSesion skipped (uncountable) when link.sharedWithTrainer is false
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA with sharedWithTrainer=false; billing porSesion; finished sessions exist.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override link with sharedWithTrainer=false; seed finished post-acceptedAt sessions.
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider after settling.
- **Esperado:** No porSesion CobroPendiente for aA (sessions can't be counted without share consent); not surfaced as an amount owed.

### payments-22 — pagosPorCobrar: only finished sessions with a finishedAt are counted
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active shared link aA; billing porSesion; mix of in-progress sessions, finished-without-finishedAt, and finished-with-finishedAt after acceptedAt.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed sessions: 1 in-progress, 1 finished but finishedAt==null, 2 finished with finishedAt after acceptedAt.
  2. Read provider after settling.
- **Esperado:** Count==2 (non-finished and null-finishedAt sessions excluded).

### payments-23 — pagosPorCobrar: one-off pending charges surface regardless of cadence/no-config
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA with NO billing config; a pending one-off Payment for aA.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override athleteBilling(aA)=null; seed one pending payment amount 1500 concept 'Clase suelta'.
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider after settling.
- **Esperado:** One CobroPendiente cadence suelto, amountArs 1500, concept 'Clase suelta', pendingPaymentIds==[that id].

### payments-24 — pagosPorCobrar: multiple one-off pendings aggregate into one suelto row
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA; 3 pending one-off payments (1000,2000,500) for aA.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed 3 pending payments for aA.
  2. Read provider after settling.
- **Esperado:** One suelto CobroPendiente: amountArs==3500, concept '3 cobros pendientes', pendingPaymentIds has all 3 ids.

### payments-25 — pagosPorCobrar: suelto config produces no recurring charge (only one-offs)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA; billing cadence suelto; no pending one-off payments.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed billing suelto; trainerPayments=[].
  2. Read provider after settling.
- **Esperado:** No CobroPendiente for aA (suelto has no recurring charge and there are no pending one-offs).

### payments-26 — pagosPorCobrar: athlete with no billing config and no pendings is skipped
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA; athleteBilling(aA)=null; no payments.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override athleteBilling(aA)=null; trainerPayments=[].
  2. Read provider after settling.
- **Esperado:** Result list does not include aA.

### payments-27 — pagosPorCobrar: results are sorted by athleteId for stable ordering
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true

- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed billing mensual for both athletes; ensure both produce a charge.
  2. Read provider after settling.
- **Esperado:** Returned list ordered aA before aZ (sorted by athleteId).

### payments-28 — pagosPorCobrar: surfaces error only when links stream errors with no prior value
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** trainerLinksStreamProvider overridden to emit an error before any value.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override trainerLinksStreamProvider with a stream that errors immediately.
  2. Read pagosPorCobrarProvider.
- **Esperado:** AsyncValue.error propagated (not data); error/stackTrace match the links error.

### payments-29 — pagosPorCobrar: stays loading while a per-athlete billing stream is loading and no results yet
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Active link aA; athleteBilling(aA) kept in loading; no one-off pendings.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Provide active link and trainer payments as data; leave athleteBillingProvider(aA) unresolved.
  2. Read provider value immediately.
- **Esperado:** AsyncValue.loading() (anyLoading && results.isEmpty).

### payments-30 — miCuota returns data(null) when athlete has no active trainer link

- **Pasos:**
  1. Override currentAthleteLinkProvider => null (then separately => ended link).
  2. Read miCuotaProvider after settling each.
- **Esperado:** Both cases resolve to AsyncValue.data(null) — section renders nothing.

### payments-31 — miCuota stays loading while the link is still loading with no value

  1. Override link provider to never complete; read miCuotaProvider immediately.
- **Esperado:** AsyncValue.loading().

### payments-39 — isoWeekPeriodKey uses ISO owning-year across New Year boundary

  2. Assert (2024-12-30)=='2025-W01' and (2026-01-01)=='2026-W01'.
- **Esperado:** Matches existing regression expectations; same physical ISO week maps to one key so weekly charges don't double-bill at year-end.
