### payments-61 — Firestore rules: athlete cannot read another athlete's payments
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Firebase emulator with rules; payments doc for athleteB; athleteA authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As athleteA, attempt to read a payment where athleteId == athleteB.
  2. Attempt watchForAthlete with athleteA's uid.
- **Esperado:** Cross-athlete read denied by rules; athleteA only sees payments where athleteId == auth.uid. (Needs emulator + auth — manual/integration.)

### payments-62 — Firestore rules: only the owning trainer may write payments and billing config
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator with rules; trainerA and trainerB accounts; athlete aA.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As trainerB, attempt to create a payment with trainerId==trainerA.
  2. As trainerB, attempt setConfig on athlete_billing/trainerA_aA.
  3. As athlete aA, attempt to write athlete_billing/trainerA_aA.
- **Esperado:** All three writes denied; only trainerA can create payments under their own trainerId and write their own billing docs; athlete read-only on billing. (Needs emulator + auth.)

# Módulo: performance

_Test-case catalog for lib/features/performance/ (PerformanceTest domain model, PerformanceTestRepository over Firestore, performanceTestsForAthleteProvider, LogPerformanceTestScreen, PerformanceProgressChart) plus its main consumer surface, the RENDIMIENTO section in coach/athlete_detail_screen.dart. Performance tests are logged by trainers for athletes and queried by recordedBy=trainerUid (athleteId filtered client-side). Key invariants covered: id auto-generation on add, comma/dot decimal parsing, all-optional fields, UTC recordedAt, ascending sort, ≥2-points gating for the chart and per-metric availability, malformed-doc skipping, no-auth save guard, and the cross-trainer visibility rule. Note: repo.watchForAthlete and repo.delete exist but are not wired to any provider/UI (flagged as dead-code regression candidates). No existing tests under test/features/performance/. Stack uses fake_cloud_firestore for repo tests and ProviderScope overrides for widget tests, so nearly everything is automatable._

### performance-01 — Repository.add() generates an id and persists the document
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore; PerformanceTestRepository constructed with it.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a PerformanceTest with id: '' , athleteId: 'athlete1', recordedBy: 'trainer1', recordedAt set, and a couple of numeric metrics (e.g. cmjCm: 30).
  2. Call repo.add(test) and await the returned model.
  3. Read the performance_tests collection from the fake Firestore.
- **Esperado:** Returned model has a non-empty id equal to the generated doc id. Exactly one doc exists in performance_tests; its stored body round-trips to the same athleteId, recordedBy, and metric values. The persisted doc id matches the returned model's id.

### performance-02 — Repository.add() persists recordedAt as a Firestore Timestamp and round-trips via fromJson
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore; repo constructed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a PerformanceTest with recordedAt = DateTime.utc(2026, 4, 7, 10, 30).
  2. Call repo.add(test).
  3. Re-read the doc and decode with PerformanceTest.fromJson({...data, 'id': docId}).
- **Esperado:** The decoded recordedAt equals 2026-04-07 10:30 UTC (TimestampConverter round-trips correctly, no off-by-timezone drift).

### performance-03 — watchRecordedBy emits only tests recorded by the given trainer
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with 2 tests by recordedBy='trainer1' and 1 test by recordedBy='trainer2'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repo.watchRecordedBy('trainer1').
  2. Read the first emission.
- **Esperado:** Stream emits a list of exactly the 2 tests whose recordedBy == 'trainer1'; the trainer2 test is excluded.

### performance-04 — watchRecordedBy reflects live add/delete changes
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Empty FakeFirebaseFirestore; repo constructed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repo.watchRecordedBy('trainer1').
  2. Call repo.add(test with recordedBy='trainer1', id='') and capture the returned id.
  3. Call repo.delete(returnedId).
- **Esperado:** Stream emits [] initially, then a list of length 1 after add, then [] again after delete.

### performance-05 — _fromDoc skips a malformed document instead of breaking the whole list
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with one valid test doc (recordedBy='trainer1') and one doc under performance_tests with recordedBy='trainer1' but a corrupt field type that breaks fromJson (e.g. recordedAt as a String or cmjCm as a non-numeric String).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repo.watchRecordedBy('trainer1').
  2. Read the first emission.
- **Esperado:** Stream emits a list of length 1 containing only the valid test; the unparseable doc is silently dropped (logged, not thrown). No exception propagates to the stream.

### performance-06 — delete() removes the document by id
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with one test doc of known id 'doc1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repo.delete('doc1').
  2. Read the performance_tests collection.
- **Esperado:** Doc 'doc1' no longer exists; collection is empty. Deleting a non-existent id does not throw.

### performance-07 — watchForAthlete filters by athleteId (currently unwired repo method)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with 2 tests for athleteId='athlete1' (recorded by different trainers) and 1 for athleteId='athlete2'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to repo.watchForAthlete('athlete1').
  2. Read the first emission.
- **Esperado:** Stream emits exactly the 2 athlete1 tests regardless of recordedBy; athlete2 test excluded. Guards behavior of this method, which is not yet consumed by any provider/UI.

### performance-08 — performanceTestsForAthleteProvider returns empty stream when no trainer is authenticated
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with currentUidProvider overridden to null and performanceTestRepositoryProvider overridden by a repo over FakeFirebaseFirestore that contains tests.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read performanceTestsForAthleteProvider('athlete1') from the container.
  2. Await the first value.
- **Esperado:** Provider resolves to an empty list (const []) without querying Firestore; no error state.

### performance-09 — performanceTestsForAthleteProvider scopes by current trainer AND athlete, sorted ascending
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with: trainer1 tests for athlete1 dated 2026-03-01, 2026-01-01, 2026-02-01; a trainer1 test for athlete2; a trainer2 test for athlete1. currentUidProvider overridden to 'trainer1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read performanceTestsForAthleteProvider('athlete1').
  2. Await the first emitted list.
- **Esperado:** List contains only trainer1's athlete1 tests (the athlete2 test and the trainer2 test are excluded), ordered ascending by recordedAt: Jan, Feb, Mar.

### performance-10 — INVARIANT: a test recorded by a different trainer for the same athlete is invisible to the current trainer
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with one test athleteId='athlete1', recordedBy='trainer2'. currentUidProvider overridden to 'trainer1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read performanceTestsForAthleteProvider('athlete1') as trainer1.
  2. Await first value.
- **Esperado:** Empty list. Confirms the query keys on recordedBy=currentTrainer, so cross-trainer data does not leak even when athleteId matches.

### performance-11 — Log form save creates a test with all optional metrics null when nothing is entered
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget test pumping LogPerformanceTestScreen(athleteId:'athlete1') inside ProviderScope; currentUidProvider overridden to 'trainer1'; performanceTestRepositoryProvider over FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the screen without entering any field.
  2. Tap 'GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN'.
  3. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** One doc is written with athleteId='athlete1', recordedBy='trainer1', a non-null recordedAt, all metric fields null and notes null. Screen pops and an 'Evaluación guardada' snackbar shows.

### performance-12 — Log form maps each entered numeric field to its correct model property
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped as in performance-11.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter values in a representative spread of fields: CMJ=32.5, Sprint 20m=2.8, Sentadilla(1RM)=140, VO2máx=55, notes='buena sesión'.
  2. Tap 'GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN' and settle.
  3. Read back the persisted doc.
- **Esperado:** Persisted test has cmjCm=32.5, sprint20mS=2.8, squat1rmKg=140, vo2maxMlKgMin=55, notes='buena sesión', and every untouched metric null. No field crosswiring.

### performance-13 — Decimal parsing accepts comma as decimal separator
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated, repo over FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '32,5' (comma) into the CMJ field.
  2. Save and read back the doc.
- **Esperado:** cmjCm == 32.5 (comma normalized to dot by _parseDouble before double.tryParse).

### performance-14 — Invalid / malformed numeric input is stored as null, not a parse error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter 'abc' into the CMJ field and '  ' (whitespace) into Sprint 10m.
  2. Save and read back the doc.
- **Esperado:** Save succeeds; cmjCm is null and sprint10mS is null (double.tryParse returns null; trimmed-empty returns null). No exception, no validation block.

### performance-15 — Zero and boundary numeric values are persisted (not coerced to null)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter '0' in CMJ and a large value like '999.9' in Sentadilla 1RM.
  2. Save and read back.
- **Esperado:** cmjCm == 0.0 (zero is a valid value, distinct from null/unset) and squat1rmKg == 999.9.

### performance-16 — Notes containing only whitespace are stored as null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Type '   ' (spaces only) into the NOTAS field.
  2. Save and read back.
- **Esperado:** Persisted notes is null (trimmed-empty collapses to null), not an empty/whitespace string.

### performance-17 — recordedAt is persisted in UTC at save time
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Save the form (any or no metrics).
  2. Read back the persisted recordedAt.
- **Esperado:** recordedAt.isUtc is true and is close to now (within test tolerance). Confirms DateTime.now().toUtc() is used so stored value matches the UTC display convention.

### performance-18 — Save is blocked and a snackbar shows when no trainer session is active
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped with currentUidProvider overridden to null; repo over FakeFirebaseFirestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the screen.
  2. Verify the GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN button is disabled (canSave=false).
  3. Attempt to invoke save.
- **Esperado:** Save button is disabled. If save runs, no doc is written and a 'No hay sesión activa. No se puede guardar.' snackbar appears. Screen does not pop.

### performance-19 — Save button shows spinner and is disabled while saving (re-entrancy guard)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated; repo whose add Future is held pending (controllable).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN.
  2. Pump one frame (do not settle).
  3. Attempt to tap the button again.
- **Esperado:** A CircularProgressIndicator replaces the label, button is disabled, and the second tap is a no-op (_saving guard prevents a duplicate add).

### performance-20 — Save failure resets saving state and shows an error snackbar without popping
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated; performanceTestRepositoryProvider overridden with a repo whose add() throws.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN.
  2. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** A 'No pudimos guardar la evaluación. Probá de nuevo.' snackbar shows; the screen stays open; the button is re-enabled (_saving reset to false) so the user can retry.

### performance-21 — Cancel button dismisses the form without writing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pushed onto a navigator inside ProviderScope; trainer authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter a value in CMJ.
  2. Tap 'Cancelar'.
- **Esperado:** Screen pops; no doc written to performance_tests.

### performance-22 — Cancel is disabled while a save is in flight
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped, trainer authenticated, repo add pending.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN.
  2. Pump one frame.
  3. Tap 'Cancelar'.
- **Esperado:** Cancel onPressed is null while _saving; tapping it does not pop the screen.

### performance-23 — Form header date renders in UTC and matches the persisted record near midnight
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** LogPerformanceTestScreen pumped (header derives from DateTime.now().toUtc()).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the screen.
  2. Read the header subtitle date text.
- **Esperado:** Header date string is formatted from a UTC instant (no toLocal()), so it agrees with the recordedAt that will be saved even across a local/UTC day boundary. (Best asserted with a fixed clock; otherwise verify formatting shape '<d> <mes> <yyyy> · HH:MM'.)

### performance-24 — PerformanceProgressChart only offers metrics that have >=2 non-null data points
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with 3 tests where CMJ is present in all 3, Sprint20m present in only 1, and Sentadilla1RM present in 2.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the chart widget.
  2. Inspect the metric chip row.
- **Esperado:** Chips are shown for CMJ and Sentadilla 1RM (>=2 points) but NOT for Sprint 20m (only 1 point). Default selected metric is the first available in display order.

### performance-25 — Chart falls back to the first metric when no metric has >=2 points
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with 2 tests that share no overlapping metric (e.g. test A has only CMJ, test B has only Cooper).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the chart.
  2. Inspect chips and the rendered line chart.
- **Esperado:** _buildAvailable returns the fallback [first metric], so one chip is shown; because the fallback metric has <2 points the LineChart is not rendered (points.length < 2 gate), but the widget builds without throwing.

### performance-26 — Selecting a metric chip switches the chart series
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with 3 tests where both CMJ and Sentadilla 1RM have >=2 points.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the chart (CMJ selected by default).
  2. Tap the 'Sentadilla 1RM' chip.
  3. Pump.
- **Esperado:** Sentadilla 1RM chip becomes selected (accent styling); the header value/unit switch to kg and reflect the latest Sentadilla value; the line chart updates to the Sentadilla series.

### performance-27 — Chart header computes delta and direction glyph between first and last point
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with tests where CMJ goes 30 -> 34 across two dates (sorted ascending).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the chart with CMJ selected.
  2. Read the header value, delta and glyph.
- **Esperado:** Current value shows 34 cm; delta shows '▲ 4.0 cm'; the span label reflects days/weeks between first and last recordedAt. A decreasing metric (e.g. sprint time 3.0 -> 2.8) shows '▼ 0.2 s'.

### performance-28 — Chart value formatting drops trailing .0 for integers and keeps one decimal otherwise
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with CMJ values 30.0 and 32.5.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump and read the header current value text.
- **Esperado:** Whole values render without decimals (e.g. '30'); fractional values render with one decimal (e.g. '32.5').

### performance-29 — Chart keeps current selection across rebuild when still valid, resets when not
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped; can rebuild parent with a new tests list.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Select 'Sentadilla 1RM'.
  2. Rebuild with a new tests list where Sentadilla 1RM still has >=2 points; verify selection.
  3. Rebuild again with a tests list where Sentadilla 1RM no longer qualifies (only CMJ does).
- **Esperado:** After the first rebuild Sentadilla 1RM remains selected (didUpdateWidget keeps a still-valid selection). After the second rebuild the selection resets to _available.first (CMJ).

### performance-30 — Chart handles a flat series (all equal values) without a zero-range crash
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with two tests where CMJ == 30 in both.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the chart with CMJ selected.
  2. Verify it renders.
- **Esperado:** Y padding defaults to 1.0 when range < 0.001, so minY/maxY differ and the LineChart renders without divide-by-zero or NaN; delta shows '▲ 0.0 cm'.

### performance-31 — Bottom-axis label thinning picks at most 4 dates for long series
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** PerformanceProgressChart pumped with 6+ tests all having the selected metric.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the chart.
  2. Inspect which date labels are rendered along the x-axis (via _labelIndices logic).
- **Esperado:** Exactly first and last indices plus ~2 evenly spaced interior indices are labeled (max 4 labels); with <=4 points all are labeled.

### performance-32 — RENDIMIENTO section shows loading card while the stream is pending
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Coach athlete_detail _RendimientoSection (or full screen) pumped with performanceTestsForAthleteProvider overridden to a never-completing/loading async value; trainer authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
  2. Read the content card before the stream emits.
- **Esperado:** A card with 'Cargando…' is shown.

### performance-33 — RENDIMIENTO section shows error card when the stream errors
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _RendimientoSection pumped with performanceTestsForAthleteProvider overridden to AsyncError.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
- **Esperado:** A card with 'No pudimos cargar las evaluaciones.' is shown; no crash.

### performance-34 — RENDIMIENTO section shows empty-state card when athlete has no tests
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _RendimientoSection pumped; provider resolves to an empty list.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
- **Esperado:** Card shows 'Sin evaluaciones todavía. Cargá la primera.'; no summary card and no chart are rendered.

### performance-35 — RENDIMIENTO summary card shows the latest (last, ASC-sorted) test and its non-null key metrics
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _RendimientoSection pumped; provider resolves to 2 ascending-sorted tests; the latest has cmjCm=34, squat1rmKg=140, sprint20mS null, vo2maxMlKgMin=55.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
  2. Inspect the summary card.
- **Esperado:** Summary card shows the latest test's date and metric rows only for non-null key metrics: 'CMJ 34 cm', 'Sentadilla 1RM 140 kg', 'VO2máx 55 ml/kg/min'; Sprint 20m row is absent (null).

### performance-36 — RENDIMIENTO count line pluralizes correctly
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _RendimientoSection pumped with provider data of length 1, then of length 3.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump with 1 test and read the count line.
  2. Pump with 3 tests and read the count line.
- **Esperado:** With 1 test: '1 evaluación registrada'. With 3 tests: '3 evaluaciones registradas'.

### performance-37 — RENDIMIENTO shows hint card instead of chart when fewer than 2 tests exist
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _RendimientoSection pumped; provider resolves to exactly 1 test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
- **Esperado:** Summary card is shown plus a card reading 'Cargá otra evaluación para ver el progreso.'; PerformanceProgressChart is NOT rendered.

### performance-38 — RENDIMIENTO renders the progress chart when >=2 tests exist
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** _RendimientoSection pumped; provider resolves to 3 ascending-sorted tests sharing at least one metric with >=2 points.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
- **Esperado:** A PerformanceProgressChart widget is present below the summary card (and the <2 hint card is absent).

### performance-39 — '+ Cargar' opens the log form as a fullscreen dialog for the correct athlete
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Coach athlete detail screen pumped with a navigator; trainer authenticated; athleteId='athlete1'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the '+ Cargar' action in the RENDIMIENTO header.
  2. Pump and settle.
- **Esperado:** LogPerformanceTestScreen is pushed (fullscreen dialog route) with athleteId='athlete1'; the form title 'Cargar evaluación' is visible.

### performance-40 — End-to-end: logging a test updates the RENDIMIENTO section live
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Full coach athlete detail screen + log form wired over a single FakeFirebaseFirestore via real performanceTestRepositoryProvider; currentUidProvider='trainer1'; athlete has 1 existing test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. From the detail screen tap '+ Cargar'.
  2. Enter CMJ=34 in the form and tap GUARDAR EVALUACIÓN.
  3. Settle back on the detail screen.
- **Esperado:** Form pops; the RENDIMIENTO summary now reflects the new latest test (CMJ 34) and the count becomes '2 evaluaciones registradas'; the PerformanceProgressChart now renders (>=2 tests). Confirms repo write -> watchRecordedBy stream -> provider -> UI flow end to end.

### performance-41 — Athlete-role user cannot reach the trainer-only log/RENDIMIENTO surface
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator/app with an athlete account signed in (role=athlete). RENDIMIENTO and the log form live under the Coach athlete-detail screen, which is a trainer surface.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Sign in as the athlete account.
  2. Attempt to navigate to a Coach athlete-detail route.
  3. Observe access.
- **Esperado:** The athlete is redirected/blocked by the coach route guard and never reaches LogPerformanceTestScreen or the RENDIMIENTO section. (Performance tests are trainer-authored; athlete self-view is not wired.) Verify against the router/role redirect for the coach area.

### performance-42 — Decimal keyboard and numeric input affordance on a real device
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** App running on an iOS device/simulator; trainer signed in; log form open.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap a numeric field (e.g. CMJ).
  2. Observe the keyboard.
  3. Type '32,5' / '32.5'.
- **Esperado:** A decimal numeric keyboard is presented (TextInputType.numberWithOptions(decimal:true)); locale comma input is accepted and parsed (matches performance-13). Manual because it depends on native keyboard/locale.

### performance-43 — Chart tooltip shows value+unit and date on touch (native gesture)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** App running on device; RENDIMIENTO chart visible with >=2 points.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Long-press / drag along the line chart over a data point.
- **Esperado:** A tooltip appears showing '<value> <unit>' and the short date (e.g. '34 cm\n7 abr'). Manual because fl_chart touch tooltips need real pointer interaction.

# Módulo: profile

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/profile/. Covers role-aware ProfileScreen routing (athlete vs trainer), athlete CUENTA/SESION/ENTRENADOR sections, stats row async states, personal-data edit form (validation + dual-write + dirty/discard), trainer public-profile edit (multi-location invariant, specialty/price/bio validation, onboarding vs edit mode), gym picker, assigned-routines list, account-deletion orchestration (re-auth, retry window, partial-with-auth-deleted), and the UserRepository dual-write privacy/immutability invariants. Existing tests use SCENARIO-NNN naming; these new cases target gaps and high-value regressions. False-automatable cases require native image picker, geolocation, real OAuth re-auth, or live Cloud Function._

### profile-01 — ProfileScreen renders athlete body when role is athlete
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Signed-in athlete account; userProfileProvider overridden to AsyncData(athlete profile).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ProfileScreen with userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile role=athlete).
  2. Settle the frame.
- **Esperado:** ProfileHeader ('TU CUENTA' / 'PERFIL'), ProfileAvatarCard, the 3-stat row, CUENTA section and SESION group render. TrainerProfileView ('YO' header) is NOT present.

### profile-02 — ProfileScreen renders TrainerProfileView when role is trainer
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Signed-in trainer account; userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile role=trainer); trainerLinksStreamProvider and trainerByIdProvider overridden with empty/null data.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ProfileScreen with role=trainer overrides.
  2. Settle the frame.
- **Esperado:** TrainerProfileView shows 'TU CUENTA'/'YO' header, identity card, PERFIL PUBLICO card; the athlete _AthleteProfile body (avatar card + 3-stat row) is NOT present.

### profile-03 — ProfileScreen defaults to athlete body while profile is loading/null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider = AsyncLoading (or AsyncData(null)).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ProfileScreen with userProfileProvider in loading state.
  2. Settle.
- **Esperado:** Falls back to _AthleteProfile (role null is treated as non-trainer). No exception; TrainerProfileView is not shown.

### profile-04 — Athlete stats row shows loading placeholders then real values
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Athlete profile; userSessionStatsProvider controllable (delayed future).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ProfileScreen (athlete) with userSessionStatsProvider pending.
  2. Assert placeholders.
  3. Complete the provider with UserSessionStats(totalSessions:143, totalVolumeKg:92000, streak:12).
  4. Settle.
- **Esperado:** While loading the three tiles show '--'. After data: SESIONES=143, VOLUMEN KG=92k (kFormat), RACHA=12.

### profile-05 — Athlete stats row shows '--' on error without crashing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Athlete profile; userSessionStatsProvider = AsyncError.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override userSessionStatsProvider to throw.
  2. Pump ProfileScreen (athlete) and settle.
- **Esperado:** All three stat tiles render '--' (error branch), screen does not throw or show a red error widget.

### profile-06 — userSessionStatsProvider returns zero stats for unauthenticated user
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider = null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read userSessionStatsProvider with currentUidProvider overridden to null.
  2. Await the value.
- **Esperado:** Returns UserSessionStats(totalSessions:0, totalVolumeKg:0, streak:0) and performs NO sessionRepository read.

### profile-07 — userSessionStatsProvider counts only finished sessions for volume and totalSessions
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** currentUidProvider set; sessionRepository.listByUid returns a mix of finished and non-finished (active/discarded) sessions.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Seed sessions: 2 finished (volume 100 + 200) and 1 active (volume 999).
  2. Override sessionRepositoryProvider with the fake.
  3. Await userSessionStatsProvider.
- **Esperado:** totalSessions=2, totalVolumeKg=300 (active session excluded). streak computed from full session list via computeStreak.

### profile-08 — Athlete CUENTA section renders 4 tiles in locked order
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Athlete profile loaded; friendship + assignedRoutines providers overridden.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ProfileCuentaSection within ProviderScope + l10n.
  2. Settle.
- **Esperado:** Tiles render in order: Solicitudes de amistad, Datos personales, Gimnasio, Mis rutinas. Historial tile is absent.

### profile-09 — CUENTA Solicitudes tile shows pending-request count subtitle only when > 0
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Athlete profile; pendingRequestCountProvider overridden.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render with pending count = 0; assert no count subtitle.
  2. Re-render with pending count = 3; assert subtitle shows the count.
- **Esperado:** Subtitle is null/hidden when count is 0; shows the localized '3' solicitudes subtitle when count is 3.

### profile-10 — CUENTA Gimnasio tile subtitle reflects gymId vs no-gym
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Athlete profile with and without gymId.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render CUENTA with profile.gymId = null; assert 'no gym' subtitle.
  2. Render with gymId set to a known catalog id; assert gymNameFromId(gymId) subtitle.
- **Esperado:** With null gymId shows the no-gym label; with a valid gymId shows the resolved gym name.

### profile-11 — CUENTA tiles navigate to correct routes on tap
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProfileCuentaSection inside a GoRouter test harness capturing pushes.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap each tile (Solicitudes, Datos personales, Gimnasio, Mis rutinas).
- **Esperado:** Pushes /profile/friend-requests, /profile/edit-personal, /profile/gym, /profile/routines respectively.

### profile-12 — assignedRoutinesCountProvider returns list length on data, 0 on loading/error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** assignedRoutinesProvider(uid) overridable.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override assignedRoutinesProvider(uid) to AsyncData([r1,r2,r3]); read count.
  2. Override to AsyncLoading; read count.
  3. Override to AsyncError; read count.
- **Esperado:** Returns 3 on data; 0 on loading; 0 on error (no flicker / no throw).

### profile-13 — ENTRENADOR section is hidden for athlete role
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile role=athlete).
- **Pasos:**

- **Esperado:** Renders SizedBox.shrink — 'ENTRENADOR' label and 'Mi perfil de entrenador' tile are NOT present.

### profile-14 — ENTRENADOR section shows 'Perfil completo' when all trainer fields present
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile with trainerBio non-empty, trainerSpecialty set, trainerMonthlyRate set, and (trainerLocations non-empty OR trainerOffersOnline true).

### profile-15 — ENTRENADOR section lists each missing field in subtitle
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  2. Settle.
- **Esperado:** Subtitle is 'Faltan: bio, especialidad, precio, ubicación o clases virtuales' (all four missing tokens, in that order).

### profile-16 — trainerProfileComplete getter is true only when bio+specialty+rate+location/online all satisfied
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure domain).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert false when any of trainerBio/trainerSpecialty/trainerMonthlyRate is null.
  2. Assert false when locations empty AND offersOnline false.
  3. Assert true when bio+specialty+rate set AND locations non-empty (online false).
  4. Assert true when bio+specialty+rate set AND offersOnline true (no locations).
- **Esperado:** trainerProfileComplete returns the documented boolean for each combination (ADR-TPO-004).

### profile-17 — trainerProfileCompleteProvider returns false for athlete/loading/null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider overridable.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set userProfileProvider to AsyncData(athlete); read provider.
  2. Set to AsyncLoading; read.
  3. Set to AsyncData(null); read.
- **Esperado:** Returns false in all three cases (defaults to false when profile is null or non-trainer).

### profile-20 — Personal edit: displayName over 50 chars blocked
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Edit screen seeded.

  2. Tap GUARDAR.

### profile-21 — Personal edit: bodyWeightKg boundary and malformed validation
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Edit screen seeded.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Enter weight '0' → save → expect out-of-range error.
  2. Enter '29' → expect out-of-range (min 30).
  3. Enter '301' → expect out-of-range (max 300).
  4. Enter 'abc' → expect invalid-number error.
  5. Enter '30' and '300' → expect valid (no error).
  6. Leave blank → expect valid (nullable).
- **Esperado:** Weight rejected for 0, 29, 301, and non-numeric; accepted for 30, 300, and blank. Comma decimals are normalized ('72,5' parses).

  4. Enter '120' and '230' → valid.

### profile-79 — UserRepository.update strips immutable fields and stamps updatedAt
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore with an existing users/{uid} doc.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call update(uid, {'uid':'x','role':'trainer','email':'e','createdAt':<ts>,'displayName':'New'}).
  2. Read back the doc.
- **Esperado:** uid/role/email/createdAt are NOT modified; displayName is updated; updatedAt is overwritten with a fresh server timestamp.

### profile-80 — UserRepository.update dual-writes userPublicProfiles for public fields with derived lowercase
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call update(uid, {'displayName':'Ana Núñez'}).
  2. Read userPublicProfiles/{uid}.
- **Esperado:** Public doc gets displayName='Ana Núñez', displayNameLowercase='ana núñez', and uid folded in (satisfies first-write CREATE rule). users doc also updated in the same batch.

### profile-81 — UserRepository.update does NOT touch trainerPublicProfiles for athlete-only fields
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call update(uid, {'displayName':'Ana'}).
  2. Check trainerPublicProfiles/{uid}.
- **Esperado:** No trainerPublicProfiles write occurs (regression guard: athlete ProfileSetup sending displayName must NOT trigger a denied trainer batch write — PR #58 bug).

### profile-82 — UserRepository.update dual-writes trainerPublicProfiles for trainer fields
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call update(uid, {'trainerBio':'b','trainerSpecialty':'strength','trainerMonthlyRate':7000,'trainerLocations':[loc],'trainerGeohashes':['gh'],'trainerOffersOnline':true}).
  2. Read trainerPublicProfiles/{uid}.
- **Esperado:** Trainer public doc receives the trainer fields plus uid; users doc also updated. averageRating/reviewCount are NOT written by the client.

### profile-83 — UserRepository.update rejects invalid trainer location state via ArgumentError
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call update(uid, {'trainerLocations':[], 'trainerOffersOnline':false}).
- **Esperado:** Throws ArgumentError before any write (server-side invariant mirror of the client block); no Firestore mutation.

### profile-84 — UserRepository.update with only non-public fields performs single users write
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call update(uid, {'bodyWeightKg':80}).
  2. Inspect writes.
- **Esperado:** Only users/{uid} is written (no userPublicProfiles or trainerPublicProfiles write) since no public/trainer field is present.

### profile-85 — UserRepository.watch ignores cold-cache exists=false but emits server-confirmed absence
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore / controllable snapshot metadata.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Emit a from-cache snapshot with exists=false → assert no null emitted.
  2. Emit a server snapshot with exists=false → assert null emitted.
  3. Emit a server snapshot with a profile → assert profile emitted.
- **Esperado:** Stream filters out cache-only absence (prevents bouncing existing users to /profile-setup); only server-confirmed absence yields null.

### profile-86 — UserRepository.getOrCreate creates users + userPublicProfiles atomically with null displayName
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore, empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call getOrCreate(uid, email).
  2. Read both collections.
- **Esperado:** users/{uid} created with displayName=null, role=athlete; userPublicProfiles/{uid} created in the same batch with uid + null public fields. REQ-UPP-009.

### profile-87 — UserRepository.getOrCreate returns existing profile without re-writing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** fake_cloud_firestore with an existing users/{uid}.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call getOrCreate(uid, email) for the existing uid.
- **Esperado:** Returns the existing UserProfile unchanged; no overwrite of createdAt/displayName.

### profile-88 — UserRepository.delete always throws UnsupportedError
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call repository.delete(uid).
- **Esperado:** Throws UnsupportedError (client deletion forbidden; account deletion only via privileged CF).

### profile-89 — userProfileProvider emits null for unauthenticated and switches stream on auth change
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authStateChangesProvider controllable; userRepository.watch mocked.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set auth to null → read provider value.
  2. Set auth to a user → read provider value.
  3. Set auth to error → read provider value.
- **Esperado:** null user → stream of null; logged-in user → repository.watch(uid) stream; auth error → stream of null (no throw).

### profile-90 — userPublicProfileProvider is auth-gated and emits null when unauthenticated
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** authStateChangesProvider controllable; userPublicProfileRepository mocked.
- **Pasos:**
  1. With auth=null, read userPublicProfileProvider(uid).
  2. With auth set, read again.
- **Esperado:** Unauthenticated → yields null without hitting the repository; authenticated → yields the repository watch stream (null if doc absent).

### profile-91 — TrainerProfileView: ALUMNOS count reflects active links; pending badge shows pending count
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile; trainerLinksStreamProvider returns mix of active and pending links.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump TrainerProfileView with 2 active + 3 pending links.
  2. Settle.
- **Esperado:** Identity card ALUMNOS=2; 'Solicitudes entrantes' row shows badge '3'. With 0 pending, no badge is rendered.

### profile-92 — TrainerProfileView: VISIBLE/OCULTO badge and summary reflect public profile presence
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile; trainerByIdProvider returns null then a TrainerPublicProfile.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render with pub=null → assert OCULTO badge + 'Aún no creaste tu perfil público...' summary, VER PREVIEW disabled.
  2. Render with pub having locations + online → assert VISIBLE badge + 'Aparecés en Coach Discovery · Presencial · Online' summary, VER PREVIEW enabled.
- **Esperado:** Badge toggles VISIBLE/OCULTO; summary composes correctly; VER PREVIEW enabled only when visible and uid non-empty.

### profile-93 — TrainerProfileView: EDITAR navigates to /profile/edit-trainer; VER PREVIEW to /coach/trainer/:uid
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile visible (pub non-null); router captures pushes.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap EDITAR → assert push('/profile/edit-trainer').
  2. Tap VER PREVIEW → assert push('/coach/trainer/<uid>').
- **Esperado:** EDITAR always pushes the trainer edit route; VER PREVIEW pushes the public preview when visible.

### profile-94 — TrainerProfileView: initials derive correctly and fall back to '·'
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure helper behavior exercised via widget).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render with displayName 'Ana Núñez' → expect initials 'AN'.
  2. Render with single name 'Ana' → expect 'AN' (first 2 letters).
  3. Render with single char 'A' → expect 'A'.
  4. Render with empty name → expect '·' and fallback name 'Coach'.
- **Esperado:** Initials are 'AN', 'AN', 'A', and '·' respectively; empty displayName shows 'Coach'.

### profile-95 — TrainerProfileView: Disponibilidad disabled-toast when uid empty
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile but currentUidProvider null (uid empty).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap 'Disponibilidad' row.
- **Esperado:** Shows snackbar 'Iniciá sesión para configurar.' instead of navigating; with a non-empty uid it pushes /coach/availability-editor?trainerId=<uid>.

### profile-96 — TrainerProfileView: Cerrar sesión row calls signOut
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Trainer profile; authNotifierProvider mocked.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the 'Cerrar sesión' menu row.
- **Esperado:** authNotifier.signOut() called once.

### profile-97 — ProfileAvatarCard: data state shows name (uppercased), derived @handle, and gym chip
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider = AsyncData(profile with displayName='ana núñez', gymId set).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ProfileAvatarCard and settle.
- **Esperado:** Name renders uppercased ('ANA NÚÑEZ'); '@'+derived handle shown; gym chip (key profile_avatar_gym_chip) shown when gymId resolves to a name.

### profile-98 — ProfileAvatarCard: skeleton on loading, error, and null profile
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** userProfileProvider in loading, error, and AsyncData(null).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Render in each state and settle.
- **Esperado:** All three render the skeleton placeholder (no name text, no crash). Missing displayName in a non-null profile shows 'SIN NOMBRE'.

### profile-99 — TimestampConverter round-trips DateTime as UTC Timestamp
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. fromJson(Timestamp) → assert returned DateTime isUtc.
  2. toJson(DateTime) → assert Timestamp.fromDate equivalence.
- **Esperado:** fromJson converts to UTC; toJson produces a Timestamp matching the input instant. Round-trip preserves the moment.

### profile-100 — UserProfile.fromJson/toJson round-trips trainer multi-location and defaults
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Decode a JSON missing trainerLocations/trainerGeohashes/trainerOffersOnline.
  2. Decode a full trainer JSON with locations and online true, then re-encode.
- **Esperado:** Missing list/flag fields default to [] and false; full round-trip preserves trainerLocations, trainerGeohashes, and trainerOffersOnline. role/gender/experience enums map via wire values.

# Módulo: profile_setup

_Executable test-case catalog for the TREINO profile_setup onboarding module (4-step Riverpod flow: username/avatar, gym, experience/gender, weight/height, then Firestore submit). Covers per-step validation invariants (ProfileSetupDraft), pure validators, notifier navigation/field/submit logic, gym search, avatar upload failure tolerance, self-heal-on-submit, cancel-onboarding, and role/router gating. Existing coverage to avoid duplicating: profile_setup_notifier_test.dart (SCENARIO-265/266/268 submit-write/self-heal) and profile_setup_header_test.dart (2-line clamp + large text scale). New cases extend rather than repeat these. 48 cases total; ~38 automatable as widget/unit tests, the rest needing native gesture/image-picker/real-auth interaction._

### profile_setup-01 — Step1 isStep1Valid true for username with exactly 3 chars
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** No backend. Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Construct ProfileSetupDraft(username: 'abc').
  2. Read draft.isStep1Valid.
- **Esperado:** isStep1Valid is true (boundary: length == 3 passes).

### profile_setup-02 — Step1 isStep1Valid false for username under 3 chars after trim
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Construct ProfileSetupDraft(username: '  ab  ') (trims to 'ab', length 2).
  2. Read draft.isStep1Valid.
- **Esperado:** isStep1Valid is false (trimmed length 2 < 3).

### profile_setup-03 — Step1 isStep1Valid false for null and whitespace-only username
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert ProfileSetupDraft(username: null).isStep1Valid is false.
  2. Assert ProfileSetupDraft(username: '   ').isStep1Valid is false (trims to empty).
- **Esperado:** Both return false; avatar being null/absent does not affect step1 validity.

### profile_setup-04 — Step2 isStep2Valid true for both a catalog gymId and the kNoGymId sentinel
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test. Import kNoGymId from domain/gym.dart.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert ProfileSetupDraft(gymId: 'smart-fit-palermo').isStep2Valid is true.
  2. Assert ProfileSetupDraft(gymId: kNoGymId).isStep2Valid is true.
  3. Assert ProfileSetupDraft(gymId: null).isStep2Valid is false.
- **Esperado:** Any non-null gymId (including the 'no-gym' sentinel) satisfies step2; null does not.

### profile_setup-05 — Step3 isStep3Valid requires BOTH experienceLevel and gender
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert draft with only experienceLevel set (gender null) is invalid.
  2. Assert draft with only gender set (experienceLevel null) is invalid.
  3. Assert draft with both ExperienceLevel.beginner + Gender.female is valid.
- **Esperado:** isStep3Valid is true only when experienceLevel != null AND gender != null.

### profile_setup-06 — Step4 isStep4Valid weight boundary: 20 and 300 are rejected, mid-range accepted
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test. Height fixed valid (e.g. 170).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert weight 20.0 + height 170 -> invalid (rule is w > 20, exclusive).
  2. Assert weight 300.0 + height 170 -> invalid (rule is w < 300, exclusive).
  3. Assert weight 20.1 + height 170 -> valid.
  4. Assert weight 299.9 + height 170 -> valid.
- **Esperado:** Weight must be strictly between 20 and 300; exact boundaries fail.

### profile_setup-07 — Step4 isStep4Valid height boundary: 100 and 250 are rejected, mid-range accepted
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test. Weight fixed valid (e.g. 70).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert height 100 + weight 70 -> invalid (rule is h > 100, exclusive).
  2. Assert height 250 + weight 70 -> invalid (rule is h < 250, exclusive).
  3. Assert height 101 + weight 70 -> valid.
  4. Assert height 249 + weight 70 -> valid.
- **Esperado:** Height must be strictly between 100 and 250; exact boundaries fail.

### profile_setup-08 — Step4 isStep4Valid false when either weight or height is null
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert draft(bodyWeightKg: 70, heightCm: null) -> invalid.
  2. Assert draft(bodyWeightKg: null, heightCm: 170) -> invalid.
  3. Assert draft(bodyWeightKg: null, heightCm: null) -> invalid.
- **Esperado:** Step4 is invalid whenever weight or height is missing.

### profile_setup-09 — isComplete true only when all four steps are valid
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupDraft unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a fully valid draft (username 'carlos', gymId set, beginner+female, weight 70, height 170).
  2. Assert isComplete is true.
  3. Drop one field (e.g. set gender null) and assert isComplete becomes false.
- **Esperado:** isComplete is the AND of isStep1Valid..isStep4Valid.

### profile_setup-10 — validateUsername returns null for valid usernames with allowed chars
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateUsername('julieta') == null.
  2. Assert validateUsername('user_1.name') == null.
  3. Assert validateUsername('ABC') == null (3 chars, boundary).
- **Esperado:** Valid usernames (letters, digits, _ and ., 3-20 chars) return null.

### profile_setup-11 — validateUsername rejects empty/null with 'Ingresá un username'
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateUsername(null) == 'Ingresá un username'.
  2. Assert validateUsername('') == 'Ingresá un username'.
  3. Assert validateUsername('   ') == 'Ingresá un username' (whitespace-only).
- **Esperado:** Null, empty and whitespace-only inputs return the 'Ingresá un username' message.

### profile_setup-12 — validateUsername length boundaries: 2 chars too short, 21 chars too long
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateUsername('ab') == 'Mínimo 3 caracteres'.
  2. Assert validateUsername('a'*21) == 'Máximo 20 caracteres'.
  3. Assert validateUsername('a'*20) == null (20 is the inclusive max).
- **Esperado:** Below 3 -> 'Mínimo 3 caracteres'; above 20 -> 'Máximo 20 caracteres'; exactly 20 is valid.

### profile_setup-13 — validateUsername rejects disallowed characters (spaces, @, accents, emoji)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateUsername('juli eta') returns 'Solo letras, números, "_" y "."' (internal space).
  2. Assert validateUsername('@juli') returns the same charset message.
  3. Assert validateUsername('niño') returns the same charset message (accented char).
  4. Assert validateUsername('user😀') returns the same charset message.
- **Esperado:** Any character outside [a-zA-Z0-9_.] yields the charset error message.

### profile_setup-14 — validateUsername trims surrounding whitespace before length/charset checks
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateUsername('  carlos  ') == null (trimmed to 'carlos').
  2. Assert validateUsername('  ab  ') == 'Mínimo 3 caracteres' (trimmed length 2).
- **Esperado:** Leading/trailing whitespace is ignored; checks run on the trimmed value.

### profile_setup-15 — validateBodyWeightKg accepts comma and dot decimals, rejects boundaries
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('82,5') == null (comma decimal accepted).
  2. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('82.5') == null (dot decimal accepted).
  3. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('20') == 'Mínimo 20 kg' (<= 20 rejected).
  4. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('300') == 'Máximo 300 kg' (>= 300 rejected).
  5. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('20.1') == null and validateBodyWeightKg('299.9') == null.
- **Esperado:** Comma/dot both parse; weight must be strictly >20 and <300; 20 and 300 are rejected.

### profile_setup-16 — validateBodyWeightKg rejects empty and non-numeric input
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateBodyWeightKg(null) == 'Ingresá tu peso'.
  2. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('') == 'Ingresá tu peso'.
  3. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('abc') == 'Número inválido'.
  4. Assert validateBodyWeightKg('7o') == 'Número inválido' (letter o, not zero).
- **Esperado:** Empty -> 'Ingresá tu peso'; unparseable -> 'Número inválido'.

### profile_setup-17 — validateHeightCm requires an integer and rejects decimals/boundaries
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Pure ProfileSetupValidators unit test.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Assert validateHeightCm('170') == null.
  2. Assert validateHeightCm('170.5') == 'Número entero inválido' (int.tryParse fails on decimal).
  3. Assert validateHeightCm('100') == 'Mínimo 100 cm' and validateHeightCm('250') == 'Máximo 250 cm'.
  4. Assert validateHeightCm('101') == null and validateHeightCm('249') == null.
  5. Assert validateHeightCm('') == 'Ingresá tu altura'.
- **Esperado:** Height must be a parseable integer strictly between 100 and 250; decimals and boundaries are rejected.

### profile_setup-18 — Notifier initial state: step 0, empty draft, not submitting, no error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with profileSetupNotifierProvider; no overrides needed for read.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read profileSetupNotifierProvider.
  2. Inspect currentStep, draft, isSubmitting, submitError.
- **Esperado:** currentStep == 0, draft is an empty ProfileSetupDraft, isSubmitting == false, submitError == null.

### profile_setup-19 — Notifier canGoNext reflects per-step validity of the current step
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with the notifier.
- **Pasos:**
  1. On step 0, assert canGoNext is false; call updateUsername('carlos'); assert canGoNext is true.
  2. Manually advance to step 1 (goNext) and assert canGoNext is false until updateGymId(kNoGymId).
  3. Repeat the pattern for step 2 (experience+gender) and step 3 (valid weight+height).
- **Esperado:** canGoNext mirrors isStepNValid for the active step; flips false->true as the step's fields become valid.

### profile_setup-20 — goNext advances only when current step is valid
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with the notifier at step 0.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goNext() with empty username; assert currentStep stays 0.
  2. Call updateUsername('carlos'); call goNext(); assert currentStep == 1.
- **Esperado:** goNext is a no-op when !canGoNext; advances by one when the step is valid.

### profile_setup-21 — goNext is a no-op on the last step (does not exceed total-1)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer; drive the notifier to a fully valid step 3.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Fill all steps validly and navigate to currentStep == 3 (last step).
  2. Call goNext().
  3. Assert currentStep remains 3.
- **Esperado:** goNext does not increment past the last step (isLastStep guard); submit is the last-step action, not goNext.

### profile_setup-22 — goBack decrements step but never below 0
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with the notifier.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call goBack() at step 0; assert currentStep stays 0.
  2. Advance to step 1, call goBack(), assert currentStep == 0.
- **Esperado:** goBack is clamped at 0 and otherwise decrements by one. Going back does NOT clear already-entered draft fields.

### profile_setup-23 — Field updaters mutate only their target draft field
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with the notifier.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call updateUsername('carlos'), updateGymId('megatlon-recoleta'), updateExperienceLevel(intermediate), updateGender(male), updateBodyWeightKg(80.5), updateHeightCm(180), updateAvatarLocalPath('/tmp/a.jpg').
  2. Read the resulting draft.
- **Esperado:** Each field holds the value last set; other fields are untouched. currentStep is unchanged by field updates.

### profile_setup-24 — updateBodyWeightKg / updateHeightCm / updateAvatarLocalPath accept null to clear
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with the notifier; seed weight/height/avatar first.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set bodyWeightKg=80, heightCm=180, avatarLocalPath='/x'.
  2. Call updateBodyWeightKg(null), updateHeightCm(null), updateAvatarLocalPath(null).
  3. Read draft.
- **Esperado:** All three fields become null (copyWith passes the explicit null through). This is the path the Step4 listeners use when a TextField is cleared/unparseable.

### profile_setup-25 — submit sets submitError and returns early when no authenticated user
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer overriding firebaseAuthProvider with a mock whose currentUser is null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Override firebaseAuthProvider.currentUser to return null.
  2. Call notifier.submit().
  3. Inspect state.
- **Esperado:** submitError is a StateError('No authenticated user'); isSubmitting stays false; no Firestore write and no rethrow.

### profile_setup-26 — submit maps kNoGymId to null gymId in the persisted partial
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth (uid u1). Seed users/u1. Fake avatar service.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set username 'carlos' and updateGymId(kNoGymId).
  2. Call submit().
  3. Read users/u1.
- **Esperado:** Persisted gymId is null (the 'no-gym' sentinel is never written verbatim).

### profile_setup-27 — submit writes a real catalog gymId verbatim
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1. Fake avatar service.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set username 'carlos' and updateGymId('smart-fit-palermo').
  2. Call submit().
  3. Read users/u1.
- **Esperado:** Persisted gymId == 'smart-fit-palermo'.

### profile_setup-28 — submit trims the username before persisting displayName
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call updateUsername('  Carlos  ').
  2. Call submit().
  3. Read users/u1 displayName and userPublicProfiles/u1 displayNameLowercase.
- **Esperado:** displayName == 'Carlos' (trimmed); displayNameLowercase == 'carlos' (derived by repo).

### profile_setup-29 — submit persists experienceLevel, gender, weight and height wire values
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Fill a full valid draft: username 'carlos', gym set, experienceLevel intermediate, gender female, bodyWeightKg 72.5, heightCm 168.
  2. Call submit().
  3. Read users/u1.
- **Esperado:** experienceLevel == 'intermediate', gender == 'female', bodyWeightKg == 72.5, heightCm == 168 (enums serialized via toJson()).

### profile_setup-30 — submit toggles isSubmitting true during the await and back to false on success
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with fake firestore + fake avatar service. Seed users/u1.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Listen to profileSetupNotifierProvider.
  2. Call submit() and capture the isSubmitting transitions (e.g. via a listener or by reading mid-future with a controllable fake).
  3. Await completion.
- **Esperado:** isSubmitting becomes true at the start and false after a successful update; submitError stays null and is cleared at start.

### profile_setup-31 — submit clears a previous submitError when retried
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer; first submit forced to fail (e.g. repo override that throws once), then succeed.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Force submit() to fail and assert submitError is set.
  2. Make the repo succeed and call submit() again.
  3. Inspect submitError.
- **Esperado:** On retry, submit sets isSubmitting true with clearSubmitError, so a successful retry ends with submitError == null.

### profile_setup-32 — submit avatar upload success writes avatarUrl
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1. avatarUploadServiceProvider overridden with a fake returning a fixed URL.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set username 'carlos' and updateAvatarLocalPath('/tmp/avatar.jpg').
  2. Call submit().
  3. Read users/u1.
- **Esperado:** avatarUrl == the fake upload URL (e.g. 'https://fake.url/avatar.jpg'); only written because upload returned non-null.

### profile_setup-33 — submit tolerates avatar upload FirebaseException and still persists the profile
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1. avatarUploadServiceProvider overridden with a fake whose upload throws FirebaseException.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set a full valid draft including updateAvatarLocalPath('/tmp/a.jpg').
  2. Call submit().
  3. Read users/u1.
- **Esperado:** submit does NOT throw; profile fields persist; avatarUrl key is absent (avatarUrl stayed null). Matches the documented 'retry from settings' fallback.

### profile_setup-34 — submit tolerates a generic (non-Firebase) avatar upload error
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1. Fake avatar service whose upload throws a plain Exception.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set username + avatarLocalPath.
  2. Call submit().
  3. Inspect state and persisted doc.
- **Esperado:** The generic catch swallows the error; submit succeeds with avatarUrl absent and no submitError.

### profile_setup-35 — submit skips avatar upload entirely when avatarLocalPath is null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore + mock auth. Seed users/u1. Avatar service fake that records whether upload was called.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set username 'carlos' with no avatar.
  2. Call submit().
  3. Assert the avatar service's upload was never invoked.
- **Esperado:** Upload is not attempted when there is no local path; avatarUrl key absent in the partial.

### profile_setup-36 — submit rethrows and records submitError when the repository update fails
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with userRepositoryProvider overridden by a fake/mock whose update throws (createIfAbsent succeeds).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set a valid draft.
  2. Call submit() inside expectLater(..., throwsA(...)).
  3. Inspect state after the throw.
- **Esperado:** submit rethrows the repo error; isSubmitting ends false; submitError holds the thrown error (so the flow can show the save-error SnackBar).

### profile_setup-37 — filteredGymsProvider returns full catalog when query is empty/whitespace
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer reading filteredGymsProvider + gymSearchQueryProvider.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Read filteredGymsProvider with empty query; assert it has all 3 hardcoded gyms.
  2. Set gymSearchQueryProvider to '   ' and assert it still returns all 3 (query trimmed to empty).
- **Esperado:** Empty or whitespace-only query returns the complete catalog (3 gyms).

### profile_setup-38 — filteredGymsProvider matches case-insensitively on name OR address substring
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderContainer with gymSearchQueryProvider + filteredGymsProvider.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Set query 'smart' -> assert only SMART FIT returned.
  2. Set query 'PALERMO' (uppercase, matches address) -> assert SMART FIT returned.
  3. Set query 'belgrano' -> assert only SPORTCLUB returned.
  4. Set query 'zzz' -> assert empty list.
- **Esperado:** Filter is a case-insensitive contains over name and address; no match yields an empty list.

### profile_setup-39 — Step2 list rebuilds as the search query changes and selection persists
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget test pumping Step2Gym inside a ProviderScope with AppTheme.

  2. Tap a gym card and verify it shows selected (check icon).
  3. Enter 'smart' into the search TextField and pump.
  4. Verify only matching gym(s) + the OTRO card remain.
- **Esperado:** Typing filters the visible GymCards; the 'OTRO GYM / SIN GYM' card is always present; previously chosen gymId stays in the notifier draft.

### profile_setup-40 — Step2 selecting 'OTRO GYM / SIN GYM' marks it selected and sets gymId to sentinel
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### profile_setup-41 — Step3 renders all three experience cards and three gender chips and updates draft on tap
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  4. Read the notifier draft.
- **Esperado:** draft.experienceLevel == advanced, draft.gender == undisclosed (OTRO maps to undisclosed); nonBinary is intentionally not offered in the UI.

### profile_setup-42 — Footer primary button is disabled until the current step is valid, enabled after
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget test pumping ProfileSetupFlow in a ProviderScope with theme + l10n.

### profile_setup-43 — Footer hides VOLVER on step 0 and shows it from step 1 onward
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### profile_setup-44 — Last-step CTA label is 'EMPEZAR' and shows a loading spinner while submitting
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget test pumping ProfileSetupFlow with fake firestore + fake (slow) avatar/repo so isSubmitting can be observed.

  2. Assert the primary button label reads 'EMPEZAR' (not 'SIGUIENTE').
  3. Tap EMPEZAR and pump one frame.
  4. Assert the button shows its loading state (primaryLoading true) and is non-interactive.
- **Esperado:** On the last step the CTA is 'EMPEZAR'; during submit it shows the spinner and blocks double-tap.

### profile_setup-45 — Save error on final submit shows the profileSetupSaveError SnackBar and keeps the user on the flow
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget test: ProfileSetupFlow with userRepositoryProvider overridden to throw on update; l10n loaded.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Drive the flow to a valid last step.
  2. Tap EMPEZAR and pump (let the failing submit settle).
  3. Verify a SnackBar with the profileSetupSaveError text appears.
  4. Verify currentStep is still the last step (no navigation away).
- **Esperado:** A failed submit surfaces the save-error SnackBar (3s) and the user remains on /profile-setup; no navigation is performed by the flow itself.

### profile_setup-46 — Cancel-onboarding affordance is only present on step 0
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
