  2. Advance to step 1 (valid username + SIGUIENTE).
  3. Assert the cancel button is no longer present.
- **Esperado:** The hard-cancel close button renders only on the first step.

### profile_setup-47 — Tapping cancel shows a confirmation dialog; 'Volver al setup' dismisses without deleting
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget test pumping ProfileSetupFlow at step 0 with authNotifierProvider overridden by a spy.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Tap the cancel IconButton.
  2. Verify a confirmation AlertDialog appears with 'Cancelar cuenta' and 'Volver al setup' actions.
  3. Tap 'Volver al setup'.
  4. Verify the dialog closes and cancelOnboarding was NOT called; user stays on step 0.
- **Esperado:** Dialog appears; choosing 'Volver al setup' (returns false) aborts cancellation — no account deletion, no navigation.

### profile_setup-48 — Confirming cancel deletes the account and navigates to /welcome; failure shows error SnackBar
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Manual emulator session with an athlete account mid-onboarding (or widget test with a mocked authNotifier + GoRouter). Native dialog + real auth/Firestore delete involved.
- **Pasos:**
  1. On step 0, tap cancel and choose 'Cancelar cuenta'.
  2. Observe the cancelOnboarding flow: Firestore profile + Firebase Auth user deleted.
  3. Verify the app navigates to /welcome on success.
  4. Re-run with cancelOnboarding forced to throw and verify the profileSetupCancelAccountError SnackBar appears and the user stays on the current step.
- **Esperado:** Confirm -> account deleted and route -> /welcome. On failure -> error SnackBar and the user remains on /profile-setup. Real auth/Firestore deletion makes the success path manual; the failure-SnackBar branch can be unit-tested with a mocked notifier.

### profile_setup-49 — Avatar picker opens the gallery and stores the chosen local path
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Real device/emulator with photos; Step1 mounted. image_picker native gallery is involved.
- **Pasos:**
  1. On step 1, tap the AvatarPickerButton.
  2. Pick an image from the gallery.
  3. Verify the avatar preview replaces the initial placeholder and that the chosen file path is stored in the draft (avatarLocalPath).
- **Esperado:** A picked image updates avatarLocalPath and renders the photo; the badge '+' and 'SUBÍ UNA FOTO' label remain. Native gallery makes this manual; the placeholder->image rendering of AvatarPickerButton can also be widget-tested by passing localPath directly.

### profile_setup-50 — Router gate: athlete with displayName already set is redirected out of /profile-setup to /home
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator seed: athlete account whose users/{uid}.displayName is already set; logged in. Router built with real redirect.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Authenticate as the seeded athlete and navigate to /profile-setup.
  2. Wait for userProfileProvider to emit the profile.
  3. Observe the resulting route.
- **Esperado:** The onboarding-complete gate redirects to /home once displayName != null (no flicker); a freshly-signed-up account with displayName null stays on /profile-setup. Relies on real auth + Firestore stream, so manual.

### profile_setup-51 — Role gate: trainer finishing profile-setup is routed to trainer onboarding, not the athlete home
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Emulator seed: trainer account (role=trainer, trainerProfileComplete=false) mid profile-setup.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As the trainer, complete the 4 steps and tap EMPEZAR so displayName is persisted.
  2. Observe routing after submit.
- **Esperado:** After displayName is set, the onboarding-complete gate sends to /home, which immediately re-applies the trainer-incomplete gate -> /profile/edit-trainer?mode=onboarding. The shared profile_setup flow has no role branch itself. Needs real auth/role, so manual.

# Módulo: reviews

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/reviews/ (athlete→trainer reviews). Covers domain model + deterministic id, ReviewRepository (Firestore upsert/get/watch), ReviewNotifier validation/lifecycle, the write bottom sheet, ReviewCta gating, ReviewTile, StarRatingInput/Display, TrainerReviewsSection, and the two external triggers in athlete_coach_view.dart (30-day prompt, post-termination prompt). New cases avoid duplicating existing SCENARIO-571..615 coverage and focus on edit/edge/role/trigger regressions. Files: lib/features/reviews/domain/review.dart, data/review_repository.dart, application/review_notifier.dart + review_providers.dart, presentation/widgets/{review_bottom_sheet,review_cta,review_tile,star_rating_display,star_rating_input,trainer_reviews_section}.dart, and lib/features/coach/athlete_coach_view.dart._

### reviews-01 — Review.idFor builds deterministic '{linkId}_{athleteId}' id
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None (pure function).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call Review.idFor('link-9','ath-3').
  2. Call it again with the same args.
  3. Call with linkId containing an underscore, e.g. Review.idFor('a_b','c').
- **Esperado:** Returns 'link-9_ath-3' both times (stable); the underscore case returns 'a_b_c' (documented join, no escaping).

### reviews-02 — Review JSON round-trip preserves all fields incl. null comment and UTC timestamps
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a Review with comment set and createdAt/updatedAt as UTC DateTimes.
  2. toJson() then Review.fromJson().
  3. Repeat with comment = null.
- **Esperado:** Decoded Review equals the original for every field; comment null survives as null; createdAt/updatedAt match (TimestampConverter handles Firestore Timestamp <-> DateTime).

### reviews-03 — ReviewRepository.upsert writes at deterministic id using set without merge
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore. A pre-existing doc at the review id containing an extra stale field.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Upsert a Review whose toJson() omits the stale field.
  2. Read back the raw doc at Review.idFor(linkId, athleteId).
- **Esperado:** Doc exists at the deterministic id and contains ONLY the new payload; the stale field is gone (set overwrites, no merge) — REQ-RV-DATA-003.

### reviews-04 — getForPair returns null when doc missing and Review when present
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore, empty then seeded.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call getForPair(linkId, athleteId) on empty store.
  2. Upsert a Review for that pair.
  3. Call getForPair again.
- **Esperado:** First call returns null (snap not exists / data null); second returns the deserialized Review.

### reviews-05 — watchForTrainer streams reviews sorted by createdAt DESC and honors limit
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore seeded with 12 reviews for trainerId with distinct createdAt; some reviews for a different trainer.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to watchForTrainer(trainerId, limit: 10).
  2. Inspect the first emission.
- **Esperado:** Emits at most 10 reviews, only for the requested trainerId, ordered newest-first by createdAt; other trainers' reviews excluded (REQ-RV-DATA-005, composite index trainerId ASC + createdAt DESC).

### reviews-06 — watchForTrainer emits empty list when trainer has no reviews
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore with no reviews for the trainer.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to watchForTrainer('trainer-x').
  2. Read first emission.
- **Esperado:** Emits an empty list (not an error, not null).

### reviews-07 — watchForLink emits null then the Review after an upsert (live edit-state)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** FakeFirebaseFirestore, empty.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Subscribe to watchForLink(linkId, athleteId).
  2. Confirm first emission is null.
  3. Upsert a Review for the same pair.
  4. Read next emission.
- **Esperado:** Stream emits null first, then the upserted Review — used by the write flow to switch new vs edit state.

### reviews-08 — ReviewNotifier.submit rejects rating below 1 synchronously, never hits repo
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Riverpod container with mocked ReviewRepository; notifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call notifier.submit(rating: 0).
  2. Call notifier.submit(rating: -1).
- **Esperado:** Each throws ArgumentError synchronously (before any await); verifyNever upsert; notifier state is not left in AsyncLoading.

### reviews-09 — ReviewNotifier.submit rejects rating above 5 synchronously, never hits repo
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mocked repo; notifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call notifier.submit(rating: 6).
  2. Call notifier.submit(rating: 100).
- **Esperado:** Throws ArgumentError synchronously; upsert never called; state unchanged.

### reviews-10 — ReviewNotifier.submit accepts comment of exactly 500 chars but rejects 501
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mocked repo (upsert stubbed ok); notifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. submit(rating: 4, comment: 'x'*500).
  2. submit(rating: 4, comment: 'x'*501).
- **Esperado:** 500-char comment is accepted and reaches upsert; 501-char throws ArgumentError before await and upsert is never called (boundary at 500 inclusive).

### reviews-11 — ReviewNotifier.submit on new review sets createdAt==updatedAt to now-UTC
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mocked repo capturing the Review; notifier built; existing = null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call submit(rating: 5, comment: 'ok') with no existing.
  2. Capture the Review passed to upsert.
- **Esperado:** Captured review has id == Review.idFor(linkId, athleteId), all link/trainer/athlete ids from args, createdAt and updatedAt both within ~60s of now in UTC.

### reviews-12 — ReviewNotifier.submit on edit preserves original createdAt, bumps updatedAt
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mocked repo capturing the Review; notifier built; an existing Review with createdAt 30 days ago.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call submit(rating: 2, comment: 'changed', existing: oldReview).
  2. Capture the Review passed to upsert.
- **Esperado:** Captured createdAt == existing.createdAt (unchanged); updatedAt is ~now (changed); rating/comment reflect the new values — invariant for edit semantics.

### reviews-13 — ReviewNotifier success transitions AsyncLoading then AsyncData(null)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mocked repo upsert resolves; notifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. await submit(rating: 5).
  2. Read state.
- **Esperado:** State ends as AsyncData<void>(null); upsert called once.

### reviews-14 — ReviewNotifier captures repo failure as AsyncError (no rethrow, no auto-retry)
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Mocked repo upsert throws; notifier built.
- **Pasos:**
  1. await submit(rating: 3).
  2. Read state.
- **Esperado:** submit completes without throwing (guarded); state is AsyncError; repo called exactly once (no retry).

### reviews-15 — ReviewNotifierArgs equality/hashCode keys the family cache correctly
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build two ReviewNotifierArgs with identical linkId/trainerId/athleteId.
  2. Build a third differing only in athleteId.
  3. Compare == and hashCode; read provider.notifier for equal args twice.
- **Esperado:** Equal args are ==, share hashCode, and resolve to the same notifier instance; differing athleteId is not equal and yields a distinct family entry.

### reviews-16 — userReviewForLinkProvider splits 'linkId:athleteId' key; missing athleteId degrades safely
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Riverpod container with mocked repo; spy on watchForLink args.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Watch userReviewForLinkProvider('link-1:ath-1').
  2. Watch userReviewForLinkProvider('link-1') (no colon).
- **Esperado:** First call invokes repo.watchForLink('link-1','ath-1'); the colon-less key passes actualLinkId='link-1' and athleteId='' (empty string fallback) without throwing.

### reviews-17 — Sheet title: new standard variant asks experience with trainer name
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; ReviewBottomSheet with existing=null, triggerVariant standard, trainerName='Ana'.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the sheet.
  2. Read the title text.
- **Esperado:** Title reads '¿Cómo fue tu experiencia con Ana?'.

### reviews-20 — Sheet pre-fills star rating and comment when editing

### reviews-21 — Sheet ENVIAR is disabled at rating 0 and enabled after selecting a star
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  4. Re-check the button.

### reviews-22 — Sheet submit success pops the sheet and shows success SnackBar
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

- **Esperado:** Sheet is popped and the localized success SnackBar (reviewSnackBarSuccess) is displayed; no error SnackBar.

### reviews-23 — Sheet submit error keeps sheet open and shows retry SnackBar
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the sheet, tap a star, tap ENVIAR, pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** SnackBar 'No pudimos guardar tu reseña. Probá de nuevo.' is shown; the sheet remains open (not popped); no auto-retry.

### reviews-24 — Sheet shows spinner and disables ENVIAR/CANCELAR while loading
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope with notifier state forced/held in AsyncLoading.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the sheet with rating>0 while state is AsyncLoading.
  2. Inspect ENVIAR (CircularProgressIndicator vs label) and both buttons' onPressed.
- **Esperado:** ENVIAR renders a CircularProgressIndicator instead of 'ENVIAR' and its onPressed is null; CANCELAR onPressed is null too (prevents double submit / dismiss mid-write).

### reviews-25 — Sheet empty comment is normalized to null on submit
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; spy notifier capturing submit args; new sheet.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open sheet, select a star, leave comment empty, tap ENVIAR.
  2. Inspect the comment argument passed to notifier.submit.
- **Esperado:** submit is called with comment: null (empty controller text maps to null, not '') so empty comments are not persisted as empty strings.

### reviews-26 — Sheet comment field enforces maxLength 500 with visible counter
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; new sheet.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the sheet.
  2. Read the TextField.maxLength.
- **Esperado:** TextField.maxLength == 500 (the built-in counter caps input client-side, complementing the notifier's 500 guard).

### reviews-27 — Sheet CANCELAR pops without writing
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; sheet shown via showModalBottomSheet; spy repo.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Open the sheet, tap CANCELAR, pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** Sheet is popped; repo.upsert never called.

### reviews-28 — StarRatingInput renders 5 stars and emits 1-based index on tap
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped with rating=0 and a captured onRatingChanged.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump StarRatingInput.
  2. Count star icons.
  3. Tap the 3rd star.
- **Esperado:** Exactly 5 star icons; tapping the 3rd fires onRatingChanged(3) (1-based).

### reviews-29 — StarRatingInput fills exactly 'rating' stars
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped with rating=4.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump StarRatingInput(rating: 4).
  2. Count starFill vs starOutline icons.
- **Esperado:** 4 starFill + 1 starOutline; at rating=0 all 5 are starOutline.

### reviews-30 — StarRatingDisplay floors fractional average to whole filled stars
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped read-only.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump StarRatingDisplay(rating: 4.7).
  2. Count fill vs outline.
  3. Repeat with rating: 5.0 and rating: 0.9.
- **Esperado:** 4.7 -> 4 fill + 1 outline (floor, no half-stars); 5.0 -> 5 fill; 0.9 -> 0 fill / 5 outline. Confirms floor() boundary, not round().

### reviews-31 — StarRatingDisplay with null rating shows all outline (no-data state)
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped with rating=null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump StarRatingDisplay(rating: null).
  2. Count icons.
- **Esperado:** 5 starOutline icons, 0 filled — represents 'no reviews yet'.

### reviews-32 — StarRatingDisplay is non-interactive (no gesture detectors)
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Widget pumped.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump StarRatingDisplay(rating: 3).
  2. Search the subtree for GestureDetector.
- **Esperado:** No GestureDetector present (contrast with StarRatingInput); display is read-only.

### reviews-33 — ReviewTile renders avatar, name, stars, comment and relative date for a known athlete
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope overriding userPublicProfileProvider(athleteId) -> profile(displayName 'Leo', avatarUrl set); Review rating=5, comment='Genial', createdAt today.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ReviewTile.
  2. Assert name, StarRatingDisplay rating, comment text, and date label.
- **Esperado:** Shows 'Leo', 5 filled stars, the comment 'Genial', and date 'hoy' (createdAt < 1 day).

### reviews-34 — ReviewTile falls back to 'Usuario eliminado' with neutral avatar when profile is null
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope overriding userPublicProfileProvider(athleteId) -> AsyncData(null).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ReviewTile.
  2. Assert displayed name and that avatarUrl is dropped.
- **Esperado:** Name renders 'Usuario eliminado'; avatarUrl is null so PostAvatar uses the neutral fallback (ADR-RV-009). Review content (stars/comment) still renders.

### reviews-35 — ReviewTile hides comment row when comment is null or empty
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope with a valid profile; two Reviews — one comment=null, one comment=''.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ReviewTile for the null-comment review.
  2. Pump for the empty-string review.
- **Esperado:** In both cases no comment Text is rendered (guard is comment != null && comment.isNotEmpty); header row still shows.

### reviews-36 — ReviewTile renders nothing while profile is loading or errored
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope overriding userPublicProfileProvider -> AsyncLoading, then AsyncError.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump ReviewTile in loading state.
  2. Pump in error state.
- **Esperado:** Both states render SizedBox.shrink (empty) — tile only appears once profile resolves to data.

### reviews-37 — ReviewTile relative-date formatting across all boundaries
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** Profile override; control createdAt relative to now.
- **Pasos:**
  1. createdAt now -> expect 'hoy'.
  2. createdAt 1 day ago -> 'hace 1 día' (singular).
  3. createdAt 5 days -> 'hace 5 días'.
  4. createdAt 29 days -> 'hace 29 días'.
  5. createdAt 30 days -> 'hace 1 mes' (singular).
  6. createdAt 90 days -> 'hace 3 meses'.
  7. createdAt 400 days -> 'DD/MM/YYYY' zero-padded.
- **Esperado:** Each label matches: <1d 'hoy'; <30d days w/ día/días singular-plural; <365d months floored w/ mes/meses; >=365d absolute DD/MM/YYYY with 2-digit padding. Catches off-by-one and singular/plural regressions.

### reviews-38 — TrainerReviewsSection always shows 'RESEÑAS' header
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope overriding trainerReviewsProvider -> AsyncData([]).
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump the section.
  2. Find header text.
- **Esperado:** Header 'RESEÑAS' is present regardless of data state.

### reviews-39 — TrainerReviewsSection shows empty-state copy when no reviews

  2. Assert text and absence of ReviewTile.
- **Esperado:** Shows 'Sin reseñas todavía'; no ReviewTile widgets rendered.

### reviews-40 — TrainerReviewsSection renders one ReviewTile per review and hides empty copy

- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

  2. Pump in error.

### reviews-42 — ReviewCta hidden when there is no active link to this trainer
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

- **Esperado:** In all three cases the widget is SizedBox.shrink (no button) — CTA is auth/role-gated to athletes with an ACTIVE link to exactly this trainer (REQ-RV-WRITE-006).

### reviews-45 — ReviewCta tap opens ReviewBottomSheet with correct args incl. existing review
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true

### reviews-46 — ReviewCta uses fallback trainer name when public profile is null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** ui · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** ProviderScope; active link; userPublicProfileProvider(trainerId) -> null/loading.

  1. Pump ReviewCta, tap, pumpAndSettle.
  2. Inspect ReviewBottomSheet.trainerName.
- **Esperado:** trainerName falls back to 'tu Personal Trainer' (sheet title still renders sensibly).

### reviews-47 — 30-day prompt fires only when active link, acceptedAt>=30d, no review, prefs flag unset
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView under ProviderScope; SharedPreferences mock with flag 'review_prompt_shown_{linkId}' unset; currentAthleteLinkProvider -> active link with acceptedAt 31 days ago; userReviewForLinkProvider -> null.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump AthleteCoachView, let the post-frame callback run, pumpAndSettle.
  2. Check for ReviewBottomSheet with triggerVariant thirtyDay.
  3. Confirm the prefs flag was written.
- **Esperado:** The thirtyDay ReviewBottomSheet is shown exactly once and prefs flag 'review_prompt_shown_{linkId}' is set to true BEFORE the sheet appears (so cancel won't re-trigger) — ADR-RV-006.

### reviews-48 — 30-day prompt suppressed when acceptedAt < 30 days
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView; active link with acceptedAt 10 days ago; review null; prefs unset.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump AthleteCoachView, run post-frame callback, pumpAndSettle.
  2. Check for any ReviewBottomSheet.
- **Esperado:** No review sheet shown; prefs flag not set (boundary: < 30 days does not qualify).

### reviews-49 — 30-day prompt suppressed when a review already exists or prefs flag set
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView; active link acceptedAt 40 days ago. Case A: userReviewForLinkProvider -> non-null. Case B: review null but prefs flag already true.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump for case A, run post-frame, pumpAndSettle.
  2. Pump fresh for case B, run post-frame, pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** Case A: no sheet (existingReview != null short-circuits). Case B: no sheet (prefs flag true short-circuits). Prevents re-prompting after submit/dismiss.

### reviews-50 — 30-day prompt suppressed when acceptedAt is null
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView; active link with acceptedAt == null; review null; prefs unset.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump AthleteCoachView, run post-frame, pumpAndSettle.
  2. Check for sheet.
- **Esperado:** No sheet shown (null acceptedAt fails the >=30d check) and no flag written — null-safety guard.

### reviews-51 — 30-day prompt check runs at most once per widget lifetime
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView; conditions met for the prompt; force currentAthleteLinkProvider to emit AsyncData multiple times.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Pump AthleteCoachView.
  2. Trigger several AsyncData emissions of the link provider.
  3. Count how many ReviewBottomSheets are shown.
- **Esperado:** The sheet is shown once; the _promptCheckScheduled guard prevents double-fire across repeated link emissions.

### reviews-52 — Post-termination shows review sheet only after terminate succeeds, with existing review
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView showing an active link; trainerLinkRepository.terminate stubbed to succeed; userReviewForLinkProvider may return an existing review; user confirms the terminate dialog.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Trigger terminate flow and confirm the dialog.
  2. Let terminate() resolve, pumpAndSettle.
  3. Inspect the shown ReviewBottomSheet.
- **Esperado:** terminate(linkId, reason: 'athlete-terminated') is called; currentAthleteLinkProvider is invalidated; then a standard-variant ReviewBottomSheet opens with linkId/trainerId/athleteId/existing captured BEFORE the await (survives widget disposal) — ADR-RV-007.

### reviews-53 — Post-termination flow aborts entirely when user cancels the confirm dialog
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** AthleteCoachView with active link; spy on terminate and showModalBottomSheet.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Trigger terminate flow.
  2. Dismiss/cancel the confirmation dialog.
  3. pumpAndSettle.
- **Esperado:** terminate is never called and no review sheet is shown (early return on !confirmed).

### reviews-54 — End-to-end: athlete submits a review and it surfaces in the trainer's RESEÑAS section
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Firebase emulator seeded with athlete + coach accounts and an active link between them; athlete authenticated.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As athlete, open the trainer public profile, tap 'DEJAR UNA RESEÑA'.
  2. Select 4 stars, type a comment, tap ENVIAR.
  3. Observe success SnackBar and sheet dismissal.
  4. Reload/view the trainer public profile TrainerReviewsSection.
- **Esperado:** Review persists at reviews/{linkId}_{athleteId}; TrainerReviewsSection shows the new tile (athlete name, 4 stars, comment, 'hoy') newest-first; re-opening the CTA now reads 'EDITAR MI RESEÑA'. Requires real auth + emulator round-trip.

### reviews-55 — Firestore rules: athlete can only upsert own review (1..5, <=500), cannot write others'
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** integration · **Automatizable:** false
- **Precondiciones:** Firebase emulator with security rules deployed; athlete A and athlete B accounts, active link for A.
- **Pasos:**
  1. As A, write reviews/{linkA}_{A} with rating 4 — expect allow.
  2. As A, attempt rating 0 or 6, or comment >500 — expect deny.
  3. As A, attempt to write reviews/{linkB}_{B} (another athlete's review) — expect deny.
  4. As A, attempt to write with mismatched trainerId/athleteId — expect deny.
- **Esperado:** Rules permit only the owning athlete's valid review (rating 1..5, comment<=500, ids consistent) and reject invalid ranges, oversized comments, and writes to other athletes' review docs — server-side enforcement of the same invariants (REQ-RV-DATA-001/002). Needs emulator rules harness.

# Módulo: workout

_Executable test-case catalog for lib/features/workout/. Covers domain invariants (RoutineSlot.effectiveSets/effectiveSetsForWeek/isPresentInWeek, RepMode/ExerciseMode/SetType derivation, SessionState volume/completion getters), pure periodization logic (plan_progress, plan_gating), the session player notifier (idempotent logSet anti-double-tap, finish/abandon counters, week clamp, resume), repositories (RoutineRepository source/visibility/assign invariants, SessionRepository finish + best-effort public counters, CustomExerciseRepository), and UI surfaces (workout_screen role split, routine_detail single-week vs periodized gating + role-gated CTA, session_player block gating, post_workout/session_detail/historial async states, routine_editor validation + save dispatch, my_exercises/custom_exercise_editor). 78 cases. Many domain/logic/data cases overlap existing tests under test/features/workout/ — IDs and titles are written to extend, not duplicate, that suite. Manual-only items (native back swipe, haptics, video upload/picker, real auth/permission-denied, push) are flagged automatable=false._

### workout-01 — RoutineSlot.effectiveSets returns explicit sets when sets list is populated
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None — pure domain.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with sets=[SetSpec(reps:10), SetSpec(reps:8)] and targetSets=5
  2. Read slot.effectiveSets
- **Esperado:** Returns the 2 explicit SetSpec rows verbatim; targetSets (5) is ignored.

### workout-02 — RoutineSlot.effectiveSets synthesizes from legacy targetSets when sets empty
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with sets=[], targetSets=3, targetRepsMin=8, targetRepsMax=12, targetWeightKg=40
  2. Read slot.effectiveSets
- **Esperado:** Returns 3 SetSpec rows each with repsMin=8, repsMax=12, weightKg=40.

### workout-03 — RoutineSlot.effectiveSets clamps targetSets to at least 1
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with sets=[], targetSets=0, targetReps=[]
  2. Read slot.effectiveSets
- **Esperado:** Returns exactly 1 synthesized set (n clamped to minimum 1), never an empty list.

### workout-04 — RoutineSlot.effectiveSets handles single uniform targetReps
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with sets=[], targetSets=4, targetReps=[10]
  2. Read slot.effectiveSets
- **Esperado:** Returns 4 rows each with reps=10 (single value repeated for targetSets).

### workout-05 — RoutineSlot.effectiveSets handles explicit per-set targetReps sequence
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with sets=[], targetReps=[6,8,10], targetSets=2
  2. Read slot.effectiveSets
- **Esperado:** Returns exactly 3 rows with reps 6, 8, 10 (one row per entry; targetSets ignored).

### workout-06 — RoutineSlot.effectiveSets handles legacy duration-based slot
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with sets=[], targetSets=3, durationSeconds=45
  2. Read slot.effectiveSets
- **Esperado:** Returns 3 rows each with type=normal and durationSeconds=45 (duration legacy path wins over reps).

### workout-07 — effectiveSetsForWeek returns the week's rows when in range
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with weeklySets=[[SetSpec(reps:5)],[SetSpec(reps:8),SetSpec(reps:8)]]
  2. Call effectiveSetsForWeek(1)
- **Esperado:** Returns week 1's 2 rows; effectiveSetsForWeek(0) returns week 0's 1 row.

### workout-08 — effectiveSetsForWeek returns authored-empty deload week as-is
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with weeklySets=[[SetSpec(reps:8)], []] (week 1 authored empty)
  2. Call effectiveSetsForWeek(1)
- **Esperado:** Returns empty list (no fallback to effectiveSets) — deload/rest week respected.

### workout-09 — effectiveSetsForWeek falls back for out-of-range or negative week
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with weeklySets=[[SetSpec(reps:8)]] and legacy targetSets=2
  2. Call effectiveSetsForWeek(99) and effectiveSetsForWeek(-1)
- **Esperado:** Both fall back to effectiveSets (single-week semantics); never throws.

### workout-10 — isPresentInWeek: empty activeWeeks mask means present in all weeks
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with activeWeeks=[]
  2. Call isPresentInWeek(0), isPresentInWeek(5), isPresentInWeek(-1)
- **Esperado:** All return true — empty mask is back-compat 'present everywhere'.

### workout-11 — isPresentInWeek: non-empty mask only matches listed weeks
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with activeWeeks=[0,2]
  2. Call isPresentInWeek(0), isPresentInWeek(1), isPresentInWeek(2)
- **Esperado:** Returns true, false, true respectively.

### workout-12 — effectiveExerciseMode derives duration from legacy durationSeconds
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with exerciseMode default (reps) and durationSeconds=30
  2. Read slot.effectiveExerciseMode
- **Esperado:** Returns ExerciseMode.duration (legacy signal honored when new field is default).

### workout-13 — effectiveRepMode derives range when targetRepsMin != targetRepsMax
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a RoutineSlot with repMode default (single), targetRepsMin=8, targetRepsMax=12
  2. Read slot.effectiveRepMode
- **Esperado:** Returns RepMode.range (legacy signal honored).

### workout-14 — SetSpec/SetType unknown enum value falls back to normal on read
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Deserialize a SetSpec JSON with type:'bogus-value' via SetSpec.fromJson
- **Esperado:** type decodes to SetType.normal (JsonKey unknownEnumValue fallback) without throwing.

### workout-15 — SessionStatus.fromJson throws on unknown wire value
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call SessionStatusX.fromJson('paused')
- **Esperado:** Throws ArgumentError; fromJson('active') and ('finished') return the correct enums.

### workout-16 — RoutineSource.fromJson defaults to system for unknown/missing value
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call RoutineSourceX.fromJson('legacy-unknown')
  2. Call RoutineSourceX.fromJson('user-created')
- **Esperado:** Returns RoutineSource.system for unknown (defensive); returns userCreated for valid wire.

### workout-17 — RoutineVisibility/RoutineStatus default defensively on unknown value
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call RoutineVisibilityX.fromJson('weird')
  2. Call RoutineStatusX.fromJson('weird')
- **Esperado:** Visibility falls back to public; status falls back to active (back-compat for docs missing the field).

### workout-18 — Routine.fromJson applies retro-compat defaults for missing fields
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Deserialize a minimal Routine JSON missing source, visibility, status, numWeeks (Phase-2 seed shape)
- **Esperado:** source=system, visibility=public, status=active, numWeeks=1, days parses (empty allowed).

### workout-19 — parseReps parses multiple separators into int list
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseReps('6-8-10'), parseReps('10/8/6'), parseReps('6 8 10'), parseReps('10')
- **Esperado:** Returns [6,8,10], [10,8,6], [6,8,10], [10] respectively.

### workout-20 — parseReps returns empty list on empty or malformed input
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call parseReps(''), parseReps('   '), parseReps('6-abc-10'), parseReps('-5')
- **Esperado:** All return [] (any invalid token invalidates the whole input).

### workout-21 — formatReps round-trips the canonical dash form
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call formatReps([]), formatReps([10]), formatReps([6,8,10])
- **Esperado:** Returns '', '10', '6-8-10' respectively.

### workout-22 — EquipmentType.fromJson maps snake_case and nulls unknown
- **Prioridad:** P2 · **Área:** data · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Call EquipmentType.fromJson('peso_corporal'), ('mancuerna'), (null), ('spaceship')
- **Esperado:** Returns pesoCorporal, mancuerna, null, null respectively (null = filter matches all).

### workout-23 — SessionState.totalVolumeKg sums reps*weight across logs
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build SessionState with setLogs [reps10@40kg, reps8@50kg]
  2. Read state.totalVolumeKg
- **Esperado:** Returns 800.0 (10*40 + 8*50).

### workout-24 — SessionState.isFullyCompleted true only when every slot meets its week's set count
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a day with 2 slots each requiring 2 sets (week 0)
  2. Log 2 sets for slot A and 1 for slot B → check isFullyCompleted
  3. Log the 2nd set for slot B → check again
- **Esperado:** First check false; after completing slot B it is true.

### workout-25 — SessionState completion respects periodized week prescription
- **Prioridad:** P0 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a slot with weeklySets=[[s,s,s],[s]] (week0=3 sets, week1=1 set), session.weekNumber=1
  2. Log 1 set for the slot
  3. Read isFullyCompleted / completedExerciseCount
- **Esperado:** isFullyCompleted=true (week 1 needs only 1 set), not 3.

### workout-26 — SessionState.completedExerciseCount counts only fully-done exercises
- **Prioridad:** P1 · **Área:** logic · **Automatizable:** true
- **Precondiciones:** None.
- **Pasos:**
  1. Build a day with 3 slots (2 sets each)
  2. Fully complete slot 1, partially complete slot 2
  3. Read completedExerciseCount
- **Esperado:** Returns 1.

### workout-123 — planProgressProvider builds requiredPairs from per-week present slots

- **Esperado:** completed set built only from finished+wasFullyCompleted sessions for that routine; a (week,day) with zero present slots is absent from requiredPairs so it is auto-satisfied; routine null → derivePlanProgress({},[],1).
